{f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = {3a}{x}_{0}^{2} - 2\left( {a + 1}\right) {x}_{0} + 1 = {3a}{\left( \frac{1}{2a}\right) }^{2} - 2\left( {a + 1}\right) \left( \frac{1}{2a}\right)  + 1 =  - \frac{1}{4a},
\]

\[
f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = a{\left( \frac{1}{2a}\right) }^{3} - \left( {a + 1}\right) {\left( \frac{1}{2a}\right) }^{2} + \frac{1}{2a} = \frac{{2a} - 1}{8{a}^{2}},
\]

\( \left( x\right)  = {f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right) \left( {x - {x}_{0}}\right)  + f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  =  - \frac{1}{4a}\left( {x - \frac{1}{2a}}\right)  + \frac{{2a} - 1}{8{a}^{2}} \Rightarrow  t\left( x\right)  =  - \frac{1}{4a}\left( {x - 1}\right) \) ,

\( f\left( x\right)  = x\left( {x - 1}\right) \left( {{ax} - 1}\right)  \leq  t\left( x\right)  \Rightarrow  a{x}^{2} - x + \frac{1}{4a} \geq  0,\;{\left( x - \frac{1}{2a}\right) }^{2} \geq  0 \) 恒成立,

函数 \( t\left( x\right) \) 必是函数 \( y = f\left( x\right) \) 的 “控制函数“,

\( \forall g\left( x\right)  = {kx} + m \geq  f\left( x\right)  \Rightarrow  \forall \widehat{f}\left( x\right)  \geq  f\left( x\right) ,\widehat{f}\left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right) , x \in  \left( {0,1}\right) \) 是函数 \( y = f\left( x\right) \) 的“控制函数“,

此时 “控制函数 “ \( g\left( x\right) \) 必与 \( y = f\left( x\right) \) 相切于 \( x \) 点, \( t\left( x\right) \) 与 \( y = f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( x = \frac{1}{2a} \) 处相切,且过点 \( \left( {1,0}\right) \) ,

在 \( \left( {\frac{1}{2a},1}\right) \) 之间的点不可能使得 \( y = f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( \left( {\frac{1}{2a},1}\right) \) 切线下方,所以 \( \widehat{f}\left( c\right)  = f\left( c\right)  \Rightarrow \; c = \frac{1}{2a} = {x}_{0} \) 或 \( c = 1 \) ,

所以曲线 \( y = f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( x = {x}_{0}\left( {{x}_{0} \in  \left( {0,1}\right) }\right) \) 处的切线过点 \( \left( {1,0}\right) \) ,且 \( c \in  \left\lbrack  {{x}_{0},1}\right\rbrack \) ,

当且仅当 \( c = {x}_{0} \) 或 \( c = 1 \) 时, \( \widehat{f}\left( c\right)  = f\left( c\right) \) .

## 课改前

## 2011 秋考

## 填空

1. 函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{x - 2} \) 的反函数为 \( {f}^{-1}\left( x\right)  = \) ___.

【答案】 \( \frac{1}{x} + 2 \)

函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 的值域为 \( \{ y \mid  y \neq  0\} \) ,由 \( y = \frac{1}{x - 2} \) 得,

\( x = \frac{1}{y} + 2,\;\therefore {f}^{-1}\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{x} + 2\left( {x \neq  0}\right) . \)

2. 若全集 \( U = R \) ，集合 \( A = \{ x \mid  x \geq  1\}  \cup  \{ x \mid  x \leq  0\} \) ，则 \( {\complement }_{U}A = \) ___.

【答案】 \( \left( {0,1}\right) \)

\( \because A = \{ x \mid  x \geq  1\}  \cup  \{ x \mid  x \leq  0\} ,\;\therefore {\complement }_{U}A = \{ x \mid  0 < x < 1\} . \)

3. 设 \( m \) 是常数，若点 \( F\left( {0,5}\right) \) 是双曲线 \( \frac{{y}^{2}}{m} - \frac{{x}^{2}}{9} = 1 \) 的一个焦点，则 \( m = \) ___.

【答案】16

由于点 \( F\left( {0,5}\right) \) 是双曲线 \( \frac{{y}^{2}}{m} - \frac{{x}^{2}}{9} = 1 \) 的一个焦点，

故该双曲线的焦点在 \( y \) 轴上,从而 \( m > 0 \) .

从而得出 \( m + 9 = {25} \) ,解得 \( m = {16} \) .

4. 不等式 \( \frac{x + 1}{x} < 3 \) 的解为___.

【答案】 \( \left( {-\infty ,0}\right)  \cup  \left( {\frac{1}{2}, + \infty }\right) \)

\( \frac{x + 1}{x} < 3 \Leftrightarrow  \frac{{2x} - 1}{x} > 0 \Leftrightarrow  x\left( {{2x} - 1}\right)  > 0 \) ,解得 \( \left\{  {x \mid  x < 0}\right. \) 或 \( \left. {x > \frac{1}{2}}\right\} \) .

5. 在极坐标系中,直线 \( \rho \left( {2\cos \theta  + \sin \theta }\right)  = 2 \) 与直线 \( \rho \cos \theta  = 1 \) 的夹角大小为___. (结果用反三角函数值表示)

【答案】 \( \arccos \frac{2\sqrt{5}}{5} \)

将极坐标方程化为直角坐标系下方程,

两直线方程分别为 \( {2x} + y = 2 \) 和 \( x = 1 \) ,设两条直线的夹角是 \( \theta \) ,

则 \( \tan \theta  = \frac{1}{2},\theta  = \arctan \frac{1}{2},\therefore \cos \theta  = \frac{2\sqrt{5}}{5},\theta  = \arccos \frac{2\sqrt{5}}{5} \) .

6. 在相距 2 千米的 \( A \) 、 \( B \) 两点处测量目标点 \( C \) ,若 \( \angle {CAB} = {75}^{ \circ  } \) ， \( \angle {CBA} = {60}^{ \circ  } \) ，则 \( A \) 、 \( C \) 两点之间的距离为___千米。

【答案】 \( \sqrt{6} \)

如图所示, \( \angle C = {45}^{ \circ  } \) ,由正弦定理得 \( \frac{AC}{\sin {60}^{ \circ  }} = \fr![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_93_1185_559_264_294_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_93_1185_559_264_294_0.jpg)39b5b00_93_1185_559_264_294_0.jpg)

\( \therefore {AC} = \frac{2\sin {60}^{ \circ  }}{\sin {45}^{ \circ  }} = \sqrt{6} \) .

7. 若圆锥的侧面积为 \( {2\pi } \) ，底面面积为 \( \pi \) ，则该圆锥的体积为___.

【答案】 \( \frac{\sqrt{3}}{3}\pi \)

设圆锥的底面半径为 \( r \) ,高为 \( h \) ,母线长为 \( l \) ,

则 \( \left\{  {\begin{array}{l} {\pi rl} = {2\pi } \\  \pi {r}^{2} = \pi  \end{array},\therefore h = \sqrt{{l}^{2} - {r}^{2}} = \sqrt{3}}\right. \) ， \( \therefore V = \frac{1}{3}\pi {r}^{2}h = \frac{\sqrt{3}\pi }{3} \) .

8. 函数 \( y = \sin \left( {\frac{\pi }{2} + x}\right) \cos \left( {\frac{\pi }{6} - x}\right) \) 的最大值为___.

【答案】 \( \frac{2 + \sqrt{3}}{4} \)

\( y = \cos x\left( {\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\cos x + \frac{1}{2}\sin x}\right)  = \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}{\cos }^{2}x + \frac{1}{2}\sin x\cos x = \frac{\sqrt{3}\left( {1 + \cos {2x}}\right) }{4} + \)

\[
\frac{1}{4}\sin {2x} = \frac{1}{2}\sin \left( {{2x} + \frac{\pi }{3}}\right)  + \frac{\sqrt{3}}{4}
\]

当 \( \sin \left( {{2x} + \frac{\pi }{3}}\right)  = 1 \) 时， \( {y}_{\max } = \frac{1}{2} + \frac{\sqrt{3}}{4} \) .

9. 马老师从课本上抄录一个随机变量 \( \xi \) 的概率分布列如下表:

<table><tr><td>\( x \)</td><td>1</td><td>2</td><td>3</td></tr><tr><td>\( P\left( {\xi  = x}\right) \)</td><td>?</td><td>!</td><td>?</td></tr></table>

请小牛同学计算 \( \xi \) 的数学期望. 尽管 “ ! ” 处完全无法看清，且两个 “ ? ” 处字迹模糊，但能肯定这两个 “? ” 处的数值相同. 据此,小牛给出了正确答案 \( {E\xi } = \) ___.

## 【答案】 2

设 “?” 处的数据为 \( x \) ,则 “!” 处的数据为 \( 1 - {2x} \) ,则

\( {E\xi } = 1 \times  x + 2\left( {1 - {2x}}\right)  + {3x} = 2. \)

10. 行列式 \( \left| \begin{array}{ll} a & b \\  c & d \end{array}\right| \left( {a, b, c, d \in  \{  - 1,1,2\} }\right) \) 所有可能的值中,最大的是___.

【答案】 6

\( \left| \begin{array}{ll} a & b \\  c & d \end{array}\right|  = {ad} - {bc},\;\because a,\;b,\;c,\;d \in  \{  - 1,1,2\} , \)

要使 \( {ad} - {bc} \) 最大,须 \( {ad} \) 取最大值 4,

\( {bc} \) 取最小值-2,

\( \therefore \left| \begin{array}{ll} a & b \\  c & d \end{array}\right| \) 最大值为 6 .

11. 在正三角形 \( {ABC} \) 中， \( D \) 是 \( {BC} \) 上的点. 若 \( {AB} = 3,{BD} = 1 \) ，则 \( \overrightarrow{AB} \cdot  \overrightarrow{AD} = \) ___.

【答案】 \( \frac{15}{2} \)![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_95_995_294_325_303_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_95_995_294_325_303_0.jpg)739b5b00_95_995_294_325_303_0.jpg)

\( A{D}^{2} = {3}^{2} + {1}^{2} - 2 \times  3 \times  1 \times  \cos {60}^{ \circ  } = 7,\therefore {AD} = \sqrt{7} \) ,

\( \cos \angle {BAD} = \frac{{3}^{2} + {\left( \sqrt{7}\right) }^{2} - 1}{2 \times  3 \times  \sqrt{7}} = \frac{5\sqrt{7}}{14} \) ，

\( \therefore \overrightarrow{AB} \cdot  \overrightarrow{AD} = \left| \overrightarrow{AB}\right|  \cdot  \left| \overrightarrow{AD}\right|  \cdot  \cos \angle {BAD} = 3 \times  \sqrt{7} \times  \frac{5\sqrt{7}}{14} = \frac{15}{2} \) .

法二: \( \because \overrightarrow{AD} = \overrightarrow{AB} + \overrightarrow{BD} \) ,

\( \therefore \overrightarrow{AB} \cdot  \overrightarrow{AD} = \overrightarrow{AB} \cdot  \left( {\overrightarrow{AB} + \overrightarrow{BD}}\right)  = {\overrightarrow{AB}}^{2} + \overrightarrow{AB} \cdot  \overrightarrow{BD} = {\left| \overrightarrow{AB}\right| }^{2} + \left| \overrightarrow{AB}\right|  \cdot  \left| \overrightarrow{BD}\right|  \cdot  \cos {120}^{ \circ  } \; = {3}^{2} + 3 \times  1 \times  \left( {-\frac{1}{2}}\right)  = \frac{15}{2} \) .

12. 随机抽取的 9 位同学中, 至少有 2 位同学在同一月份出生的概率为___ (默认每个月的天数相同, 结果精确到 0.001 ).

【答案】0.985

随机抽取的 9 位同学中, 均不在同一月份出生的概率为

\( P = \frac{{A}_{12}^{9}}{{12}^{9}} \approx  {0.01547} \) ,则这少有 2 位同学在同一月份出生的概率为

\( 1 - {0.01547} = {0.98453} \approx  {0.985}. \)

13. 已知点 \( O\left( {0,0}\right) \text{ 、 }{Q}_{0}\left( {0,1}\right) \) 和点 \( {R}_{0}\left( {3,1}\right) \) ,记 \( {Q}_{0}{R}_{0} \) 的中点为 \( {P}_{1} \) ,取 \( {Q}_{0}{P}_{1} \) 和 \( {P}_{1}{R}_{0} \) 中的一条, 记其端点为 \( {Q}_{1}\text{ 、 }{R}_{1} \) 使之满足 \( \left( {\left| {O{Q}_{1}}\right|  - 2}\right) \left( {\left| {O{R}_{1}}\right|  - 2}\right)  < 0 \) ,记 \( {Q}_{1}{R}_{1} \) 的中点为 \( {P}_{2} \) ,取 \( {Q}_{1}{P}_{2} \) 和 \( {P}_{2}{R}_{1} \) 中的一条,记其端点为 \( {Q}_{2}\text{ 、 }{R}_{2} \) ,使之满足 \( \left( {\left| {O{Q}_{2}}\right|  - 2}\right) \left( {\left| {O{R}_{2}}\right|  - 2}\right)  < 0 \) . 依次下去,得到 \( {P}_{1},{P}_{2},\cdots ,{P}_{n},\cdots \) ，则 \( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n\infty }}\left| {{Q}_{0}{P}_{n}}\right|  = \) ___.

【答案】 \( \sqrt{3} \)

条件 \( \left( {\left| {O{Q}_{n}}\right|  - 2}\right) \left( {\left| {O{R}_{n}}\right|  - 2}\right)  < 0 \) 的意思是

\( {Q}_{0}{R}_{0} \) 上到原点距离为 2 的点 (设为 \( P \) ) 始终在 \( {Q}_{n}{R}_{n} \) 之间,

且 \( {Q}_{n}{R}_{n} \) 的长度不断缩小,直到为 0,而 \( {P}_{n} \) 是 \( {Q}_{n - 1}{R}_{n - 1} \) 的中点,

也始终在 \( {Q}_{n - 1}{R}_{n - 1} \) 之间,故当取极限时 \( P \) 与 \( {P}_{n} \) 两点就重合,

\( P \) 就是以原点为圆心,以 2 为半径的圆与 \( y = 1 \) 的交点,此时,

\( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n\infty }}\left| {{Q}_{0}{P}_{n}}\right|  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n\infty }}\sqrt{O{P}_{n}^{2} - O{Q}_{0}^{2}} = \sqrt{O{P}^{2} - O{Q}_{0}^{2}} = \sqrt{O{P}^{2} - O{Q}^{2}} = \sqrt{3} \)

选择

14. 设 \( g\left( x\right) \) 是定义在 \( R \) 上,以 1 为周期的函数,若函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = x + g\left( x\right) \) 在区间 \( \left\lbrack  {3,4}\right\rbrack \) 上的值域为 \( \left\lbrack  {-2,5}\right\rbrack \) ，则 \( f\left( x\right) \) 在区间 \( \left\lbrack  {-{10},{10}}\right\rbrack \) 上的值域为___.

【答案】 \( \left\lbrack  {-{15},{11}}\right\rbrack \)

本小题考查函数的性质.

令 \( f\left( x\right) \) 分别在 \( {x}_{1},{x}_{2}\left( {{x}_{1},{x}_{2} \in  \left\lbrack  {3,4}\right\rbrack  }\right) \) 处取得最大值和最小值,

即 \( f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  = {x}_{1} + g\left( {x}_{1}\right)  = 5, f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  = {x}_{2} + g\left( {x}_{2}\right)  =  - 2 \) ,

因为 \( y = x \) 是增函数, \( y = g\left( x\right) \) 周期为 1,

则 \( f\left( {{x}_{1} + 6}\right) \) 是 \( f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( \left\lbrack  {9,{10}}\right\rbrack \) 上的最大值,

\( f\left( {{x}_{2} - {13}}\right) \) 是 \( f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( \left\lbrack  {-{10}, - 9}\right\rbrack \) 上的最小值,

\( f\left( {{x}_{1} + 6}\right)  = {x}_{1} + 6 + g\left( {{x}_{1} + 6}\right)  = {x}_{1} + g\left( {x}_{1}\right)  + 6 = {11}, \)

\( f\left( {{x}_{2} - {13}}\right)  = {x}_{2} - {13} + g\left( {{x}_{2} - {13}}\right)  = {x}_{2} + g\left( {x}_{2}\right)  - {13} =  - {15}, \)

故值域为: \( \left\lbrack  {-{15},{11}}\right\rbrack \) .

15. 若 \( a, b \in  R \) ,且 \( {ab} > 0 \) ,则下列不等式中,恒成立的是 ( ).

A. \( {a}^{2} + {b}^{2} > {2ab} \) B. \( a + b \geq  2\sqrt{ab} \) C. \( \frac{1}{a} + \frac{1}{b} > \frac{2}{\sqrt{ab}} \) D. \( \frac{b}{a} + \frac{a}{b} \geq  2 \)

【答案】 \( D \)

\( \because {a}^{2} + {b}^{2} - {2ab} = {\left( a - b\right) }^{2} \geq  0, A \) 错误,

对 \( B\text{ 、 }C \) ,当 \( a < 0, b < 0 \) 时,明显错误,

对 \( D,\because {ab} > 0,\therefore \frac{b}{a} > 0,\frac{a}{b} > 0,\therefore \frac{b}{a} + \frac{a}{b} \geq  2\sqrt{\frac{b}{a} \times  \frac{a}{b}} = 2 \) ,

当且仅当 \( \frac{b}{a} = \frac{a}{b} \) 即 \( a = b \) 时,取等号,故选 \( D \) .

16. 下列函数中,既是偶函数,又是在区间 \( \left( {0, + \infty }\right) \) 上单调递减的函数是 ( ).

A. \( y = \ln \frac{1}{\left| x\right| } \) B. \( y = {x}^{3} \) C. \( y = {2}^{\left| x\right| } \) D. \( y = \cos x \)

【答案】 \( A \)

对于 \( y = \ln \frac{1}{\left| x\right| } \) ,

函数的定义域为 \( \left( {-\infty ,0}\right)  \cup  \left( {0, + \infty }\right) \) ,

将 \( x \) 用 \( - x \) 代替函数的解析式不变，

所以是偶函数

当 \( x \in  \left( {0, + \infty }\right) \) 时, \( y = \ln \frac{1}{\left| x\right| } = \ln \frac{1}{x} \) ,

\( \because {y}^{\prime } =  - \frac{1}{x} < 0 \) ,

\( \therefore y = \ln \frac{1}{\left| x\right| } \) 在区间 \( \left( {0, + \infty }\right) \) 上单调递减的函数.

17. 设 \( {A}_{1},{A}_{2},{A}_{3},{A}_{4},{A}_{5} \) 是空间中给定的 5 个不同点,则使 \( \overrightarrow{M{A}_{1}} + \overrightarrow{M{A}_{2}} + \overrightarrow{M{A}_{3}} + \overrightarrow{M{A}_{4}} + \; \overrightarrow{M{A}_{5}} = \overrightarrow{0} \) 成立的点 \( M \) 的个数为 ( ).

A. 0 B. 1 C. 5 D. 10

## 【答案】 \( B \)

从特例入手,不妨设, \( {A}_{1},{A}_{2},{A}_{3},{A}_{4},{A}_{5} \) 共线,

且 \( \overrightarrow{{A}_{1}{A}_{2}} = \overrightarrow{{A}_{2}{A}_{3}} = \overrightarrow{{A}_{3}{A}_{4}} = \overrightarrow{{A}_{4}{A}_{5}} \) ,取 \( {A}_{3} \) 为 \( M \) ,

则 \( \overrightarrow{M{A}_{1}} + \overrightarrow{M{A}_{2}} + \overrightarrow{M{A}_{3}} + \overrightarrow{M{A}_{4}} + \overrightarrow{M{A}_{5}} = \overrightarrow{{A}_{3}{A}_{1}} + \overrightarrow{{A}_{3}{A}_{2}} + \overrightarrow{0} + \overrightarrow{{A}_{3}{A}_{4}} + \overrightarrow{{A}_{3}{A}_{5}} = \overrightarrow{0} \) ,

故存在满足条件的点,下面证明满足题意点 \( M \) 只有一个,用反证法:

假设满足题意的除 \( M \) 点外还有 \( N \) ,则

\( \overrightarrow{M{A}_{1}} + \overrightarrow{M{A}_{2}} + \overrightarrow{M{A}_{3}} + \overrightarrow{M{A}_{4}} + \overrightarrow{M{A}_{5}} = \overrightarrow{0} \) ①

\( \overrightarrow{N{A}_{1}} + \overrightarrow{N{A}_{2}} + \overrightarrow{N{A}_{3}} + \overrightarrow{N{A}_{4}} + \overrightarrow{N{A}_{5}} = \overrightarrow{0} \) ②

①-②得， \( 5\overrightarrow{NM} = \overrightarrow{0} \) ， \( \therefore \overrightarrow{NM} = \overrightarrow{0} \) ， \( \therefore M \) 与 \( N \) 重合，

\( \therefore \) 满足条件的点 \( M \) 有且只有一个,故选 \( B \) .

18. 设 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 是各项为正数的无穷数列, \( {A}_{i} \) 是边长为 \( {a}_{i},{a}_{i + 1} \) 的矩形的面积 \( \left( {\mathrm{i} = 1,2,\cdots }\right) \) ,则 \( \left\{  {A}_{n}\right\} \) 为等比数列的充要条件是 ( )

A. \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 是等比数列

B. \( {a}_{1},{a}_{3},\cdots ,{a}_{{2n} - 1},\cdots \) 或 \( {a}_{2},{a}_{4},\cdots ,{a}_{2n},\cdots \) 是等比数列

C. \( {a}_{1},{a}_{3},\cdots ,{a}_{{2n} - 1},\cdots \) 和 \( {a}_{2},{a}_{4},\cdots ,{a}_{2n},\cdots \) 均是等比数列

D. \( {a}_{1},{a}_{3},\cdots ,{a}_{{2n} - 1},\cdots \) 和 \( {a}_{2},{a}_{4},\cdots ,{a}_{2n},\cdots \) 均是等比数列,且公比相同

## 【答案】 \( D \)

由题意知 \( {A}_{i} = {a}_{i} \cdot  {a}_{i + 1} \) ,

若 \( \left\{  {A}_{n}\right\} \) 是等比数列,则 \( \frac{{A}_{n + 1}}{{A}_{n}} = \frac{{a}_{n + 1} \cdot  {a}_{n + 2}}{{a}_{n} \cdot  {a}_{n + 1}} = \frac{{a}_{n + 2}}{{a}_{n}} \) 为非 0 常数,

即 \( \frac{{A}_{2}}{{A}_{1}} = \frac{{a}_{3}}{{a}_{1}},\frac{{A}_{3}}{{A}_{2}} = \frac{{a}_{4}}{{a}_{2}},\cdots \cdots \) ,

\( \therefore {a}_{1},{a}_{3},{a}_{5},\cdots \) 和 \( {a}_{2},{a}_{4},{a}_{6},\cdots \) 成等比数列,且公比相等;

反之, 若奇数项和偶数项分别成等比数列, 且公比相等,

设为 \( q \) ,则 \( \frac{{A}_{n + 1}}{{A}_{n}} = \frac{{a}_{n + 2}}{{a}_{n}} = q \) ,则 \( \left\{  {A}_{n}\right\} \) 是等比数列.

故选 \( D \)

【解析】答

19. 已知复数 \( {z}_{1} \) 满足 \( \left( {{z}_{1} - 2}\right) \left( {1 + \mathrm{i}}\right)  = 1 - \mathrm{i} \) ( \( \mathrm{i} \) 为虚数单位),复数 \( {z}_{2} \) 的虚部为 2,且 \( {z}_{1} \cdot  {z}_{2} \) 是实数, 求 \( {z}_{2} \) .

【答案】 \( 4 + 2\mathrm{i} \)

\( \left( {{z}_{1} - 2}\right) \left( {1 + \mathrm{i}}\right)  = 1 - \mathrm{i} \Rightarrow  {z}_{1} = 2 - \mathrm{i}, \)

设 \( {z}_{2} = a + 2\mathrm{i},\;a \in  R \) ,

则 \( {z}_{1}{z}_{2} = \left( {2 - \mathrm{i}}\right) \left( {a + 2\mathrm{i}}\right)  = \left( {{2a} + 2}\right)  + \left( {4 - a}\right) \mathrm{i} \) ,

\( \because {z}_{1}{z}_{2} \in  R \) ,

\( \therefore a = 4 \) ,

\( \therefore {z}_{2} = 4 + 2\mathrm{i} \) .

20. 已知函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = a \cdot  {2}^{x} + b \cdot  {3}^{x} \) ,其中常数 \( a, b \) 满足 \( a \cdot  b \neq  0 \)

(1)若 \( a \cdot  b > 0 \) ，判断函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 的单调性；

【答案】函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( R \) 上是减函数.

当 \( a > 0, b > 0 \) 时,任意 \( {x}_{1},{x}_{2} \in  R,{x}_{1} < {x}_{2} \) ,

则 \( f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  = a\left( {{2}^{{x}_{1}} - {2}^{{x}_{2}}}\right)  + b\left( {{3}^{{x}_{1}} - {3}^{{x}_{2}}}\right) \)

\( \because {2}^{{x}_{1}} < {2}^{{x}_{2}}, a > 0 \Rightarrow  a\left( {{2}^{{x}_{1}} - {2}^{{x}_{2}}}\right)  < 0,{3}^{{x}_{1}} < {3}^{{x}_{2}}, b > 0 \Rightarrow  b\left( {{3}^{{x}_{1}} - {3}^{{x}_{2}}}\right)  < 0 \) ,

\( \therefore f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  < 0 \) ,函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( R \) 是增函数.

当 \( a < 0 \) ， \( b < 0 \) 时，同理，函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( R \) 上是减函数.

(2)若 \( a \cdot  b < 0 \) ，求 \( f\left( {x + 1}\right)  > f\left( x\right) \) 时的 \( x \) 的取值范围.

【答案】当 \( a < 0, b > 0 \) 时， \( x > {\log }_{1.5}\left( {-\frac{a}{2b}}\right) \) ；当 \( a > 0, b < 0 \) 时， \( x < {\log }_{1.5}\left( {-\frac{a}{2b}}\right) \) .

\( f\left( {x + 1}\right)  - f\left( x\right)  = a \cdot  {2}^{x} + {2b} \cdot  {3}^{x} > 0 \)

当 \( a < 0, b > 0 \) 时, \( {\left( \frac{3}{2}\right) }^{x} >  - \frac{a}{2b} \) ,则 \( x > {\log }_{1.5}\left( {-\frac{a}{2b}}\right) \) ;

当 \( a > 0 \) ， \( b < 0 \) 时， \( {\left( \frac{3}{2}\right) }^{x} <  - \frac{a}{2b} \) ，则 \( x < {\log }_{1.5}\left( {-\frac{a}{2b}}\right) \) .

21. 已知 \( {ABCD} - {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 是底面边长为 1 的正四棱柱， \( {O}_{1} \) 为 \( {A}_{1}{C}_{1![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_99_259_1751_343_337_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_99_259_1751_343_337_0.jpg)39b5b00_99_259_1751_343_337_0.jpg)

(1)设 \( A{B}_{1} \) 与底面 \( {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 所成角的大小为 \( \alpha \) ，二面角 \( A - {B}_{1}{D}_{1} - {A}_{1} \) 的大小为 \( \beta \) . 求证: \( \tan \beta  =![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_100_419_367_297_316_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_100_419_367_297_316_0.jpg)39b5b00_100_419_367_297_316_0.jpg)

设正四棱柱的高为 \( h \) ,

连 \( A{O}_{1}, A{A}_{1} \bot \) 底面 \( {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 于 \( {A}_{1} \) ,

\( \therefore A{B}_{1} \) 与底面 \( {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 所成的角为 \( \angle A{B}_{1}{A}_{1} \) ,即 \( \angle A{B}_{1}{A}_{1} = \alpha \)

\( \because A{B}_{1} = A{D}_{1},{O}_{1} \) 为 \( {B}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 中点, \( \therefore A{O}_{1} \bot  {B}_{1}{D}_{1} \) ,又 \( {A}_{1}{O}_{1} \bot  {B}_{1}{D}_{1} \) ,

\( \therefore \angle A{O}_{1}{A}_{1} \) 是二面角 \( A - {B}_{1}{D}_{1} - {A}_{1} \) 的平面角,即 \( \angle A{O}_{1}{A}_{1} = \beta \)

\( \therefore \tan \alpha  = \frac{A{A}_{1}}{{A}_{1}{B}_{1}} = h,\tan \beta  = \frac{A{A}_{1}}{{A}_{1}{O}_{1}} = \sqrt{2}h = \sqrt{2}\tan \alpha \) .

( 2 )若点 \( C \) 到平面 \( A{B}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 的距离为 \( \frac{4}{3} \) ，求正四棱柱 \( {ABCD} - {A}_{1}{B}_![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_100_416_1191_340_387_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_100_416_1191_340_387_0.jpg)9b5b00_100_416_1191_340_387_0.jpg)

建立如图空间直角坐标系,有 \( A\left( {0,0, h}\right) ,{B}_{1}\left( {1,0,0}\right) ,{D}_{1}\left( {0,1,0}\right) , C\left( {1,1, h}\right) \)

\( \overrightarrow{A{B}_{1}} = \left( {1,0, - h}\right) ,\;\overrightarrow{A{D}_{1}} = \left( {0,1, - h}\right) ,\;\overrightarrow{AC} = \left( {1,1,0}\right) \)

设平面 \( A{B}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 的一个法向量为 \( \overrightarrow{n} = \left( {x, y, z}\right) \) ,

\( \because \left\{  {\begin{array}{l} \overrightarrow{n} \bot  \overrightarrow{A{B}_{1}} \\  \overrightarrow{n} \bot  \overrightarrow{A{D}_{1}} \end{array} \Leftrightarrow  \left\{  {\begin{array}{l} \overrightarrow{n} \cdot  \overrightarrow{A{B}_{1}} = 0 \\  \overrightarrow{n} \cdot  \overrightarrow{A{D}_{1}} = 0 \end{array},\text{ 取 }z = 1\text{ 得 }\overrightarrow{n} = \left( {h, h,1}\right) }\right. }\right. \)

\( \therefore \) 点 \( C \) 到平面 \( A{B}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 的距离为 \( d = \frac{\left| \overrightarrow{n} \cdot  \overrightarrow{AC}\right| }{\left| \overrightarrow{n}\right| } = \frac{h + h + 0}{\sqrt{{h}^{2} + {h}^{2} + 1}} = \frac{4}{3} \) ,

则 \( h = 2 \) .

22. 已知数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 和 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 的通项公式分别为 \( {a}_{n} = {3n} + 6,{b}_{n} = {2n} + 7\left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) . 将集合 \( \left\{  {x \mid  x = {a}_{n}, n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right\}   \cup  \left\{  {x \mid  x = {b}_{n}, n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right\} \) 中的元素从小到大依次排列,构成数列 \( {c}_{1},{c}_{2},{c}_{3} \) , \( \cdots ,\;{c}_{n},\;\cdots . \)

(1)写出 \( {c}_{1},\;{c}_{2},\;{c}_{3},\;{c}_{4} \) ；

【答案】 \( 9;{11};{12};{13} \)

\[
{c}_{1} = 9,\;{c}_{2} = {11},\;{c}_{3} = {12},\;{c}_{4} = {13}.
\]

( 2 )求证:在数列 \( \left\{  {c}_{n}\right\} \) 中，但不在数列 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 中的项恰为 \( {a}_{2},{a}_{4},\cdots ,{a}_{2n},\cdots \) ；

【答案】见解析

① 任意 \( n \in  {N}^{ * } \) ,设 \( {a}_{{2n} - 1} = 3\left( {{2n} - 1}\right)  + 6 = {6n} + 3 = {b}_{k} = {2k} + 7 \) ,

则 \( k = {3n} - 2 \) ,即 \( {a}_{{2n} - 1} = {b}_{{3n} - 2} \) ;

② 假设 \( {a}_{2n} = {6n} + 6 = {b}_{k} = {2k} + 7 \Leftrightarrow  k = {3n} - \frac{1}{2} \in  {N}^{ * } \) (矛盾), \( \therefore {a}_{2n} \notin  \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \)

\( \therefore \) 在数列 \( \left\{  {c}_{n}\right\} \) 中,但不在数列 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 中的项恰为 \( {a}_{2},{a}_{4},\cdots ,{a}_{2n},\cdots \) .

(3)求数列 \( \left\{  {c}_{n}\right\} \) 的通项公式.

【答案】 \( {c}_{n} = \left\{  {\begin{array}{ll} {6k} + 3 & \left( {n = {4k} - 3}\right) \\  {6k} + 5 & \left( {n = {4k} - 2}\right) \\  {6k} + 6 & \left( {n = {4k} - 1}\right) \\  {6k} + 7 & \left( {n = {4k}}\right)  \end{array}, k \in  {N}^{ * }}\right. \)

\( {b}_{{3k} - 2} = 2\left( {{3k} - 2}\right)  + 7 = {6k} + 3 = {a}_{{2k} - 1}, \)

\( {b}_{{3k} - 1} = {6k} + 5,\;{a}_{2k} = {6k} + 6,\;{b}_{3k} = {6k} + 7, \)

\( \because {6k} + 3 < {6k} + 5 < {6k} + 6 < {6k} + 7 \) ,

\( \therefore \) 当 \( k = 1 \) 时,依次有 \( {b}_{1} = {a}_{1} = {c}_{1},{b}_{2} = {c}_{2},{a}_{2} = {c}_{3},{b}_{3} = {c}_{4},\cdots \)

\[
\therefore {c}_{n} = \left\{  {\begin{array}{ll} {6k} + 3 & \left( {n = {4k} - 3}\right) \\  {6k} + 5 & \left( {n = {4k} - 2}\right) \\  {6k} + 6 & \left( {n = {4k} - 1}\right) \\  {6k} + 7 & \left( {n = {4k}}\right)  \end{array},\;k \in  {N}^{ * }}\right.
\]

的距离,记作 \( d\left( {P, l}\right) \)

(1) 求点 \( P\left( {1,1}\right) \) 到线段 \( l : x - y - 3 = 0\left( {3 \leq  x \leq  5}\right) \) 的距离 \( d\left( {P, l}\right) \) ;

【答案】 \( d\left( {P, l}\right)  = {\left| PQ\right| }_{\min } = \sqrt{5} \) .

设 \( Q\left( {x, x - 3}\right) \) 是线段 \( l : x - y - 3 = 0\left( {3 \leq  x \leq  5}\right) \) 上一点,则

\( \left| {PQ}\right|  = \sqrt{{\left( x - 1\right) }^{2} + {\left( x - 4\right) }^{2}} = \sqrt{2{\left( x - \frac{5}{2}\right) }^{2} + \frac{9}{2}}\left( {3 \leq  x \leq  5}\right) , \)

当 \( x = 3 \) 时, \( d\left( {P, l}\right)  = {\left| PQ\right| }_{\min } = \sqrt{5} \) .

( 2 )设 \( l \) 是长为 2 的线段，求点的集合 \( D = \{ P \mid  d\left( {P, l}\right)  \leq  1\} \) 所表示的图形面积；

【答案】 \( S = 4 + \pi \) .

设线段 \( l \) 的端点分别为 \( A, B \) ,以直线 \( {AB} \) 为 \( x ![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_102_902_735_387_266_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_102_902_735_387_266_0.jpg)39b5b00_102_902_735_387_266_0.jpg)

则 \( A\left( {-1,0}\right) , B\left( {1,0}\right) \) ,点集 \( D \) 由如下曲线围成

\( {l}_{1} : \;y = 1\left( {\left| x\right|  \leq  1}\right) ,\;{l}_{2} : \;y =  - 1\left( {\left| x\right|  \leq  1}\right) , \)

\( {C}_{1} : \;{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2} + {y}^{2} = 1\left( {x \leq   - 1}\right) ,\;{C}_{2} : \;{\left( x - 1\right) }^{2} + {y}^{2} = 1\left( {x \geq  1}\right) \)

其面积为 \( S = 4 + \pi \) .

(3)写出到两条线段 \( {l}_{1} \) ， \( {l}_{2} \) 距离相等的点的集合 \( \Omega  = \left\{  {P \mid  d\left( {P,{l}_{1}}\right)  = d\left( {P,{l}_{2}}\right) }\right\} \) ，其中 \( {l}_{1} = {AB} \) ， \( {l}_{2} = \; {CD}, A, B, C, D \) 是下列三组点中的一组.

【答案】① \( A\left( {1,3}\right) , B\left( {1,0}\right) , C\left( {-1,3}\right) , D\left( {-1,0}\right) \) .

② \( A\left( {1,3}\right) \) ， \( B\left( {1,0}\right) \) ， \( C\left( {-1,3}\right) \) ， \( D\left( {-1, - 2}\right) \) .

③ \( A\left( {0,1}\right) , B\left( {0,0}\right) , C\left( {0,0}\right) , D\left( {2,0}\right) \) .

①选择 \( A\left( {1,3}\right) , B\left( {1,0}\right) , C\left( {-1,3}\right) , D\left( {-1,0}\right) ,\Omega  = \{ \left( {x, y}\right)  \mid  x = 0\} \) .

②选择 \( A\left( {1,3}\right) \) ， \( B\left( {1,0}\right) \) ， \( C\left( {-1,3}\right) \) ， \( D\left( {-1, - 2}\right) \)

\( \Omega  = \{ \left( {x, y}\right)  \mid  x = 0, y \geq  0\}  \cup  \left\{  {\left( {x, y}\right)  \mid  {y}^{2} = {4x}, - 2 \leq  y < 0}\right\}   \cup  \{ \left( {x, y}\right)  \mid  x + y + 1 = 0, x \leqq  1\} . \)

③选择 \( A\left( {0,1}\right) \) ， \( B\left( {0,0}\right) \) ， \( C\left( {0,0}\right) \) ， \( D\left( {2,0}\right) \)

\( \Omega  = \{ \left( {x, y}\right)  \mid  x \leq  0, y \leq  0\}  \cup  \{ \left( {x, y}\right)  \mid  y = x,0 < x \leq  1\} \)

\( \cup  \left\{  {\left( {x, y}\right)  \mid  {x}^{2} = {2y} - 1,1 < x \leq  2}\right\}   \cup  \{ \left( {x, y}\right)  \mid  {4x} - {2y} - 3 = 0,{x2}\} \)

①选择 \( A\left( {1,3}\right) , B\left( {1,0}\right) , C\left( {-1,3}\right) , D\left( {-1,0}\right) ,\Omega  = \{ \left( {x, y}\right)  \mid  x = 0\} \) .

②选择 \( A\left( {1,3}\right) , B\left( {1,0}\right) , C\left( {-1,3}\right) , D\left( {-1, - 2}\right) \)

\( \Omega  = \{ \left( {x, y}\right)  \mid  x = 0, y \geq  0\}  \cup  \{ \left( {x, y}\right)  \mid  {y}^{2} = {4x}, - 2 \leq  y < 0\}  \cup  \{ \left( {x, y}\right)  \mid  x + y + 1 = 0, x \leqq  1\} . \)

③选择 \( A\left( {0,1}\right) \) ， \( B\left( {0,0}\right) \) ， \( C\left( {0,0}\right) \) ， \( D\left( {2,0}\right) \)

\( \Omega  = \{ \left( {x, y}\right)  \mid  x \leq  0, y \leq  0\}  \cup  \{ \left( {x, y}\right)  \mid  y = x,0 < x \leq  1\} \)

\( \cup  \left\{  {\left( {x, y}\right)  \mid  {x}^{![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_103_425_218_268_517_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_103_425_218_268_517_0.jpg)39![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_103_779_218_344_530_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_103_779_218_344_530_0.jpg)39![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_103_1194_212_336_493_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_103_1194_212_336_493_0.jpg)9b5b00_103_1194_212_336_493_0.jpg)

## 2012 秋考

## 选择

1. 若 \( 1 + \sqrt{2}\mathrm{i} \) 是关于 \( x \) 的实系数方程 \( {x}^{2} + {bx} + c = 0 \) 的一个复数根,则 ().

A. \( b = 2, c = 3 \) B. \( b =  - 2, c = 3 \) C. \( b =  - 2, c =  - 1 \) D. \( b = 2, c =  - 1 \)

## 【答案】 \( B \)

因为 \( 1 + \sqrt{2}\mathrm{i} \) 是实系数方程的一个复数根,

所以 \( 1 - \sqrt{2}\mathrm{i} \) 也是方程的根,

则 \( 1 + \sqrt{2}\mathrm{i} + 1 - \sqrt{2}\mathrm{i} = 2 =  - b,\;\left( {1 + \sqrt{2}\mathrm{i}}\right) \left( {1 - \sqrt{2}\mathrm{i}}\right)  = 3 = c \) ,

所以解得 \( b =  - 2, c = 3 \) .

2. 在 \( {ABC} \) 中,若 \( {\sin }^{2}A + {\sin }^{2}B < {\sin }^{2}C \) ,则 \( {ABC} \) 的形状是 ().

A. 锐角三角形 B. 直角三角形 C. 钝角三角形 D. 不能确定

【答案】 \( C \)

由 \( {\sin }^{2}A + {\sin }^{2}B < {\sin }^{2}C \) ,根据正弦定理可知 \( {a}^{2} + {b}^{2} < {c}^{2} \) ,

在三角形中 \( \cos C = \frac{{a}^{2} + {b}^{2} - {c}^{2}}{2ab} < 0 \) ,

所以 \( C \) 为钝角，三角形为钝角三角形.

3. 设 \( {10} \leq  {x}_{1} < {x}_{2} < {x}_{3} < {x}_{4} \leq  {10}^{4},{x}_{5} = {10}^{5} \) . 随机变量 \( {\xi }_{1} \) 取值 \( {x}_{1}\text{ 、 }{x}_{2}\text{ 、 }{x}_{3}\text{ 、 }{x}_{4}\text{ 、 }{x}_{5} \) 的概率均为 0.2,随机变量 \( {\xi }_{2} \) 取值 \( \frac{{x}_{1} + {x}_{2}}{2}\text{ 、 }\frac{{x}_{2} + {x}_{3}}{2}\text{ 、 }\frac{{x}_{3} + {x}_{4}}{2}\text{ 、 }\frac{{x}_{4} + {x}_{5}}{2}\text{ 、 }\frac{{x}_{5} + {x}_{1}}{2} \) 的概率也为 0.2 . 若记 \( D{\widehat{\xi }}_{1}\text{ 、 }D{\widehat{\xi }}_{2} \) 分别为 \( {\widehat{\xi }}_{1}\text{ 、 }{\widehat{\xi }}_{2} \) 的方差,则(   )

A. \( D{\overline{\xi }}_{1} > D{\overline{\xi }}_{2} \) B. \( D{\overline{\xi }}_{1} = D{\overline{\xi }}_{2} \)

C. \( D{\overline{\xi }}_{1} < D{\overline{\xi }}_{2} \) D. \( D{\overline{\xi }}_{1} \) 与 \( D{\overline{\xi }}_{2} \) 的大小关系与 \( {x}_{1}\text{ 、 }{x}_{2}\text{ 、 }{x}_{3}\text{ 、 }{x}_{4} \) 的取值有关

## 【答案】 \( A \)

考查样本估计总体的平均数和方差, 主要是对方差概念的理解, 利用基本不等式求解.

由随机变量 \( {\widehat{\xi }}_{1},{\widehat{\xi }}_{2} \) 的取值情况,它们的平均数分别为:

\( \overline{{x}_{1}} = \frac{1}{5}\left( {{x}_{1} + {x}_{2} + {x}_{3} + {x}_{4} + {x}_{5}}\right) , \)

\( \overline{{x}_{2}} = \frac{1}{5}\left( {\frac{{x}_{1} + {x}_{2}}{2} + \frac{{x}_{2} + {x}_{3}}{2} + \frac{{x}_{3} + {x}_{4}}{2} + \frac{{x}_{4} + {x}_{5}}{2} + \frac{{x}_{5} + {x}_{1}}{2}}\right)  = \overline{{x}_{1}}, \)

且随机变量 \( {\widehat{\xi }}_{1},{\widehat{\xi }}_{2} \) 的概率都为 0.2,所以有 \( D{\widehat{\xi }}_{1} > D{\widehat{\xi }}_{2} \) .

4. 设 \( {a}_{n} = \frac{1}{n}\sin \frac{n\pi }{25},{S}_{n} = {a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + \cdots  + {a}_{n} \) . 在 \( {S}_{1},{S}_{2},\cdots ,{S}_{100} \) 中,正数的个数是 ( ).

A. 25 B. 50 C. 75 D. 100

## 【答案】 \( D \)

对于 \( 1 \leq  k \leq  {25},{a}_{k} \geq  0 \) (唯 \( {a}_{25} = 0 \) ),所以 \( {S}_{k}\left( {1 \leq  k \leq  {25}}\right) \) 都为正数.

当 \( {26} \leq  k \leq  {49} \) 时,令 \( \frac{\pi }{25} = \alpha \) ,则 \( \frac{k\pi }{25} = {k\alpha ![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_104_414_1785_303_275_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_104_414_1785_303_275_0.jpg)9b5b00_104_414_1785_303_275_0.jpg)

其终边两两关于 \( x \) 轴对称,即有 \( \sin {k\alpha } =  - \sin \left( {{50} - {k\alpha }}\right) \) ,

所以 \( {S}_{k} = \frac{1}{1}\sin \alpha  + \frac{1}{2}\sin {2\alpha } + \cdots  + \frac{1}{23}\sin {23\alpha } + \frac{1}{24}\sin {24\alpha } + 0 \)

\( + \frac{1}{26}\sin {26\alpha } + \frac{1}{27}\sin {27\alpha } + \cdots  + \frac{1}{k}\sin {k\alpha } \)

\( = \frac{1}{1}\sin \alpha  + \frac{1}{2}\sin {2\alpha } + \cdots  + \left( {\frac{1}{24} - \frac{1}{26}}\right) \sin {24\alpha } +  + \left( {\frac{1}{23} - \frac{1}{27}}\right) \sin {23\alpha } \)

\( + \cdots  + \left( {\frac{1}{{50} - k} - \frac{1}{k}}\right) \sin \left( {{50} - k}\right) \alpha \) ,其中 \( k = {26},{27},\cdots ,{49} \) ,

此时 \( 0 < {50} - k < k \) ,

所以 \( \frac{1}{{50} - k} - \frac{1}{k} > 0 \) ,又 \( 0 < \left( {{50} - k}\right) \alpha  \leq  {24\alpha } < \pi \) ,所以 \( \sin \left( {{50} - k}\right) \alpha  > 0 \) ,

从而当 \( k = {26},{27},\cdots ,{49} \) 时， \( {S}_{k} \) 都是正数， \( {S}_{50} = {S}_{49} + {S}_{50} = {S}_{49} + 0 = {S}_{49} > 0 \) .

对于 \( k \) 从 51 到 100 的情况同上可知 \( {S}_{k} \) 都是正数.

填空

5. 计算: \( \frac{3 - i}{1 + i} = \) ___(i 为虚数单位).

【答案】 \( 1 - 2\mathrm{i} \)

复数 \( \frac{3 - i}{1 + i} = \frac{\left( {3 - \mathrm{i}}\right) \left( {1 - \mathrm{i}}\right) }{\left( {1 + \mathrm{i}}\right) \left( {1 - \mathrm{i}}\right) } = \frac{2 - {4i}}{2} = 1 - 2\mathrm{i} \) .

6. 若集合 \( A = \{ x \mid  {2x} + {10}\} , B = \{ x\left| \right| x - 1 \mid   < 2\} \) ，则 \( A \cap  B = \) ___.

【答案】 \( \left( {-\frac{1}{2},3}\right) \)

根据集合 \( A = \{ x \mid  {2x} + {10}\}  = \left\{  {x\left| {\;x >  - \frac{1}{2}}\right. }\right\} \) ，

\( B = \{ x\left| \right| x - 1 \mid   < 2\}  = \{ x \mid   - 1 < x < 3\} , \)

所以 \( A \cap  B = \left\{  {x\left| {\; - \frac{1}{2} < x < 3}\right. }\right\} \) ,即 \( \left( {-\frac{1}{2},3}\right) \) .

7. 函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = \left| \begin{matrix} 2 & \cos x \\  \sin x &  - 1 \end{matrix}\right| \) 的值域是___.

【答案】 \( \left\lbrack  {-\frac{5}{2}, - \frac{3}{2}}\right\rbrack \)

函数 \( f\left( x\right)  =  - \sin x\cos x - 2 =  - 2 - \frac{1}{2}\sin {2x} \) ,

因为 \( - 1 \leq  \sin {2x} \leq  1 \) ,所以 \( - \frac{5}{2} \leq  f\left( x\right)  \leq   - \frac{3}{2} \) .

8. 若 \( \overrightarrow{n} = \left( {-2,1}\right) \) 是直线 \( l \) 的一个法向量，则 \( l \) 的倾斜角的大小为___(结果用反三角函数值表示).

【答案】arctan2

设直线的倾斜角为 \( \alpha \) ,则 \( \tan \alpha  = 2 \) ,所以 \( \alpha  = \arctan 2 \) .

9. 在 \( {\left( x - \frac{2}{x}\right) }^{6} \) 的二项展开式中，常数项等于___.

【答案】 -160

\( {T}_{r + 1} = {C}_{6}^{r}{x}^{6 - r}{\left( -\frac{2}{x}\right) }^{r} = {C}_{6}^{r}{\left( -1\right) }^{r}{x}^{6 - {2r}}, \)

令 \( 6 - {2r} = 0 \) ,得 \( r = 3 \) ,

故常数项为 \( {C}_{6}^{3}{\left( -2\right) }^{3} =  - {160} \) .

10. 有一列正方体，棱长组成以 1 为首项， \( \frac{1}{2} \) 为公比的等比数列，体积分别记为 \( {V}_{1} \) ， \( {V}_{2} \) ， \( \cdots \) ， \( {V}_{n},\cdots \) ,则 \( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n\infty }}\left( {{V}_{1} + {V}_{2} + \cdots  + {V}_{n}}\right)  = \) ___.

【答案】 \( \frac{8}{7} \)

由题意可知, 该列正方体的体积构成以

1 为首项, \( \frac{1}{8} \) 为公比的等比数列,

\( \therefore {V}_{1} + {V}_{2} + \cdots  + {V}_{n} = \frac{1 - \frac{1}{{8}^{n}}}{1 - \frac{1}{8}} = \frac{8}{7}\left( {1 - \frac{1}{{8}^{n}}}\right) \) ,

\( \therefore \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\left( {{V}_{1} + {V}_{2} + \cdots  + {V}_{n}}\right)  = \frac{8}{7} \) .

11. 已知函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{\left| x - a\right| }\left( {a\text{ 为常数 }}\right) \) . 若 \( f\left( x\right) \) 在区间 \( \lbrack 1, + \infty ) \) 上是增函数,则 \( a \) 的取值范围是 ___.

【答案】 \( ( - \infty ,1\rbrack \)

根据函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{\left| x - a\right| } = \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {\mathrm{e}}^{x - a}, \\  {\mathrm{e}}^{-x + a}, \end{array}\right. \)

看出当 \( x \geq  a \) 时函数为增函数,

而已知函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 在区间 \( \lbrack 1, + \infty ) \) 上为增函数,

所以 \( a \) 的取值范围为 \( ( - \infty ,1\rbrack \) .

12. 若一个圆锥的侧面展开图是面积为 \( {2\pi } \) 的半圆面,则该圆锥的体积为___.

【答案】 \( \frac{\sqrt{3}}{3}\pi \)

根据该圆锥的底面圆的半径为 \( r \) ,母线长为 \( l \) ,

根据条件得到 \( \frac{1}{2}\pi {l}^{2} = {2\pi } \) ,

【解析】得母线长 \( l = 2,{2\pi r} = {\pi l} = {2\pi }, r = 1 \) ,

所以该圆锥的体积为: \( V = \frac{1}{3}{Sh} = \frac{1}{3} \times  \sqrt{{2}^{2} - {1}^{2}}\pi  = \frac{\sqrt{3}}{3}\pi \) .

13. 已知 \( y = f\left( x\right)  + {x}^{2} \) 是奇函数,且 \( f\left( 1\right)  = 1 \) . 若 \( g\left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right)  + 2 \) ,则 \( g\left( {-1}\right)  = \) ___.

【答案】-1

因为函数 \( y = f\left( x\right)  + {x}^{2} \) 为奇函数,

所以 \( g\left( 1\right)  = f\left( 1\right)  + 2 \) ,又 \( f\left( 1\right)  = 1 \) ,

所以 \( g\left( 1\right)  = 3, f\left( {-1}\right)  =  - 3 \) ,

\( g\left( {-1}\right)  = f\left( {-1}\right)  + 2 =  - 3 + 2 =  - 1,\;f\left( {-1}\right)  =  - f\left( 1\right)  =  - 1. \)

14. 如图,在极坐标系中,过点 \( M\left( {2,0}\right) \) 的直线 \( l \) 与极轴的夹角 \( \alpha  = \frac{\pi }{6} \) . 若将 \( l \) 的极坐标方程写

成 \( \rho  = f\left( \theta \right) \) 的形式，则 \( f![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_108_889_1135_284_155_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_108_889_1135_284_155_0.jpg)9b5b00_108_889_1135_284_155_0.jpg)

【答案】 \( \frac{1}{\sin \left( {\frac{\pi }{6} - \theta }\right) } \)

根据该直线过点 \( M\left( {2,0}\right) \) ,

可以直接写出代数形式的方程为: \( y = \frac{1}{2}\left( {x - 2}\right) \) ,

将此化成极坐标系下的参数方程即可,

化简得 \( f\left( \theta \right)  = \frac{1}{\sin \left( {\frac{\pi }{6} - \theta }\right) } \) .

15. 三位同学参加跳高、跳远、铅球项目的比赛. 若每人都选择其中两个项目，则有且仅有两人选择的项目完全相同的概率是___(结果用最简分数表示).

【答案】 \( \frac{2}{3} \)

三位同学从三个项目选其中两个项目有 \( {C}_{3}^{2}{C}_{3}^{2}{C}_{3}^{2} = {27} \) 中,

若有且仅有两人选择的项目完成相同,则有 \( {C}_{3}^{2}{C}_{3}^{2}{C}_{2}^{1} = {18} \) ,

所以有且仅有两人选择的项目完成相同的概率为 \( \frac{18}{27} = \frac{2}{3} \) .

16. 在平行四边形 \( {ABCD} \) 中, \( \angle A = \frac{\pi }{3} \) ,边 \( {AB},{AD} \) 的长分别为2,1. 若 \( M, N \) 分别是边 \( {BC},{CD} \) 上的点，且满足 \( \frac{\left| \overrightarrow{BM}\right| }{\left| \overrightarrow{BC}\right| } = \frac{\left| \overrightarrow{CN}\right| }{\left| \overrightarrow{CD}\right| } \) ，则 \( \overrightarrow{AM} \cdot  \overrightarrow{AN} \) 的取值范围是___.

【答案】 \( \left\lbrack  {2,5}\right\rbrack \)

以向量 \( {AB} \) 所在直线为 \( x \) 轴,

以向量 \( {AD} \) 所在![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_109_406_1085_331_256_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_109_406_1085_331_256_0.jpg)9b5b00_109_406_1085_331_256_0.jpg)

因为 \( {AB} = 2,{AD} = 1 \) ,

所以 \( A\left( {0,0}\right) , B\left( {2,0}\right) , C\left( {\frac{5}{2},1}\right) , D\left( {\frac{1}{2},1}\right) \)

设 \( N\left( {x,1}\right) \left( {\frac{1}{2} \leq  x \leq  \frac{5}{2}}\right) \) ,则 \( {BM} = \frac{1}{2}{CN} \) ,

\( {CN} = \frac{5}{2} - x,\;{BM} = \frac{5}{4} - \frac{1}{2}x, \)

\( M\left( {2 + \frac{5}{8} - \frac{1}{4}x,\left( {\frac{5}{4} - \frac{1}{2}x}\right) \sin \frac{\pi }{3}}\right) \)

根据题意，

有 \( \overrightarrow{AN} = \left( {x,1}\right) ,\overrightarrow{AM} = \left( {\frac{21}{8} - \frac{x}{4},\frac{5\sqrt{3} - 2\sqrt{3}x}{8}}\right) \) .

所以 \( \overrightarrow{AN} \cdot  \overrightarrow{AM} = x\left( {\frac{21}{8} - \frac{x}{4}}\right)  + \frac{5\sqrt{3} - 2\sqrt{3}x}{8}\left( {\frac{1}{2} \leq  x \leq  \frac{5}{2}}\right) \) ,

所以 \( 2 \leq  \overrightarrow{AM} \cdot  \overrightarrow{AN} \leq  5 \) .

17. 已知函数 \( y = f\left( x\right) \) 的图像是折线段 \( {ABC} \) ,若中 \( A\left( {0,0}\right) , B\left( {\frac{1}{2},5}\right) , C\left( {1,0}\right) \) . 函数 \( y = \; {xf}\left( x\right) \left( {0 \leq  x \leq  1}\right) \) 的图像与 \( x \) 轴围成的图形的面积为___.

【答案】 \( \frac{5}{4} \)

根据题意得到, \( f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {10x}, \\   - {10x} + {10}, \end{array}\right. \)

从而得到 \( y = {xf}\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {10}{x}^{2}, \\   - {10}{x}^{2} + {10x}, \end{array}\right. \)

所以围成的面积为 \( S = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{1}{2}}{10x}\mathrm{\;d}x + {\int }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{1}\left( {-{10}{x}^{2} + {10x}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{5}{4} \) ,

所以围成的图形的面积为 \( \frac{5}{4} \) .

18. 如图, \( {AD} \) 与 \( {BC} \) 是四面体 \( {ABCD![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_110_1215_1241_225_296_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_110_1215_1241_225_296_0.jpg)b5b00_110_1215_1241_225_296_0.jpg)

\( {AD} = \)

\( {2c} \) ,且 \( {AB} + {BD} = {AC} + {CD} = {2a} \) ,其中 \( a, c \) 为常数,则四面体 \( {ABCD} \) 的体积的最大值是 ___.

【答案】 \( \frac{2}{3}c\sqrt{{a}^{2} - {c}^{2} - 1} \)

据题 \( {AB} + {BD} = {AC} + {CD} = {2a} \) ,也就是说,

线段 \( {AB} + {BD} \) 与线段 \( {AC} + {CD} \) 的长度是定值,

因为棱 \( {AD} \) 与棱 \( {BC} \) 互相垂直，

当 \( {BC} \bot \) 平面 \( {ABD} \) 时,此时有最大值,

此时最大值为: \( \frac{2}{3}c\sqrt{{a}^{2} - {c}^{2} - 1} \) .

【解析】答

19. 如图,在四棱锥 \( P - {ABCD} \) 中,底面 \( {ABCD} \) 是矩形, \( {PA} \bot \) 底面 \( {ABCD}, E \) 是 \( {PC} \) 的中

点. 已知 \( {AB} = 2,{![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_111_954_471_357_270_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_111_954_471_357_270_0.jpg)39b5b00_111_954_471_357_270_0.jpg)

(1)三角形 \( {PCD} \) 的面积;

【答案】 \( 2\sqrt{3} \) .

因为 \( {PA} \bot \) 底面 \( {ABCD} \) ,所以 \( {PA} \bot  {AD} \) ,又 \( {AD} \bot  {CD} \) ,

所以 \( {CD} \bot  {CD} \bot \) 平面 \( {PAD} \) ,从而 \( {CD} \bot  {PD} \) .

因为 \( {PD} = \sqrt{{2}^{2} + {\left( 2\sqrt{2}\right) }^{2}} = 2\sqrt{3},{CD} = 2 \) ,

所以三角形 \( {PCD} \) 的面积为

\[
\frac{1}{2} \times  2 \times  2\sqrt{3} = 2\sqrt{3}.
\]

(2) 异面直线 \( {BC} \) 与 \( {AE} \) 所成的![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_111_1016_1313_447_349_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_111_1016_1313_447_349_0.jpg)b5b00_111_1016_1313_447_349_0.jpg)

[解法一] 如图所示, 建立空间直角坐标系, 则 \( B\left( {2,0,0}\right) ,\;C\left( {2,2\sqrt{2},0}\right) ,\;E\left( {1,\sqrt{2},1}\right) \) , \( \overrightarrow{AE} = \left( {1,\sqrt{2},1}\right) ,\;\overrightarrow{BC} = \left( {0,2\sqrt{2},0}\right) . \)

设 \( \overrightarrow{AE} \) 与 \( \overrightarrow{BC} \) 的夹角为 \( \theta \) ,则

\[
\cos \theta  = \frac{\overrightarrow{AE} \cdot  \overrightarrow{BC}}{\left| \overrightarrow{AE}\right|  \cdot  \left| \overrightarrow{BC}\right| } = \frac{4}{2 \times  2\sqrt{2}} = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2},\;\theta  = \frac{\pi }{4}.
\]

由此可知,异面直线 \( {BC} \) 与 \( {AE} ![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_112_1021_243_353_262_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_112_1021_243_353_262_0.jpg)9b5b00_112_1021_243_353_262_0.jpg)

[解法二]取 \( {PB} \) 中点 \( F \) ,连接 \( {EF}\text{ 、 }{AF} \) ,则

\( {EF}//{BC} \) ,从而 \( \angle {AEF} \) (或其补角) 是异面直线 \( {BC} \) 与 \( {AE} \) 所成的角

在 \( {AEF} \) 中,由 \( {EF} = \sqrt{2}\text{ 、 }{AF} = \sqrt{2}\text{ 、 }{AE} = 2 \) 知 \( {AEF} \) 是等腰直角三角形,

所以 \( \angle {AEF} = \frac{\pi }{4} \) .

因此异面直线 \( {BC} \) 与 \( {AE} \) 所成的角的大小是 \( \frac{\pi }{4} \)

20. 已知函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = \lg \left( {x + 1}\right) \) .

(1)若 \( 0 < f\left( {1 - {2x}}\right)  - f\left( x\right)  < 1 \) ，求 \( x \) 的取值范围；

【答案】 \( - \frac{2}{3} < x < \frac{1}{3} \) .

由 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} 2 - {2x} > 0 \\  x + 1 > 0 \end{array}\right. \) ,得 \( - 1 < x < 1 \) .

由 \( 0 < \lg \left( {2 - {2x}}\right)  - \lg \left( {x + 1}\right)  = \lg \frac{2 - {2x}}{x + 1} < 1 \) 得 \( 1 < \frac{2 - {2x}}{x + 1} < {10} \) .

因为 \( x + 1 > 0 \) ,所以 \( x + 1 < 2 - {2x} < {10x} + {10}, - \frac{2}{3} < x < \frac{1}{3} \) .

由 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l}  - 1 < x < 1 \\   - \frac{2}{3} < x < \frac{1}{3} \end{array}\right. \) 得 \( - \frac{2}{3} < x < \frac{1}{3} \) .

( 2 )若 \( g\left( x\right) \) 是以 2 为周期的偶函数，且当 \( 0 \leq  x \leq  1 \) 时，有 \( g\left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right) \) ，求函数 \( y = \; g\left( x\right) \left( {x \in  \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack  }\right) \) 的反函数.

【答案】 \( y = 3 - {10}^{x},\;x \in  \left\lbrack  {0,\lg 2}\right\rbrack \) .

当 \( x \in  \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack \) 时, \( 2 - x \in  \left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack \) ,因此

\( y = g\left( x\right)  = g\left( {x - 2}\right)  = g\left( {2 - x}\right)  = f\left( {2 - x}\right)  = \lg \left( {3 - x}\right) . \)

由单调性可得 \( y \in  \left\lbrack  {0,\lg 2}\right\rbrack \) .

因为 \( x = 3 - {10}^{y} \) ,所以所求反函数是 \( y = 3 - {10}^{x}, x \in  \left\lbrack  {0,\lg 2}\right\rbrack \) .

21. 海事救援船对一艘失事船进行定位:以失事船的当前位置为原点，以正北方向为 \( y \) 轴正方向建立平面直角坐标系 (以 1 海里为单位长度),则救援船恰在失事船的正南方向 12 海里 \( A \) 处, 如图. 现假设:

①失事船的移动路径可视为抛物线 \( y = \frac{12}{49}![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_113_1017_680_280_326_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_113_1017_680_280_326_0.jpg)9b5b00_113_1017_680_280_326_0.jpg)

救援船出发 \( t \) 小时后，失事船所在位置的横坐标为 \( {7t} \) .

(1)当 \( t = {0.5} \) 时，写出失事船所在位置 \( P \) 的纵坐标. 若此时两船恰好会合，求救援船速度的大小和方向;

【答案】速度的大小为 \( \sqrt{949} \) 海里/时,方向为北偏东 \( \arctan \frac{7}{30} \) 弧度.

\( t = {0.5} \) 时, \( P \) 的横坐标 \( {x}_{p} = {7t} = \frac{7}{2} \) ,代入抛物线方程 \( y = \frac{12}{49}{x}^{2} \) 中,

得 \( P \) 的纵坐标 \( {y}_{p} = 3 \) .

由 \( \left| {AP}\right|  = \frac{\sqrt{949}}{2} \) ,得救援船速度的大小为 \( \sqrt{949} \) 海里/时.

由 \( \tan \angle {OAP} = \frac{\frac{7}{2}}{3 + {12}} = \frac{7}{30} \) ,得 \( \angle {OAP} = \arctan \frac{7}{30} \) ,故救援船速度的方向

为北偏东 \( \arctan \frac{7}{30} \) 弧度.

(2)问救援船的时速至少是多少海里才能追上失事船？

【答案】 25 海里.

设救援船的时速为 \( v \) 海里,经过 \( t \) 小时追上失事船,此时位置为 \( \left( {{7t},{12}{t}^{2}}\right) \) .

由 \( {vt} = \sqrt{{\left( 7t\right) }^{2} + {\left( {12}{t}^{2} + {12}\right) }^{2}} \) ,整理得 \( {v}^{2} = {144}\left( {{t}^{2} + \frac{1}{{t}^{2}}}\right)  + {337} \) .

因为 \( {t}^{2} + \frac{1}{{t}^{2}} \geq  2 \) ,当且仅当 \( t = 1 \) 时等号成立,

所以 \( {v}^{2} \geq  {144} \times  2 + {337} = {25}^{2} \) ,即 \( v \geq  {25} \) .

因此, 救援船的时速至少是 25 海里才能追上失事船.

22. 在平面直角坐标系 \( {xOy} \) 中,已知双曲线 \( {C}_{1} : 2{x}^{2} - {y}^{2} = 1 \) .

(1)过 \( {C}_{1} \) 的左顶点引 \( {C}_{1} \) 的一条渐近线的平行线，求该直线与另一条渐近线及 \( x \) 轴围成的三角形的面积;

【答案】 \( \frac{\sqrt{2}}{8} \)

双曲线 \( {C}_{1} : \frac{{x}^{2}}{\frac{1}{2}} - {y}^{2} = 1 \) ,左顶点 \( A\left( {-\frac{\sqrt{2}}{2},0}\right) \) ,渐近线方程: \( y =  \pm  \sqrt{2}x \) .

过点 \( A \) 与渐近线 \( y = \sqrt{2}x \) 平行的直线方程为 \( y = \sqrt{2}\left( {x + \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}}\right) \) ,即 \( y = \sqrt{2}x + 1 \) .

【解析】方程组 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} y =  - \sqrt{2}x \\  y = \sqrt{2}x + 1 \end{array}\right. \) 得 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} x =  - \frac{\sqrt{2}}{4} \\  y = \frac{1}{2} \end{array}\right. \)

所以所求三角形的面积为 \( S = \frac{1}{2}\left| {OA}\right| \left| y\right|  = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{8} \) .

(2)设斜率为 1 的直线 \( l \) 交 \( {C}_{1} \) 于 \( P\text{ 、 }Q \) 两点，若 \( l \) 与圆 \( {x}^{2} + {y}^{2} = 1 \) 相切，求证: \( {OP}\bot {OQ} \) ；

【答案】见解析

设直线 \( {PQ} \) 的方程是 \( y = x + b \) . 因直线与已知圆相切,

故 \( \frac{\left| b\right| }{\sqrt{2}} = 1 \) ,即 \( {b}^{2} = 2 \) .

由 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} y = x + b \\  2{x}^{2} - {y}^{2} = 1 \end{array}\right. \) ,得 \( {x}^{2} - {2bx} - {b}^{2} - 1 = 0 \) .

设 \( P\left( {{x}_{1},{y}_{1}}\right) \text{ 、 }Q\left( {{x}_{2},{y}_{2}}\right) \) ,则 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {x}_{1} + {x}_{2} = {2b} \\  {x}_{1}{x}_{2} =  - {b}^{2} - 1 \end{array}\right. \)

所以 \( \overrightarrow{OP} \cdot  \overrightarrow{OQ} = {x}_{1}{x}_{2} + {y}_{1}{y}_{2} = 2{x}_{1}{x}_{2} + b\left( {{x}_{1} + {x}_{2}}\right)  + {b}^{2} = 2\left( {-{b}^{2} - 1}\right)  + b \cdot  {2b} + {b}^{2} = {b}^{2} - 2 \; = 0 \) ,

故 \( {OP} \bot  {OQ} \) .

(3)设椭圆 \( {C}_{2} : 4{x}^{2} + {y}^{2} = 1 \) . 若 \( M \) 、 \( N \) 分别是 \( {C}_{1} \) 、 \( {C}_{2} \) 上的动点，且 \( {OM}\bot {ON} \) ，求证: \( O \) 到直线 \( {MN} \) 的距离是定值.

【答案】见解析

当直线 \( {ON} \) 垂直于 \( x \) 轴时,

\( \left| {ON}\right|  = 1,\left| {OM}\right|  = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2} \) ,则 \( O \) 到直线 \( {MN} \) 的距离为 \( \frac{\sqrt{3}}{3} \) .

当直线 \( {ON} \) 不垂直于 \( x \) 轴时,

设直线 \( {ON} \) 的方程为 \( y = {kx} \) (显然 \( \left| k\right|  > \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2} \) ),则直线 \( {OM} \) 的方程为 \( y =  - \frac{1}{k}x \) .

由 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} y = {kx} \\  4{x}^{2} + {y}^{2} = 1 \end{array}\right. \) 得 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {x}^{2} = \frac{1}{4 + {k}^{2}} \\  {y}^{2} = \frac{{k}^{2}}{4 + {k}^{2}} \end{array}\right. \) 所以 \( {\left| ON\right| }^{2} = \frac{1 + {k}^{2}}{4 + {k}^{2}} \) ,

同理 \( {\left| OM\right| }^{2} = \frac{1 + {k}^{2}}{2{k}^{2} - 1} \) .

设 \( O \) 到直线 \( {MN} \) 的距离为 \( d \) ,因为 \( \left( {{\left| OM\right| }^{2} + {\left| ON\right| }^{2}}\right) {d}^{2} = {\left| OM\right| }^{2}{\left| ON\right| }^{2} \) ,

所以 \( \frac{1}{{d}^{2}} = \frac{1}{{\left| OM\right| }^{2}} + \frac{1}{{\left| ON\right| }^{2}} = \frac{3{k}^{2} + 3}{{k}^{2} + 1} = 3 \) ,即 \( d = \frac{\sqrt{3}}{3} \) .

综上, \( O \) 到直线 \( {MN} \) 的距离是定值.

23. 对于数集 \( X =  - 1,{x}_{1},{x}_{2},\cdots ,{x}_{n} \) ,其中 \( 0 < {x}_{1} < {x}_{2} < \cdots  < {x}_{n}, n \geq  2 \) ,定义向量集 \( Y = \; \left\{  {\overrightarrow{a} \mid  \overrightarrow{a} = \left( {s, t}\right) , s \in  X, t \in  X}\right\} \) . 若对于任意 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{1} \in  Y \) ,存在 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{2} \in  Y \) ,使得 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{1} \cdot  {\overrightarrow{a}}_{2} = 0 \) ,则称 \( X \) 具有性质 \( P \) . 例如 \( X = \{  - 1,1,2\} \) 具有性质 \( P \) .

(1)若 \( x > 2 \) ，且 \( \{  - 1,1,2, x\} \) ，求 \( x \) 的值；

【答案】 \( x = 4 \) .

选取 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{1} = \left( {x,2}\right) , Y \) 中与 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{1} \) 垂直的元素必有形式 \( \left( {-1, b}\right) \) .

所以 \( x = {2b} \) ,从而 \( x = 4 \) .

( 2 )若 \( X \) 具有性质 \( P \) ，求证: \( 1 \in  X \) ，且当 \( {x}_{n} > 1 \) 时， \( {x}_{1} = 1 \) ；

【答案】证明见解析.

取 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{1} = \left( {{x}_{1},{x}_{1}}\right)  \in  Y \) . 设 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{2} = \left( {s, t}\right)  \in  Y \) 满足 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{1} \cdot  {\overrightarrow{a}}_{2} = 0 \) .

由 \( \left( {s + t}\right) {x}_{1} = 0 \) 得 \( s + t = 0 \) ,所以 \( s\text{ 、 }t \) 异号.

因为-1是 \( X \) 中唯一的负数,所以 \( s\text{ 、 }t \) 中之一为 -1,另一为 1,

故 \( 1 \in  X \) .

假设 \( {x}_{k} = 1 \) ,其中 \( 1 < k < n \) ,则 \( 0 < {x}_{1} < 1 < {x}_{n} \) .

选取 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{1} = \left( {{x}_{1},{x}_{n}}\right)  \in  Y \) ,并设 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{2} = \left( {s, t}\right)  \in  Y \) 满足 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{1} \cdot  {\overrightarrow{a}}_{2} = 0 \) ,即 \( s{x}_{1} + t{x}_{n} = 0 \) ,

则 \( s\text{ 、 }t \) 异号,从而 \( s\text{ 、 }t \) 之中恰有一个为 -1 .

若 \( s =  - 1 \) ,则2,矛盾;

若 \( t =  - 1 \) ,则 \( {x}_{n} = s{x}_{1} < s \leq  {x}_{n} \) ,矛盾.

所以 \( {x}_{1} = 1 \) .

(3)若 \( X \) 具有性质 \( P \) ，且 \( {x}_{1} = 1,{x}_{2} = q \) ( \( q \) 为常数)，求有穷数列 \( {x}_{1} \) ， \( {x}_{2} \) ， \( \cdots \) ， \( {x}_{n} \) 的通项公式.

【答案】 \( {x}_{i} = {q}^{i - 1},\mathrm{i} = 1,2,\cdots , n \) .

猜测 \( {x}_{i} = {q}^{i - 1},\mathrm{i} = 1,2,\cdots , n \) .

\[
\text{ 记 }{A}_{k} = \left\{  {-1,1,{x}_{2},\cdots ,{x}_{k}}\right\}  , k = 2,3,\cdots , n\text{ . }
\]

先证明: 若 \( {A}_{k + 1} \) 具有性质 \( P \) ,则 \( {A}_{k} \) 也具有性质 \( P \) .

任取 \( \overrightarrow{{a}_{1}} = \left( {s, t}\right) , s\text{ 、 }t \in  {A}_{k} \) . 当 \( s\text{ 、 }t \) 中出现 -1 时,显然有 \( \overrightarrow{{a}_{2}} \) 满足 \( \overrightarrow{{a}_{1}} \cdot  \overrightarrow{{a}_{2}} = 0 \) ;

当 \( s \neq   - 1 \) 且 \( t \neq   - 1 \) 时, \( s\text{ 、 }t \geq  1 \) .

因为 \( {A}_{k + 1} \) 具有性质 \( P \) ,所以有 \( \overrightarrow{{a}_{2}} = \left( {{s}_{1},{t}_{1}}\right) ,{s}_{1}\text{ 、 }{t}_{1} \in  {A}_{k + 1} \) ,使得 \( \overrightarrow{{a}_{1}} \cdot  \overrightarrow{{a}_{2}} = 0 \) ,

从而 \( {s}_{1} \) 和 \( {t}_{1} \) 中有一个是 -1,不妨设 \( {s}_{1} =  - 1 \) .

假设 \( {t}_{1} \in  {A}_{k + 1} \) 且 \( {t}_{1} \notin  {A}_{k} \) ,则 \( {t}_{1} = {x}_{k + 1} \) . 由 \( \left( {s, t}\right)  \cdot  \left( {-1,{x}_{k + 1}}\right)  = 0 \) ,得 \( s = t{x}_{k + 1} \geq  {x}_{k + 1} \) ,

与

\( s \in  {A}_{k} \) 矛盾. 所以 \( {t}_{1} \in  {A}_{k} \) . 从而 \( {A}_{k} \) 也具有性质 \( P \) .

现用数学归纳法证明: \( {x}_{i} = {q}^{i - 1},\mathrm{i} = 1,2,\cdots , n \) .

当 \( n = 2 \) 时,结论显然成立;

假设 \( n = k \) 时, \( {A}_{k} = \left\{  {-1,1,{x}_{2},\cdots ,{x}_{k}}\right\} \) 有性质 \( P \) ,则 \( {x}_{i} = {q}^{i - 1},\mathrm{i} = 1,2,\cdots , k \) ;

当 \( n = k + 1 \) 时,若 \( {A}_{k + 1} = \left\{  {-1,1,{x}_{2},\cdots ,{x}_{k},{x}_{k + 1}}\right\} \) 有性质 \( P \) ,则 \( {A}_{k} = \)

\( \left\{  {-1,1,{x}_{2},\cdots ,{x}_{k}}\right\} \)

也有性质 \( P \) ,所以 \( {A}_{k + 1} = \left\{  {-1,1, q,\cdots ,{q}^{k - 1},{x}_{k + 1}}\right\} \) .

取 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{1} = \left( {{x}_{k + 1}, q}\right) \) ,并设 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{2} = \left( {s, t}\right) \) 满足 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{1} \cdot  {\overrightarrow{a}}_{2} = 0 \) ,即 \( {x}_{k + 1}s + {qt} = 0 \) .

由此可得 \( s \) 与 \( t \) 中有且只有一个为 -1 .

若 \( t =  - 1 \) ,则 1,不可能;

所以 \( s =  - 1,{x}_{k + 1} = {qt} \leq  q \cdot  {q}^{k - 1} = {q}^{k} \) ,又 \( {x}_{k + 1} > {q}^{k - 1} \) ,所以 \( {x}_{k + 1} = {q}^{k} \) .

综上所述， \( {x}_{i} = {q}^{i - 1},\mathrm{i} = 1,2,\cdots , n \) .

一、填空题 (本大题满分 56 分) 本大题共有 14 题, 要求直接填写结果, 每题答对得 4 分, 否则一律得零分。

1. 已知集合 \( A = \{ 1,2, k\} , B = \{ 2,5\} \) . 若 \( A \cup  B = \{ 1,2,3,5\} \) ，则 \( k = \) ___.

## 【答案】 3

\( \because A = \{ 1,2, k\} , B = \{ 2,5\} \) ,且 \( A \cup  B = \{ 1,2,3,5\} \)

\( \therefore 3 \in  A \)

\( \therefore k = 3 \)

3

2. 函数 \( y = \sqrt{x + 2} \) 的定义域是___.

【答案】 \( \lbrack  - 2, + \infty ) \)

\( \because \) 函数 \( y = \sqrt{x + 2} \) ,

\( \therefore x + 2 \geq  0 \) ,

\( \therefore x \geq   - 2 \) ,

\( \lbrack  - 2, + \infty ) \)

3. 抛物线 \( {y}^{2} = {8x} \) 的焦点坐标是___.

【答案】 \( \left( {2,0}\right) \)

抛物线 \( {y}^{2} = {8x} \) ,

所以 \( p = 4 \) ,

所以焦点 \( \left( {2,0}\right) \) ,

故答案为 \( \left( {2,0}\right) \)

4. 若复数 \( z \) 满足 \( {iz} = 1 + \mathrm{i} \) ( \( \mathrm{i} \) 为虚数单位),则 \( z = \) ___.

【答案】 \( 1 - \mathrm{i} \)

由 \( {iz} = 1 + \mathrm{i} \) ,得 \( z = \frac{1 + i}{i} = \frac{\left( {1 + \mathrm{i}}\right) \left( {-\mathrm{i}}\right) }{i\left( {-\mathrm{i}}\right) } = 1 - \mathrm{i} \; 1 - \mathrm{i} \) .

5. 函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = \sin \left( {{2x} + \frac{\pi }{4}}\right) \) 的最小正周期为___.

【答案】 \( \pi \)

\[
f\left( x\right)  = \sin \left( {{2x} + \frac{\pi }{4}}\right) ,
\]

\( \because \omega  = 2 \) ,

\( \therefore T = \frac{2\pi }{2} = \pi \) ,

则函数的最小正周期为 \( \pi \) .

\( \pi \)

6. 方程 \( {4}^{x} - {2}^{x + 1} = 0 \) 的解为___.

## 【答案】 1

\( \because {4}^{x} = {2}^{2x} \) ,

\( \therefore \) 方程 \( {4}^{x} - {2}^{x + 1} = 0 \) 可化为: \( {2}^{2x} = {2}^{x + 1} \) ,

\( \therefore {2x} = x + 1 \) ,

\( \therefore x = 1 \) .

1.

7. 若 \( {\left( 2x - 1\right) }^{5} = {a}_{0} + {a}_{1}x + {a}_{2}{x}^{2} + {a}_{3}{x}^{3} + {a}_{4}{x}^{4} + {a}_{5}{x}^{5} \) ,则 \( {a}_{0} + {a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + {a}_{3} + {a}_{4} + {a}_{5} = \) ___.

## 【答案】 1

令 \( x = 1 \) 可得， \( {\left( 2 - 1\right) }^{5} = 1 = {a}_{0} + {a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + {a}_{3} + {a}_{4} + {a}_{5} \) ，

则 \( {a}_{0} + {a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + {a}_{3} + {a}_{4} + {a}_{5} = 1 \) ,

1.

8. 若 \( f\left( x\right)  = \frac{\left( {x + 2}\right) \left( {x + m}\right) }{x} \) 为奇函数,则实数 \( m = \) ___.

【答案】 -2

\( \because f\left( x\right)  = \frac{\left( {x + 2}\right) \left( {x + m}\right) }{x} \) 为奇函数,

\( \therefore f\left( {-1}\right)  =  - f\left( 1\right) \)

即 \( m - 1 = 3\left( {1 + m}\right) \)

\( \therefore m =  - 2 \)

-2

9. 函数 \( y = {\log }_{2}x + \frac{4}{{\log }_{2}x}\left( {x \in  \left\lbrack  {2,4}\right\rbrack  }\right) \) 的最大值为___.

## 【答案】 5

设 \( t = {\log }_{2}x,\;\because x \in  \left\lbrack  \begin{array}{ll} 2, & 4 \end{array}\right\rbrack  ,\;\therefore t \in  \left\lbrack  \begin{array}{ll} 1, & 2 \end{array}\right\rbrack \)

\( \because y = t + \frac{4}{t} \) 的导函数 \( {y}^{\prime } = 1 - \frac{4}{{t}^{2}} < {0t} \in  \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack \)

\( \therefore y = t + \frac{4}{t} \) 在 \( \left\lbrack  \begin{array}{ll} 1, & 2 \end{array}\right\rbrack \) 上为减函数,

\( \therefore y = t + \frac{4}{t} \) 的最大值为 \( 1 + \frac{4}{1} = 5 \)

\( \therefore y = {\log }_{2}x + \frac{4}{{\log }_{2}x}\left( {x \in  \left\lbrack  {2,4}\right\rbrack  }\right) \) 的最大值为 5

故答案为 5

10. 若复数 \( z \) 满足 \( \left| {z - \mathrm{i}}\right|  \leq  \sqrt{2} \) ( \( \mathrm{i} \) 为虚数单位),则 \( z \) 在复平面内所对应的图形的面积为___.

【答案】 \( {2\pi } \)

\( \because \left| {z - \mathrm{i}}\right|  \leq  \sqrt{2} \) ,

\( \therefore z \) 在复平面内所对应的点 \( Z \) 的轨迹是以 \( \left( {0,1}\right) \) 为圆心, \( \sqrt{2} \) 为半径的实心圆,

\( \therefore \) 该圆的面积为: \( \pi {\left( \sqrt{2}\right) }^{2} = {2\pi } \) .

\( {2\pi } \)

11. 某校要从 2 名男生和 4 名女生中选出 4 人担任某游泳赛事的志愿者工作，则在选出的志愿者中，男、女生都有的概率为___. (结果用数值表示)

【答案】 \( \frac{14}{15} \)

根据题意,从 2 名男生和 4 名女生中选出 4 人,有 \( {C}_{6}^{4} = {15} \) 种取法,

其中全部为女生的有 \( {C}_{4}^{4} = 1 \) 种情况,没有全部为男生的情况,

则选出的 4 名志愿者中,男、女生都有的情况有 \( {15} - 1 = {14} \) 种,

则其概率为 \( \frac{14}{15} \) ;

故答案为 \( \frac{14}{15} \) .

12. 若不等式 \( {x}^{2} - {kx} + k - 1 > 0 \) 对 \( x \in  \left( {1,2}\right) \) 恒成立，则实数 \( k \) 的取值范围是___.

【答案】 \( \left( {-\infty ,2}\right) \)

不等式 \( {x}^{2} - {kx} + k - 1 > 0 \) 可化为 \( \left( {1 - x}\right) k > 1 - {x}^{2} \)

\( \because x \in  \left( {1,2}\right) \)

\( \therefore k \leq  \frac{1 - {x}^{2}}{1 - x} = 1 + x \)

\( \therefore y = 1 + x \) 是一个增函数

\( \therefore k \leq  1 + 1 = 2 \)

\( \therefore \) 实数 \( k \) 取值范围是 \( ( - \infty ,2\rbrack \)

\( ( - \infty ,2\rbrack \)

13. 已知等差数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的首项及公差均为正数,令 \( {b}_{n} = \sqrt{{a}_{n}} + \sqrt{{a}_{{2012} - n}}\left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }, n < {2012}}\right) \) . 当 \( {b}_{k} \) 是数列 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 的最大项时， \( k = \) ___.

【答案】 1006

设 \( \sqrt{{a}_{n}} = x,\sqrt{{a}_{{2012} - n}} = y \) ,

\( \because {b}_{n} = \sqrt{{a}_{n}} + \sqrt{{a}_{{2012} - n}}\left( {n \in  {N}^{ * },\;n < {2012}}\right) \) ,

\( \therefore \) 根据基本不等式 \( {\left( x + y\right) }^{2} = {x}^{2} + {y}^{2} + {2xy} \leq  {x}^{2} + {y}^{2} + {x}^{2} + {y}^{2} = 2\left( {{x}^{2} + {y}^{2}}\right) \) ,

得 \( {b}_{n}^{2} = {\left( \sqrt{{a}_{n}} + \sqrt{{a}_{{2012} - n}}\right) }^{2} \leq  2\left( {{a}_{n} + {a}_{{2012} - n}}\right)  = 2\left( {2{a}_{1006}}\right)  = 4{a}_{1006} \) ,

当且仅当 \( {a}_{n} = {a}_{{2012} - n} \) 时， \( {b}_{n} \) 取到最大值，

此时 \( n = {1006} \) ,所以 \( k = {1006} \) .

1006.

14. 若矩阵 \( \left\lbrack  \begin{array}{l} {a}_{11} \\  {a}_{21} \end{array}\right\rbrack \) 满足 \( {a}_{11},{a}_{12},{a}_{21},{a}_{22} \in  \{  - 1,1\} \) ,且 \( \left| \begin{array}{l} {a}_{11} \\  {a}_{21} \end{array}\right|  = 0 \) ,则这样的互不相等的矩阵共有___个.

【答案】 8

\( \because \left| \begin{array}{l} {a}_{11} \\  {a}_{21} \end{array}\right|  = {a}_{11}{a}_{22} - {a}_{12}{a}_{21} = 0,\;{a}_{11},\;{a}_{12},\;{a}_{21},\;{a}_{22} \in  \{  - 1,\;1\} , \)

\( \therefore \) 矩阵 \( \left\lbrack  \begin{array}{l} {a}_{11} \\  {a}_{21} \end{array}\right\rbrack \) 可以是 \( \left\lbrack  \begin{array}{l} 1 \\  1 \end{array}\right\rbrack  \text{ 、 }\left\lbrack  \begin{array}{l} 1 \\   - 1 \end{array}\right\rbrack  \text{ 、 }\left\lbrack  \begin{array}{l}  - 1 \\  1 \end{array}\right\rbrack  \text{ 、 }\left\lbrack  \begin{array}{l}  - 1 \\   - 1 \end{array}\right\rbrack  \text{ 、 }\left\lbrack  \begin{array}{l}  - 1 \\  1 \end{array}\right\rbrack  \text{ 、 }\left\lbrack  \begin{array}{l}  - 1 \\   - 1 \end{array}\right\rbrack  \text{ 、 }\left\lbrack  \begin{array}{l} 1 \\  1 \end{array}\right\rbrack  \text{ 、 }\left\lbrack  \begin{array}{l} 1 \\   - 1 \end{array}\right\rbrack \)

二、选择题 (本大题满分 20 分) 本大题共有 4 题, 每题都给出四个结论, 其中有且只有一个结论是正确的,选对得 5 分,否则一律得零分。

15. 已知椭圆 \( {C}_{1} : \frac{{x}^{2}}{12} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{4} = 1,{C}_{2} : \frac{{x}^{2}}{16} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{8} = 1 \) ,则 ( )

A. \( {C}_{1} \) 与 \( {C}_{2} \) 顶点相同 B. \( {C}_{1} \) 与 \( {C}_{2} \) 长轴长相同

C. \( {C}_{1} \) 与 \( {C}_{2} \) 短轴长相同 D. \( {C}_{1} \) 与 \( {C}_{2} \) 焦距相等

## 【答案】 \( D \)

因为椭圆 \( {C}_{1} : \frac{{x}^{2}}{12} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{4} = 1 \) ,所以 \( a = 2\sqrt{3}, b = 2, c = 2\sqrt{2} \) .

椭圆 \( {C}_{2} : \frac{{x}^{2}}{16} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{8} = 1 \) ,所以 \( a = 4, b = 2\sqrt{2}, c = 2\sqrt{2} \) ;

所以两个椭圆有相同的焦距.

D.

16. 记函数 \( y = f\left( x\right) \) 的反函数为 \( y = {f}^{-1}\left( x\right) \) . 如果函数 \( y = f\left( x\right) \) 的图象过点 \( \left( {1,0}\right) \) ,那么函数 \( y \; = {f}^{-1}\left( x\right)  + 1 \) 的图象过点 ( )

A. \( \left( {0,0}\right) \) B. \( \left( {0,2}\right) \) C. \( \left( {1,1}\right) \) D. \( \left( {2,0}\right) \)

## 【答案】 \( B \)

\( \because y = f\left( x\right) \) 的图象过点 \( \left( {1,0}\right) \) ,

\( \therefore \) 其反函数 \( y = {f}^{-1}\left( x\right) \) 必过点 \( \left( {0,1}\right) \) ,即 \( {f}^{-1}\left( 0\right)  = 1 \) ,

\( \therefore y = {f}^{-1}\left( x\right)  + 1 \) 的图象过点 \( \left( {0,2}\right) \) .

\( B \)

17. 已知空间三条直线 \( l\text{ 、 }m\text{ 、 }n \) . 若 \( l \) 与 \( m \) 异面,且 \( l \) 与 \( n \) 异面,则 ( )

A. \( m \) 与 \( n \) 异面 B. \( m \) 与 \( n \) 相交

C. \( m \) 与 \( n \) 平行 D. \( m \) 与 \(![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_122_464_1130_720_518_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_122_464_1130_720_518_0.jpg)9b5b00_122_464_1130_720_518_0.jpg)

图3

\( \because \) 空间三条直线 \( l\text{ 、 }m\text{ 、 }n \) . 若 \( l \) 与 \( m \) 异面,且 \( l \) 与 \( n \) 异面,

\( \because m \) 与 \( n \) 可能异面 (如图 3),也可能平行 (图 1),也可能相交 (图 2).

故选 \( D \)

18. 设 \( O \) 为 \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 所在平面内一点. 若实数 \( x\text{ 、 }y\text{ 、 }z \) 满足 \( x\overrightarrow{OA} + y\overrightarrow{OB} + z\overrightarrow{OC} = \overrightarrow{0} \) , \( \left( {{x}^{2} + {y}^{2} + {z}^{2} \neq  0}\right) \) ,则 “ \( {xyz} = 0 \) ” 是 “点 \( O \) 在 \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 的边所在直线上” 的 ( )

A. 充分而不必要条件 B. 必要而不充分条件

C. 充要条件 D. 既不充分也不必要条件

## 【答案】 \( C \)

\( \because O \) 为 \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 所在平面内一点. 实数 \( x\text{ 、 }y\text{ 、 }z \) 满足 \( x\overrightarrow{OA} + y\overrightarrow{OB} + z\overrightarrow{OC} = \)

\( \overrightarrow{0}\left( {{x}^{2} + {y}^{2} + {z}^{2} \neq  0}\right) , \)

\( \therefore x\overrightarrow{OA} + y\overrightarrow{OB} =  - z\overrightarrow{OC} \) ,

若 \( {xyz} = 0 \) ” 则 \( x\text{ 、 }y\text{ 、 }z \) 中只能有一个为 0,(否则若 \( x = y = 0 \) ,可推出 \( z = 0 \) ,这与 \( {x}^{2} + {y}^{2} + {z}^{2} \neq  0 \) 矛盾)

假设 \( x = 0\left( {y\text{ 、 }z\text{ 不为 0 }}\right) \) ,可得 \( y\overrightarrow{OB} =  - z\overrightarrow{OC},\therefore \overrightarrow{OB} =  - \frac{z}{y}\overrightarrow{OC} \) ,

\( \therefore \) 向量 \( \overrightarrow{OB} \) 和 \( \overrightarrow{OC} \) 共线, \( \therefore O \) 只能在 \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 边 \( {BC} \) 上;

若点 \( O \) 在 \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 的边所在直线上,假设在边 \( {AB} \) 上,说明向量 \( \overrightarrow{OB} \) 和 \( \overrightarrow{OA} \) 共线, \( \therefore z = 0,\therefore {xyz} = 0 \) ,

\( \therefore \) “ \( {xyz} = 0 \) ” 是 “点 \( O \) 在 \( \bigtriangleup  {ABC} \) 的边所在直线上” 的充要条件；

\( C \) .

三、解答题 (本大题满分 74 分) 本大题共有 5 题, 解答下列各题必须写出必要的步骤。

19. 如图,正四棱柱 \( {ABCD} - {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 的底面边长为 1,高为 \![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_123_282_1474_329_482_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_123_282_1474_329_482_0.jpg)9b5b00_123_282_1474_329_482_0.jpg)

(1)三棱锥 \( {C}_{1} - {MBC} \) 的体积；

【答案】 \( \frac{1}{6} \) 连接 \( {CM} \) ,

\( \because \) 正方形 \( {ABCD} \) 中, \( M \) 为 \( {AB} \) 中点,且边长为 1,

\( \therefore \bigtriangleup {BCM} \) 的面积为 \( S = \frac{1}{4}{S}_{ABCD} = \frac{1}{4} \) .

又 \( \because C{C}_{1} \bot \) 平面 \( {ABCD} \) ,

\( \therefore C{C}_{1} \) 是三棱锥 \( {C}_{1} - {MBC} \) 的高,

\( \therefore \) 三棱锥 \( {C}_{1} - {MBC} \) 的体积为: \( {V}_{{C1} - {MBC}} = \frac{1}{3} \times  \frac{1}{4} \times  2 = \frac{1}{6} \) ；

(2)异面直线 \( {CD} \) 与 \( M{C}_{1} \) 所成角的大小 (结果用反三角函数值表示).

【答案】 \( \arctan 2\sqrt{5} \)

连接 \( B{C}_{1} \)

\( \because {CD}//{AB} \) ，

\( \therefore \angle {C}_{1}{MB} \) (或其补角) 为异面直线 \( {CD} \) 与 \( M{C}_{1} \) 所成的角.

\( \because {AB} \bot \) 平面 \( {B}_{1}{C}_{1}{CB}, B{C}_{1} \subset \) 平面 \( {B}_{1}{C}_{1}{CB} \) ,

\( \therefore {AB} \bot  B{C}_{1} \) .

\( {Rt}\bigtriangleup M{C}_{1}B \) 中, \( B{C}_{1} = \sqrt{B{C}^{2} + C{C}_{1}^{2}} = \sqrt{5},{MB} = \frac{1}{2}{AB} = \frac{1}{2} \)

\( \therefore \tan \angle {C}_{1}{MB} = \frac{B{C}_{1}}{BM} = 2\sqrt{5} \)

所以异面直线 \( {CD} \) 与 \( M{C}_{1} \![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_124_422_1154_334_485_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_124_422_1154_334_485_0.jpg)9b5b00_124_422_1154_334_485_0.jpg)

20. 某环线地铁按内、外环线同时运行, 内、外环线的长均为 30 千米 (忽略内、外环线长度差异).

(1)当 9 列列车同时在内环线上运行时，要使内环线乘客最长候车时间为 10 分钟，求内环线列车的最小平均速度;

【答案】 20 千米/小时

设内环线列车的平均速度为 \( v \) 千米/小时,则要使内环线乘客最长候车时间为 10 分钟,可得 \( \frac{30}{9v} \times  {60} \leq  {10} \)

\( \therefore v \geq  {20} \)

\( \therefore \) 要使内环线乘客最长候车时间为 10 分钟,内环线列车的最小平均速度是 20 千米/ 小时;

(2)新调整的方案要求内环线列车平均速度为 25 千米/小时，外环线列车平均速度为 30 千米/ 小时. 现内、外环线共有 18 列列车全部投入运行, 要使内外环线乘客的最长候车时间之差不超过 1 分钟, 向内、外环线应各投入几列列车运行?

【答案】内环线投入 10 列列车运行, 外环线投入 8 列列车

设内环线投入 \( x \) 列列车运行,则外环线投入 \( \left( {{18} - x}\right) \) 列列车运行,内、外环线乘客最长候车时间分别为 \( {t}_{1},{t}_{2} \) 分钟,

则 \( {t}_{1} = \frac{30}{25x} \times  {60} = \frac{72}{x},{t}_{2} = \frac{30}{{30}\left( {{18} - x}\right) } \times  {60} = \frac{60}{{18} - x} \)

\( \therefore \left| {{t}_{1} - {t}_{2}}\right|  = \left| {\frac{72}{x} - \frac{60}{{18} - x}}\right|  \leq  1 \)

\( \therefore \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {x}^{2} - {150x} + {1296} \leq  0 \\  {x}^{2} + {114x} - {1296} \leq  0 \end{array}\right. \)

\( \therefore \frac{{150} - \sqrt{17316}}{2} \leq  x \leq  \frac{-{114} + \sqrt{18180}}{2} \)

\( \because x \in  {N}_{ + },\;\therefore x = {10} \)

\( \therefore \) 当内环线投入 10 列列车运行,外环线投入 8 列列车时,内外环线乘客的最长候车时间之差不超过 1 分钟.

21. 已知双曲线 \( {C}_{1} : \;{x}^{2} - \frac{{y}^{2}}{4} = 1 \) .

(1)求与双曲线 \( {C}_{1} \) 有相同焦点,且过点 \( P\left( {4,\sqrt{3}}\right) \) 的双曲线 \( {C}_{2} \) 的标准方程；

【答案】 \( \frac{{x}^{2}}{4} - {y}^{2} = 1 \)

\( \because \) 双曲线 \( {C}_{1} : \;{x}^{2} - \frac{{y}^{2}}{4} = 1 \) ,

\( \therefore \) 焦点坐标为 \( \left( {\sqrt{5},0}\right) ,\left( {-\sqrt{5},0}\right) \)

设双曲线 \( {C}_{2} \) 的标准方程为 \( \frac{{x}^{2}}{{a}^{2}} - \frac{{y}^{2}}{{b}^{2}} = 1\left( {{a0}, b > 0}\right) \) ,

\( \because \) 双曲线 \( {C}_{2} \) 与双曲线 \( {C}_{1} \) 有相同焦点,且过点 \( P\left( {4,\sqrt{3}}\right) \)

\( \therefore \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {a}^{2} + {b}^{2} = 5 \\  \frac{16}{{a}^{2}} - \frac{3}{{b}^{2}} = 1 \end{array}\right. \) ,解得 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} a = 2 \\  b = 1 \end{array}\right. \)

\( \therefore \) 双曲线 \( {C}_{2} \) 的标准方程为 \( \frac{{x}^{2}}{4} - {y}^{2} = 1 \)

(2)直线 \( l : y = x + m \) 分别交双曲线 \( {C}_{1} \) 的两条渐近线于 \( A \) 、 \( B \) 两点. 当 \( \overrightarrow{OA}\overrightarrow{OB} = 3 \) 时，求实数 \( m \) 的值.

【答案】 \( \pm  \sqrt{3} \)

双曲线 \( {C}_{1} \) 的两条渐近线为 \( y = {2x}, y =  - {2x} \) 由 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} y = {2x} \\  y = x + m \end{array}\right. \) ,可得 \( x = m, y = {2m},\therefore A\left( {m,{2m}}\right) \) 由 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} y =  - {2x} \\  y = x + m \end{array}\right. \) ,可得 \( x =  - \frac{1}{3}m, y = \frac{2}{3}m,\therefore B\left( {-\frac{1}{3}m,\frac{2}{3}m}\right) \)

\[
\therefore \overrightarrow{OA}\overrightarrow{OB} =  - \frac{1}{3}{m}^{2} + \frac{4}{3}{m}^{2} = {m}^{2}
\]

\[
\because \overrightarrow{OA}\overrightarrow{OB} = 3
\]

\[
\therefore {m}^{2} = 3
\]

\[
\therefore m =  \pm  \sqrt{3}
\]

22. 已知数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 、 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 、 \( \left\{  {c}_{n}\right\} \) 满足 \( \left( {{a}_{n + 1} - {a}_{n}}\right) \left( {{b}_{n + 1} - {b}_{n}}\right)  = {c}_{n}\left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) .

(1)设 \( {c}_{n} = {3n} + 6 \) ， \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 是公差为3的等差数列. 当 \( {b}_{1} = 1 \) 时，求 \( {b}_{2} \) 、 \( {b}_{3} \) 的值；

【答案】 \( {b}_{2} = 4;\;{b}_{3} = 8 \)

\[
\because {a}_{n + 1} - {a}_{n} = 3\text{ , }
\]

\[
\therefore {b}_{n + 1} - {b}_{n} = n + 2\text{ , }
\]

\[
\because {b}_{1} = 1\text{ , }
\]

\[
\therefore {b}_{2} = 4,\;{b}_{3} = 8\text{ . }
\]

( 2 )设 \( {c}_{n} = {n}^{3}\text{ ， }{a}_{n} = {n}^{2} - {8n} \) . 求正整数 \( k \) ，使得对一切 \( n \in  {N}^{ * } \) ，均有 \( {b}_{n} \geq  {b}_{k} \) ；

【答案】 \( k = 4 \)

\[
\because {a}_{n} = {n}^{2} - {8n}\text{ . }
\]

\[
\therefore {a}_{n + 1} - {a}_{n} = {2n} - 7\text{ , }
\]

\[
\therefore {b}_{n + 1} - {b}_{n} = \frac{{n}^{3}}{{2n} - 7}\text{ , }
\]

由 \( {b}_{n + 1} - {b}_{n} > 0 \) ,解得 \( n \geq  4 \) ,即 \( {b}_{4} < {b}_{5} < {b}_{6}\cdots \) ;

由 \( {b}_{n + 1} - {b}_{n} < 0 \) ,解得 \( n \leq  3 \) ,即 \( {b}_{1} > {b}_{2} > {b}_{3} > {b}_{4} \) .

\( \therefore k = 4 \) .

(3) 设 \( {c}_{n} = {2}^{n} + n,{a}_{n} = \frac{1 + {\left( -1\right) }^{n}}{2} \) . 当 \( {b}_{1} = 1 \) 时,求数列 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 的通项公式.

\( \therefore {b}_{n} = \left\{  {\begin{array}{l}  - \frac{{2}^{n}}{3} - \frac{n}{2} + \frac{13}{6}, \\  \frac{{2}^{n}}{3} + \frac{n}{2} + \frac{5}{3}, \end{array}k \in  {N}_{ + }}\right. \)

\[
\because {a}_{n + 1} - {a}_{n} = {\left( -1\right) }^{n + 1}\text{ , }
\]

\[
\therefore {b}_{n + 1} - {b}_{n} = {\left( -1\right) }^{n + 1}\left( {{2}^{n} + n}\right) \text{ . }
\]

\[
\therefore {b}_{n} - {b}_{n - 1} = {\left( -1\right) }^{n}\left( {{2}^{n - 1} + n - 1}\right) \left( {n \geq  2}\right) \text{ . }
\]

\[
\text{ 故 }{b}_{2} - {b}_{1} = {2}^{1} + 1\text{ ; }
\]

\[
{b}_{3} - {b}_{2} = \left( {-1}\right) \left( {{2}^{2} + 2}\right) ,
\]

...

\[
{b}_{n - 1} - {b}_{n - 2} = {\left( -1\right) }^{n - 1}\left( {{2}^{n - 2} + n - 2}\right) .
\]

\[
{b}_{n} - {b}_{n - 1} = {\left( -1\right) }^{n}\left( {{2}^{n - 1} + n - 1}\right) .
\]

当 \( n = {2k} \) 时,以上各式相加得

\[
{b}_{n} - {b}_{1} = \left( {2 - {2}^{2} + \cdots  - {2}^{n - 2} + {2}^{n - 1}}\right)  + \left\lbrack  {1 - 2 + \cdots  - \left( {n - 2}\right)  + \left( {n - 1}\right) }\right\rbrack   = \frac{2 - {2}^{n - 1}\left( {-2}\right) }{1 - \left( {-2}\right) } +
\]

\[
\frac{n}{2} = \frac{2 + {2}^{n}}{3} + \frac{n}{2}
\]

\[
\therefore {b}_{n} = \frac{2 + {2}^{n}}{3} + \frac{n}{2} + 1 = \frac{{2}^{n}}{3} + \frac{n}{2} + \frac{5}{3}\text{ . }
\]

\[
\text{ 当 }n = {2k} - 1\text{ 时, }
\]

\[
{b}_{n} = {b}_{n + 1} - {\left( -1\right) }^{n + 1}\left( {{2}^{n} + n}\right)  = \frac{{2}^{n + 1}}{3} + \frac{n + 1}{2} + \frac{5}{3} - \left( {{2}^{n} + n}\right)  =  - \frac{{2}^{n}}{3} - \frac{n}{2} + \frac{13}{6}
\]

\[
\therefore {b}_{n} = \left\{  {\begin{array}{l}  - \frac{{2}^{n}}{3} - \frac{n}{2} + \frac{13}{6}, \\  \frac{{2}^{n}}{3} + \frac{n}{2} + \frac{5}{3}, \end{array}k \in  {N}_{ + }}\right.
\]

23. 定义向量 \( \overrightarrow{OM} = \left( {a, b}\right) \) 的 “相伴函数” 为 \( f\left( x\right)  = a\sin x + b\cos x \) ,函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = a\sin x + \; b\cos x \) 的 “相伴向量” 为 \( \overrightarrow{OM} = \left( {a, b}\right) \) (其中 \( O \) 为坐标原点). 记平面内所有向量的 “相伴函数” 构成的集合为 \( S \) .

(1)设 \( g\left( x\right)  = 3\sin \left( {x + \frac{\pi }{2}}\right)  + 4\sin x \) ，求证: \( g\left( x\right)  \in  S \) ；

【答案】见解析

\[
g\left( x\right)  = 3\sin \left( {x + \frac{\pi }{2}}\right)  + 4\sin x = 4\sin x + 3\cos x,
\]

其 ‘相伴向量’ \( \overrightarrow{OM} = \left( {4,3}\right) , g\left( x\right)  \in  S \) .

( 2 )已知 \( h\left( x\right)  = \cos \left( {x + \alpha }\right)  + 2\cos x \) ，且 \( h\left( x\right)  \in  S \) ，求其 “相伴向量” 的模；

【答案】 \( \sqrt{5 + 4\cos \alpha } \)

\( h\left( x\right)  = \cos \left( {x + \alpha }\right)  + 2\cos x \)

\( = \left( {\cos x\cos \alpha  - \sin x\sin \alpha }\right)  + 2\cos x \)

\( =  - \sin a\sin x + \left( {\cos a + 2}\right) \cos x \)

\( \therefore \) 函数 \( h\left( x\right) \) 的 ‘相伴向量’ \( \overrightarrow{OM} = \left( {-\sin \alpha ,\cos \alpha  + 2}\right) \) .

则 \( \left| \overrightarrow{OM}\right|  = \sqrt{{\left( -\sin \alpha \right) }^{2} + {\left( \cos \alpha  + 2\right) }^{2}} = \sqrt{5 + 4\cos \alpha } \) .

(3)已知 \( M\left( {a, b}\right) \left( {b \neq  0}\right) \) 为圆 \( C : \;{\left( x - 2\right) }^{2} + {y}^{2} = 1 \) 上一点，向量 \( \overrightarrow{OM} \) 的 “相伴函数”

\( f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( x = {x}_{0} \) 处取得最大值. 当点 \( M \) 在圆 \( C \) 上运动时,求 \( \tan 2{x}_{0} \) 的取值范围.

\( \left\lbrack  {-\sqrt{3},\;0)\cup (0,\;\sqrt{3}}\right\rbrack \)

\( \overrightarrow{OM} \) 的 ‘相伴函数’ \( f\left( x\right)  = a\sin x + b\cos x = \sqrt{{a}^{2} + {b}^{2}}\sin \left( {x + \varphi }\right) \) ,

\[
\text{ 其中 }\cos \varphi  = \frac{a}{\sqrt{{a}^{2} + {b}^{2}}},\sin \varphi  = \frac{b}{\sqrt{{a}^{2} + {b}^{2}}}\text{ . }
\]

当 \( x + \varphi  = {2k\pi } + \frac{\pi }{2}, k \in  Z \) 时, \( f\left( x\right) \) 取到最大值,故 \( {x}_{0} = {2k\pi } + \frac{\pi }{2} - \varphi , k \in  Z \) .

\[
\therefore \tan {x}_{0} = \tan \left( {{2k\pi } + \frac{\pi }{2} - \varphi }\right)  = \cot \varphi  = \frac{a}{b}\text{ , }
\]

24. \( \operatorname{an}2{x}_{0} = \frac{2\tan {x}_{0}}{1 - {\tan }^{2}{x}_{0}} = \frac{2 \times  \frac{a}{b}}{1 - {\left( \frac{a}{b}\right) }^{2}} = \frac{2}{\frac{b}{a} - \frac{a}{b}} \) .

\( \frac{b}{a} \) 为直线 \( {OM} \) 的斜率,由几何意义知: \( \frac{b}{a} \in  \left\lbrack  {-\frac{\sqrt{3}}{3},0}\right)  \cup  \left( {0,\frac{\sqrt{3}}{3}}\right\rbrack \) .

令 \( m = \frac{b}{a} \) ,则 \( \tan 2{x}_{0} = \frac{2}{m - \frac{1}{m}}, m \in  \left\lbrack  {-\frac{\sqrt{3}}{3},0}\right)  \cup  \left( {0,\frac{\sqrt{3}}{3}}\right\} \) .

当 \( - \frac{\sqrt{3}}{3} \leq  m < 0 \) 时,函数 \( \tan 2{x}_{0} = \frac{2}{m - \frac{1}{m}} \) 单调递减, \( \therefore 0 < \tan 2{x}_{0} \leq  \sqrt{3} \) ;

当 \( 0 < m \leq  \frac{\sqrt{3}}{3} \) 时,函数 \( \tan 2{x}_{0} = \frac{2}{m - \frac{1}{m}} \) 单调递减, \( \therefore  - \sqrt{3} \leq  \tan 2{x}_{0} < 0 \) .

综上所述， \( \tan 2{x}_{0} \in  \left\lbrack  {-\sqrt{3},0}\right)  \cup  \left( {0,\sqrt{3}}\right\rbrack \) .

## 2013 秋考

填空

1. 计算: \( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{n + {20}}{{3n} + {13}} = \) ___.

【答案】 \( \frac{1}{3} \)

根据极限运算法则, \( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n\infty }}\frac{n + {20}}{{3n} + {13}} = \frac{1}{3} \) .

2. 设 \( m \in  R,{m}^{2} + m - 2 + \left( {{m}^{2} - 1}\right) \mathrm{i} \) 是纯虚数,其中 \( \mathrm{i} \) 是虚数单位,则 \( m = \) ___.

【答案】 -2

\( \because \) 复数 \( z = \left( {{m}^{2} + m - 2}\right)  + \left( {m - 1}\right) \mathrm{i} \) 为纯虚数,

\( \therefore {m}^{2} + m - 2 = 0,{m}^{2} - 1 \neq  0 \) ,解得 \( m =  - 2 \) ,

-2 .

3. 若 \( \left| \begin{matrix} {x}^{2} & {y}^{2} \\   - 1 & 1 \end{matrix}\right|  = \left| \begin{matrix} x & x \\  y &  - y \end{matrix}\right| \) ,则 \( x + y = \) ___.

【答案】 0

\[
{x}^{2} + {y}^{2} =  - {2xy} \Rightarrow  x + y = 0.
\]

4. 已知 \( {ABC} \) 的内角 \( A, B, C \) 所对应边分别为 \( a, b, c \) ,若 \( 3{a}^{2} + {2ab} + 3{b}^{2} - 3{c}^{2} = 0 \) ,则角 \( C \) 的大小是___ (结果用反三角函数值表示).

【答案】 \( \pi  - \arccos \frac{1}{3} \)

\( 3{a}^{2} + {2ab} + 3{b}^{2} - 3{c}^{2} = 0 \Rightarrow  {c}^{2} = {a}^{2} + {b}^{2} + \frac{2}{3}{ab} \) ,

故 \( \cos C =  - \frac{1}{3}, C = \pi  - \arccos \frac{1}{3} \) .

5. 设常数 \( a \in  R \) . 若 \( {\left( {x}^{2} + \frac{a}{x}\right) }^{5} \) 的二项展开式中 \( {x}^{7} \) 项的系数为 -10 , 则 \( a = \) ___.

【答案】-2

\[
{\left( {x}^{2} + \frac{a}{x}\right) }^{5} \Rightarrow  {C}_{5}^{r}{\left( {x}^{2}\right) }^{5 - r}{\left( \frac{a}{x}\right) }^{r} =  - {10}{x}^{7} \Rightarrow  r = 1,\;{C}_{5}^{1}a =  - {10}
\]

\[
\Rightarrow  {5a} =  - {10},\;a =  - 2\text{ . }
\]

6. 方程 \( \frac{3}{{3}^{x} - 1} + \frac{1}{3} = {3}^{x - 1} \) 的实数解为___.

【答案】 \( {\log }_{3}4 \)

原方程整理后变为 \( {3}^{2x} - 2 \cdot  {3}^{x} - 8 = 0 \Rightarrow  {3}^{x} = 4 \Rightarrow  x = {\log }_{3}4 \) .

7. 在极坐标系中，曲线 \( \rho  = \cos \theta  + 1 \) 与 \( \rho \cos \theta  = 1 \) 的公共点到极点的距离为___.

【答案】 \( \frac{1 + \sqrt{5}}{2} \)

联立方程组得 \( \rho \left( {\rho  - 1}\right)  = 1 \Rightarrow  \rho  = \frac{1 \pm  \sqrt{5}}{2} \) ，

又 \( \rho  \geq  0 \) ,故所求为 \( \frac{1 + \sqrt{5}}{2} \) .

8. 盒子中装有编号为1,2,3,4,5,6,7,8,9的九个球,从中任意取出两个,则这两个球的编号之积为偶数的概率是___ (结果用最简分数表示).

【答案】 \( \frac{13}{18} \)

【分析】: 从随机任意取出两个,基本事件总数 \( n = {C}_{9}^{2} = {36} \) ,这两个球的编号之积为偶数包含的基本事件个数 \( m = {C}_{4}^{2} + {C}_{4}^{1}{C}_{5}^{1} = {26} \) ,由此能求出这两个球的编号之积为偶数的概率.

9 个数 5 个奇数, 4 个偶数,

根据题意所求概率为 \( 1 - \frac{{C}_{5}^{2}}{{C}_{9}^{2}} = \frac{13}{18} \) .

\( \frac{13}{18} \) .

9. 设 \( {AB} \) 是椭圆 \( \Gamma \) 的长轴,点 \( C \) 在 \( \Gamma \) 上,且 \( \angle {CBA} = \frac{\pi }{4} \) . 若 \( {AB} = 4,{BC} = \sqrt{2} \) ,则 \( \Gamma \) 的两个焦点之间的距离为___.

【答案】 \( \frac{4}{3}\sqrt{6} \)

如图,设椭圆的标准方程为 \( \frac{{x}^{2}}{{a}^{2}} + ![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_132_428_217_648_527_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_132_428_217_648_527_0.jpg)39b5b00_132_428_217_648_527_0.jpg)

由题意知, \( {2a} = 4, a = 2 \) .

\( \because \angle {CBA} = \frac{\pi }{4},{BC} = \sqrt{2},\therefore \) 点 \( C \) 的坐标为 \( C\left( {-1,1}\right) \) ,

因点 \( C \) 在椭圆上， \( \therefore \frac{{\left( -1\right) }^{2}}{4} + \frac{{1}^{2}}{{b}^{2}} = 1 \) ，

\( \therefore {b}^{2} = \frac{4}{3} \) ,

\( \therefore {c}^{2} = {a}^{2} - {b}^{2} = 4 - \frac{4}{3} = \frac{8}{3},\;c = \frac{2\sqrt{6}}{3} \) ,

则 \( \Gamma \) 的两个焦点之间的距离为 \( \frac{4\sqrt{6}}{3} \) .

\( \frac{4\sqrt{6}}{3} \)

10. 设非零常数 \( d \) 是等差数列 \( {x}_{1},{x}_{2},{x}_{3},\cdots ,{x}_{19} \) 的公差,随机变量 \( \xi \) 等可能地取值 \( {x}_{1},{x}_{2} \) , \( {x}_{3},\cdots ,{x}_{19} \) ，则方差 \( {D\xi } = \) ___.

【答案】 \( \sqrt{30}\left| d\right| \)

\( {E\xi } = {x}_{10},\;{D\xi } = \sqrt{\frac{{d}^{2}}{19}\left( {{9}^{2} + {8}^{2} + \cdots  + {1}^{2} + {0}^{2} + {1}^{2} + \cdots  + {9}^{2}}\right) } = \sqrt{30}\left| d\right| . \)

11. 若 \( \cos x\cos y + \sin x\sin y = \frac{1}{2},\sin {2x} + \sin {2y} = \frac{2}{3} \) ，则 \( \sin \left( {x + y}\right)  = \) ___.

【答案】 \( \frac{2}{3} \)

\( \cos \left( {x - y}\right)  = \frac{1}{2},\;\sin {2x} + \sin {2y} = 2\sin \left( {x + y}\right) \cos \left( {x - y}\right)  = \frac{2}{3}, \)

故 \( \sin \left( {x + y}\right)  = \frac{2}{3} \) .

12. 设 \( a \) 为实常数, \( y = f\left( x\right) \) 是定义在 \( R \) 上的奇函数,当 \( x < 0 \) 时, \( f\left( x\right)  = {9x} + \frac{{a}^{2}}{x} + 7 \) ,若 \( f\left( x\right)  \geq  a + 1 \) 对一切 \( x \geq  0 \) 成立,则 \( a \) 的取值范围为___.

【答案】 \( a \leq   - \frac{8}{7} \)

\( f\left( 0\right)  = 0 \) ,故 \( 0 \geq  a + 1 \Rightarrow  a \leq   - 1 \) ;

当 \( x > 0 \) 时, \( f\left( x\right)  = {9x} + \frac{{a}^{2}}{x} - 7 \geq  a + 1 \) ,

即 \( 6\left| a\right|  \geq  a + 8 \) ,又 \( a \leq   - 1 \) ,故 \( a \leq   - \frac{8}{7} \) .

13. 在 \( {xOy} \) 平面上,将两个半圆弧 \( {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2} + {y}^{2} = 1\left( {x \geq  1}\right) \) 和 \( {\left( x - 3\right) }^{2} + {y}^{2} = 1\left( {x \geq  3}\right) \) 、两条直线 \( y = 1 \) 和 \( y =  - 1 \) 围成的封闭图形记为 \( D \) ,如图中阴影部分. 记 \( D \) 绕 \( y \) 轴旋转一周而成的几何体为 \( \Omega \) ,过 \( \left( {0, y}\right) \left( {\left| y\right|  \leq  1}\right) \) 作 \( \Omega \) 的水平截面,所得截面面积为 \( {4\pi }\sqrt{1 - {y}^{2}} + {8\pi } \) ,试利用祖暅原理、一个平放的圆柱和![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_133_304_1684_489_286_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_133_304_1684_489_286_0.jpg)9b5b00_133_304_1684_489_286_0.jpg)

【答案】 \( 2{\pi }^{2} + {16\pi } \)

根据提示,一个半径为 1,高为 \( {2\pi } \) 的圆柱平放,

一个高为 2,底面面积 \( {8\pi } \) 的长方体,这两个几何体与 \( \Omega \) 放在一起,

根据祖暅原理，每个平行水平面的截面面积都相等，

故它们的体积相等,即 \( \Omega \) 的体积值为

\( \pi  \cdot  {1}^{2} \cdot  {2\pi } + 2 \cdot  {8\pi } = 2{\pi }^{2} + {16\pi } \) .

14. 对区间 \( I \) 上有定义的函数 \( g\left( x\right) \) ,记 \( g\left( I\right)  = \{ y \mid  y = g\left( x\right) , x \in  I\} \) ,已知定义域为 \( \left\lbrack  {0,3}\right\rbrack \) 的函数 \( y \; = f\left( x\right) \) 有反函数 \( y = {f}^{-1}\left( x\right) \) ,且 \( {f}^{-1}\left( {\lbrack 0,1}\right) ) = \lbrack 1,2),{f}^{-1}\left( \left( {2,4}\right\rbrack  \right)  = \lbrack 0,1) \) ,若方程 \( f\left( x\right)  - x \; = 0 \) 有解 \( {x}_{0} \) ,则 \( {x}_{0} = \) ___.

## 【答案】 2

根据反函数定义,当 \( x \in  \lbrack 0,1) \) 时, \( f\left( x\right)  \in  (2,4\rbrack \) ;

\( x \in  \lbrack 1,2) \) 时, \( f\left( x\right)  \in  \lbrack 0,1) \) ,而 \( y = f\left( x\right) \) 的定义域为 \( \left\lbrack  {0,3}\right\rbrack \) ,

故当 \( x \in  \left\lbrack  {2,3}\right\rbrack \) 时, \( f\left( x\right) \) 的取值应在集合 \( \left( {-\infty ,0}\right)  \cup  \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack   \cup  \left( {4, + \infty }\right) \) ,

故若 \( f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = {x}_{0} \) ,只有 \( {x}_{0} = 2 \) .

选择

15. 设常数 \( a \in  R \) ,集合 \( A = \{ x \mid  \left( {x - 1}\right) \left( {x - a}\right)  \geq  0\} , B = \{ x \mid  x \geq  a - 1\} \) . 若 \( A \cup  B = R \) ,则 \( a \) 的取值范围为( ).

A. \( \left( {-\infty ,2}\right) \) B. \( \left( {-\infty ,2}\right) \) C. \( \left( {2, + \infty }\right) \) D. \( \lbrack 2, + \infty ) \)

## 【答案】 \( B \)

\( \because B = \lbrack a - 1, + \infty ), A \cup  B = R,\therefore A \supseteq  \left( {-\infty , a - 1}\right) \)

由 \( \left( {x - 1}\right) \left( {x - a}\right)  \geq  0 \Rightarrow \) 当 \( a = 1 \) 时, \( x \in  R \) ,当 \( a = 1 \) 符合题意

当 \( a > 1 \) 时, \( x \in  ( - \infty ,1\rbrack  \cup  \lbrack a, + \infty ) \Rightarrow  1 \geq  a - 1 \) 解得: 1 当 \( a < 1 \) 时, \( x \smallsetminus  {in}( \)

\( -  \smallsetminus  \inf {ty} \) , \( a\rbrack  \smallsetminus  \operatorname{cup}\left\lbrack  {1, +  \smallsetminus  \inf {ty}}\right. ) \smallsetminus \) Rightarrow a \( \smallsetminus \) geqslant \( a - 1 \smallsetminus \) Rightarrow \( a < 1 \) .

综上, \( a \smallsetminus \) leqslant 2

16. 钱大姐常说 “便宜没好货”，她这句话的意思是:“不便宜”是 “好货” 的( )

A. 充要条件 B. 既不充分也不必要条件

C. 充分条件 D. 必要条件

## 【答案】 \( D \)

便宜 \( \Rightarrow \) 没好货,

等价于,好货 \( \Rightarrow \) 不便宜.

故选 \( D \)

17. 在数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 中, \( {a}_{n} = {2}^{n} - 1 \) ,若一个 7 行 12 的矩阵的第 \( \mathrm{i} \) 行第 \( j \) 列的元素 \( {a}_{i, j} = {a}_{i} \cdot  {a}_{j} + {a}_{i} + \; {a}_{j},\;\left( {\mathrm{i} = 1,\;2,\;\cdots ,\;{71};\;j = 1,\;2,\;\cdots ,\;{12}}\right) \) 则该矩阵元素能取到的不同数值的个数为 ( )

A. 18 B. 28 C. 48 D. 63

【答案】 \( A \)

\( {a}_{i, j} = {a}_{i} \cdot  {a}_{j} + {a}_{i} + {a}_{j} = {2}^{i + j} - 1, \)

而 \( \mathrm{i} + j = 2,3,\cdots ,{19} \) ,故不同数值个数为 18 个.

18. 在边长为 1 的正六边形 \( {ABCDEF} \) 中，记以 \( A \) 为起点，其余顶点为终点的向量分别为 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{1} \) ， \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{2},{\overrightarrow{a}}_{3},{\overrightarrow{a}}_{4},{\overrightarrow{a}}_{5} \) ; 以 \( D \) 为起点,其余顶点为终点的向量分别为 \( {\overrightarrow{d}}_{1},{\overrightarrow{d}}_{2},{\overrightarrow{d}}_{3},{\overrightarrow{d}}_{4},{\overrightarrow{d}}_{5} \) . 若 \( m, M \) 分别为 \( \left( {{\overrightarrow{a}}_{i} + {\overrightarrow{a}}_{j} + {\overrightarrow{a}}_{k}}\right)  \cdot  \left( {{\overrightarrow{d}}_{r} + {\overrightarrow{d}}_{s} + {\overrightarrow{d}}_{t}}\right) \) 的最小值、最大值,其中 \( \{ \mathrm{i}, j, k\}  \subseteq  \{ 1,2,3,4,5\} \) , \( \{ r, s, t\}  \subseteq  \{ 1,2,3,4,5\} \) ,则 \( m, M \) 满足 ().

A. \( m = 0, M > 0 \) B. \( m < 0, M > 0 \) C. \( m < 0, M = 0 \) D. \( m < 0, M < 0 \)

## 【答案】 \( D \)

由题意,以 \( A \) 为起点,

其余顶点为终点的向量分别为 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{1},{\overrightarrow{a}}_{2},{\overrightarrow{a}}_{3},{\overrightarrow{a}}_{4},{\overrightarrow{a}}_{5} \) ;

以 \( D \) 为起点,其余顶点为终点的向量分别为 \( {\overrightarrow{d}}_{1},{\overrightarrow{d}}_{2},{\overrightarrow{d}}_{3},{\overrightarrow{d}}_{4},{\overrightarrow{d}}_{5} \) .

\( \therefore \) 利用向量的数量积公式,可知只有 \( \overrightarrow{AF} \cdot  \overrightarrow{DE} = \overrightarrow{AB} \cdot  \overrightarrow{DC} > 0 \) ,其余数量积均小于等于 0 ,

\( \because m, M \) 分别为 \( \left( {{\overrightarrow{a}}_{i} + {\overrightarrow{a}}_{j} + {\overrightarrow{a}}_{k}}\right)  \cdot  \left( {{\overrightarrow{d}}_{r} + {\overrightarrow{d}}_{s} + {\overrightarrow{d}}_{t}}\right) \) 的最小值、最大值,

\( \therefore m < 0, M < 0 \) .

故选 \( D \)

【解析】答

19. 如图,在长方体 \( {ABCD} - {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 中, \( {AB![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_136_328_763_392_254_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_136_328_763_392_254_0.jpg)39b5b00_136_328_763_392_254_0.jpg)

直线 \( B{C}_{1} \) 平行于平面 \( D{A}_{1}C \) ,并求直线 \( B{C}_{1} \) 到平面 \( D{A}_{1}C \) 的距离.

【答案】证明见解析,距离为 \( \frac{2}{3} \) .

证明: 因为 \( {ABCD} - {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 为长方体,

故 \( {AB}//{C}_{1}{D}_{1},{AB} = {C}_{1}{D}_{1} \) ,

故 \( {AB}{C}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 为平行四边形,故 \( B{C}_{1}//A{D}_{1} \) ,

显然 \( B \) 不在平面 \( {D}_{1}{AC} \) 上,

于是直线 \( B{C}_{1} \) 平行于平面 \( {D}_{1}{AC} \) ;

直线 \( B{C}_{1} \) 到平面 \( {D}_{1}{AC} \) 的距离即为点 \( B \) 到平面 \( {D}_{1}{AC} \) 的距离设为 \( h \)

考虑三棱锥 \( {ABC}{D}_{1} \) 的体积,以 \( {ABC} \) 为底面,

可得 \( V = \frac{1}{3} \times  \left( {\frac{1}{2} \times  1 \times  2}\right)  \times  1 = \frac{1}{3} \)

而 \( A{D}_{1}C \) 中, \( {AC} = {D}_{1}C = \sqrt{5}, A{D}_{1} = \sqrt{2} \) ,

故 \( {S}_{A{D}_{1}C} = \frac{3}{2} \)

所以, \( V = \frac{1}{3} \times  \frac{3}{2} \times  h = \frac{1}{3} \Rightarrow  h = \frac{2}{3} \) ,

即直线 \( B{C}_{1} \) 到平面 \( {D}_{1}{AC} \) 的距离为 \( \frac{2}{3} \) .

20. 甲厂以 \( x \) 千克/小时的速度运输生产某种产品 (生产条件要求 \( 1 \leq  x \leq  {10} \) ),每小时可获得利润是 \( {100}\left( {{5x} + 1 - \frac{3}{x}}\right) \) 元.

(1)要使生产该产品 2 小时获得的利润不低于 3000 元，求 \( x \) 的取值范围；

【答案】 \( 3 \leq  x \leq  {10} \)

根据题意，

\[
{200}\left( {{5x} + 1 - \frac{3}{x}}\right)  \geq  {3000} \Rightarrow  {5x} - {14} - \frac{3}{x} \geq  0
\]

又 \( 1 \leq  x \leq  {10} \) ,可解得 \( 3 \leq  x \leq  {10} \)

(2)要使生产 900 千克该产品获得的利润最大，问:甲厂应该选取何种生产速度？并求最大利润.

【答案】 \( x = 6 \) 时, \( {y}_{\max } = {457500} \) 元.

设利润为 \( y \) 元,

则 \( y = \frac{900}{x} \cdot  {100}\left( {{5x} + 1 - \frac{3}{x}}\right)  = 9 \times  {10}^{4}\left\lbrack  {-3{\left( \frac{1}{x} - \frac{1}{6}\right) }^{2} + \frac{61}{12}}\right\rbrack \)

故 \( x = 6 \) 时, \( {y}_{\max } = {457500} \) 元.

21. 已知函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = 2\sin \left( {\omega x}\right) \) ,其中常数 \( \omega  > 0 \) .

(1)若 \( y = f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( \left\lbrack  {-\frac{\pi }{4},\frac{2\pi }{3}}\right\rbrack \) 上单调递增，求 \( \omega \) 的取值范围；

【答案】 \( 0 < \omega  \leq  \frac{3}{4} \)

因为 \( \omega  > 0 \) ,根据题意有:

\[
\left\{  {\begin{array}{l}  - \frac{\pi }{4}\omega  \geq   - \frac{\pi }{2} \\  \frac{2\pi }{3}\omega  \leq  \frac{\pi }{2} \end{array} \Rightarrow  0 < \omega  \leq  \frac{3}{4}.}\right.
\]
