A. \( \frac{3\sqrt{3}}{2} \) B. \( \frac{5\sqrt{3}}{2} \) C. \( \frac{11}{2} \) D. \( \frac{13}{2} \)

## 【答案】 \( D \)

以 \( O \) 为极点, \( x \) 轴正半轴为极轴建立极坐标系,设 \( A\left( {\rho ,\theta }\right) \) ,则 \( B\left( {\rho ,\theta  + \frac{\pi }{3}}\right) \) ,且 \( \rho \sin \theta  = 1,\rho \cos \theta  = 4\sqrt{3}, B \) 的纵坐标为: \( \rho \sin \left( {\theta  + \frac{\pi }{3}}\right)  = \frac{1}{2}\rho \sin \theta  + \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\rho \cos \theta  = \; \frac{1}{2} + \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \times  4\sqrt{3} = \frac{13}{2} \) . 故答案选 \( D \) .

17. 记方程①: \( {x}^{2} + {a}_{1}x + 1 = 0 \) ,方程②: \( {x}^{2} + {a}_{2}x + 2 = 0 \) ,方程③: \( {x}^{2} + {a}_{3}x + 4 = 0 \) ,其中 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},{a}_{3} \) 是正实数. 当 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},{a}_{3} \) 成等比数列时,下列选项中,能推出方程③无实根的是 ( ).

A. 方程①有实根，且②有实根 B. 方程①有实根，且②无实根

C. 方程①无实根，且②有实根 D. 方程①无实根，且②无实根

## 【答案】 \( B \)

方程③无实根，则 \( {\Delta }_{3} = {a}_{3}^{2} - {16} < 0 \) ，又 \( {\Delta }_{1} = {a}_{1}^{2} - 4,{\Delta }_{2} = {a}_{2}^{2} - 8 \) ，当 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},{a}_{3} \) 成等比数列时, \( {a}_{2}^{2} = {a}_{1}{a}_{3} \) ,即有 \( {a}_{3} = \frac{{a}_{2}^{2}}{{a}_{1}} \) ,由 \( {\Delta }_{3} < 0 \) 得 \( {a}_{3}^{2} - {16} = {\left( \frac{{a}_{2}^{2}}{{a}_{1}}\right) }^{2} - {16} < 0 \) ,即 \( {a}_{2}^{4} \; < {16}{a}_{1}^{2} \)

当方程①有实根，且②无实根时， \( {a}_{1}^{2} > 4 \) ， \( {a}_{2}^{2} < 8 \) ，可以推出 \( {a}_{2}^{4} < {64} < {16} \times  4 < \; {16}{a}_{1}^{2} \) ,选择 \( B \) .

故答案选 \( B \) .

18. 设 \( {P}_{n}\left( {{x}_{n},{y}_{n}}\right) \) 是直线 \( {2x} - y = \frac{n}{n + 1}\left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) 与圆 \( {x}^{2} + {y}^{2} = 2 \) 在第一象限的交点,则极限 \( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{{y}_{n} - 1}{{x}_{n} - 1} = \left( \right) . \)

A. -1

B. \( - \frac{1}{2} \) C. 1 D. 2

【答案】 \( A \)

【法一】当 \( n\infty \) 时,直线 \( {2x} - y = \frac{n}{n + 1}\left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) 趋向于 \( {2x} - y = 1 \) ,直线与圆的交点趋向于 \( P\left( {1,1}\right) \) , \( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{{y}_{n} - 1}{{x}_{n} - 1} \) 可以理解为过点 \( P\left( {1,1}\right) \) 所作的圆的切线的斜率 \( k \) ,设切线方程为 \( y - 1 = k\left( {x - 1}\right) \) ,结合 \( d = r \) ,即 \( \frac{\left| 1 - k\right| }{\sqrt{{k}^{2} + 1}} = \sqrt{2} \) ,解之 \( k =  - 1 \) ,即 \( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n\infty }}\frac{{y}_{n} - 1}{{x}_{n} - 1} =  - 1. \)

【法二】 \( {P}_{n}\left( {{x}_{n},{y}_{n}}\right) \) 在 \( {x}^{2} + {y}^{2} = 2 \) 上,可得 \( {x}_{n}^{2} + {y}_{n}^{2} = 2 \Rightarrow  1 - {x}_{n}^{2} = {y}_{n}^{2} - 1 \Rightarrow  \frac{{y}_{n} - 1}{{x}_{n} - 1} = \; - \frac{{x}_{n} + 1}{{y}_{n} + 1} \)

同【法一】可得 \( {P}_{n}\left( {{x}_{n},{y}_{n}}\right) \) 趋向于 \( P\left( {1,1}\right) \) ,所以 \( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{{y}_{n} - 1}{{x}_{n} - 1} =  - \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{{x}_{n} + 1}{{y}_{n} + 1} =  - 1 \) 选择 \( A \) . 故答案选 \( A \) .

## 【解析】答

19. 如图,在长方体中 \( {ABCD} - {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1}{D}_{1}, A{A}_{1} = 1,{AB} = {AD} = 2, E\text{ 、 }F \) 分![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_191_305_264_381_262_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_191_305_264_381_262_0.jpg)39b5b00_191_305_264_381_262_0.jpg)

(1)证明 \( {A}_{1}\text{ 、 }{C}_{1}\text{ 、 }F\text{ 、 }E \) 四点共面；

【答案】证明过程见解析

由于 \( E\text{ 、 }F \) 分别是棱 \( {AB}\text{ 、 }{BC} \) 的中点,所以 \( {EF}//{AC} \) ,又 \( {AC}//{A}_{1}{C}_{1} \) ,所以 \( {EF}//{A}_{1}{C}_{1} \) ,由公理三的推论,可知 \( {A}_{1}\text{ 、 }{C}_{1}\text{ 、 }F\text{ 、 }E \) 四点共面.

(2)求直线 \( C{D}_{1} \) 与平面 \( {A}_{1}{C}_{1}{FE} \) 所成角的大小.

【答案】 \( \arcsin \frac{\sqrt{15}}{15} \)

连接 \( {A}_{1}F\text{ 、 }{A}_{1}B \) 由于 \( C{D}_{1}//{A}_{1}B \) ,所以直线 \( C{D}_{1} \) 与平面 \( {A}_{1}{C}_{1}{FE} \) 所成角的大小与 \( {A}_{1}B \) 与平面 \( {A}_{1}{C}_{1}{FE} \) 所成角的大小相等. 设 \( {A}_{1}B \) 与平面 \( {A}_{1}{C}_{1}{FE} \) 所成角为 \( \theta \) ,点 \( B \) 到平面 \( {A}_{1}{EF} \) 的距离为 \( d \) ,则 \( \sin \theta  = \frac{d}{{A}_{1}B} \) ,在三棱锥 \( {A}_{1} - {EFB} \) 中,体积 \( {V}_{A - {EFB}} = \; {V}_{B - {A}_{1}{EF}} \) ,所以 \( \frac{1}{3}{S}_{\Delta EFB} \cdot  A{A}_{1} = \frac{1}{3}{S}_{\Delta {A}_{1}{EF}} \cdot  d \) ,即 \( d = \frac{{S}_{\Delta EFB} \cdot  A{A}_{1}}{{S}_{\Delta {A}_{1}{EF}}} \) ,结合题中的数据,可以计算出 \( {S}_{\Delta EFB} = \frac{1}{2},{AF} = {A}_{1}B = \sqrt{5},{A}_{1}F = {EF} = \sqrt{2},{A}_{1}F = \sqrt{6} \) ,由此可以计算出 \( {S}_{\Delta {A}_{1}{EF}} = \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \) ,所以 \( d = \frac{\sqrt{3}}{3} \) ,

所以 \( \sin \theta  = \frac{d}{{A}_{1}B} = \frac{\sqrt{15}}{15} \) ,即 \( \theta  = \arcsin \frac{\sqrt{15}}{15} \) ,所以直线 \( C{D}_{1} \) 与平面 \( {A}_{1}{C}_{1}{FE} \) 所成角的大小为 \( \arcsin \frac{\sqrt{![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_191_470_1606_381_263_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_191_470_1606_381_263_0.jpg)9b5b00_191_470_1606_381_263_0.jpg)

20. 如图， \( A \) 、 \( B \) 、 \( C \) 三地有直道相通， \( {AB} = 5 \) 千米， \( {AC} = 3 \) 千米， \( {BC} = 4 \) 千米，现甲、乙两警员同时从 \( A \) 地出发匀速前往 \( B \) 地,经过 \( t \) 小时,他们之间的距离为 \( f\left( t\right) \) (单位: 千米). 甲的路线是 \( {AB} \) ,速度是 5 千米/小时,乙的路线是 \( {ACB} \) ,速度为 8 千米/小时. 乙到达 \( B \) 地后原地等待,设 \(![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_192_282_419_411_252_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_192_282_419_411_252_0.jpg)39b5b00_192_282_419_411_252_0.jpg)

(1)求 \( {t}_{1} \) 与 \( f\left( {t}_{1}\right) \) 的值；

【答案】 \( \frac{3}{8},\frac{3\sqrt{41}}{8} \) ;

由题中条件可知 \( {t}_{1} = \frac{3}{8} \) 小时,此时甲与 \( A \) 点距离为 \( \frac{15}{8} \) 千米,由余弦定理可知

\( {\left\lbrack  f\left( {t}_{1}\right) \right\rbrack  }^{2} = 9 + {\left( \frac{15}{8}\right) }^{2} - 2 \times  3 \times  \frac{15}{8} \times  \frac{3}{5} = \frac{369}{64} \) ,所以 \( f\left( {t}_{1}\right)  = \frac{3\sqrt{41}}{8} \) ;

( 2 )已知警员的对讲机的有效通话距离为 3 千米. 当 \( {t}_{1} \leq  t \leq  1 \) 时，

【答案】求 \( f\left( t\right) \) 的表达式,并判断 \( f\left( t\right) \) 在 \( \left\lbrack  {{t}_{1},1}\right\rbrack \) 上的最大值是否超过 3 ? 说明理由.

\( f\left( t\right)  = \left\{  {\begin{array}{l} \sqrt{{25}{t}^{2} - {42t} + {18}},\frac{3}{8} \leq  {t}_{1} \leq  \frac{7}{8} \\  5 - {5t},\frac{7}{8} < t \leq  1 \end{array};}\right. \) 最大值不超过 3 .

易知,当 \( t = \frac{7}{8} \) 时乙到达 \( B \) 位置,所以

① 当 \( \frac{3}{8} \leq  t \leq  \frac{7}{8} \) 时， \( {\left\lbrack  f\left( {t}_{1}\right) \right\rbrack  }^{2} = {\left( 7 - 8t\right) }^{2} + {\left( 5 - 5t\right) }^{2} - 2 \cdot  \left( {7 - {8t}}\right)  \cdot  \left( {5 - {5t}}\right)  \cdot  \frac{4}{5} = {25}{t}^{2} \)

\( - {42t} + {18} \)

② 当 \( \frac{7}{8} \leq  t \leq  1 \) 时， \( f\left( t\right)  = 5 - {5t} \) ；综合①②， \( f\left( t\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{l} \sqrt{{25}{t}^{2} - {42t} + {18}},\frac{3}{8} \leq  {t}_{1} \leq  \frac{7}{8} \\  5 - {5t},\frac{7}{8} < t \leq  1 \end{array}\right. \)

当 \( \frac{3}{8} \leq  t \leq  \frac{21}{25} \) 时, \( f\left( t\right) \) 单调递减,此时函数的值域为 \( \left\lbrack  {\frac{3}{5},\frac{3\sqrt{41}}{8}}\right\rbrack \) ;

当 \( \frac{21}{25} \leq  t \leq  \frac{7}{8} \) 时, \( f\left( t\right) \) 单调递增,此时函数的值域为 \( \left\lbrack  {\frac{3}{5},\frac{5}{8}}\right\rbrack \) ;

当 \( \frac{7}{8} \leq  t \leq  1 \) 时, \( f\left( t\right) \) 单调递减,此时函数的值域为 \( \left\lbrack  {0,\frac{5}{8}}\right\rbrack \) ;

由此,函数 \( f\left( t\right) \) 在 \( \left\lbrack  {{t}_{1},1}\right\rbrack \) 上的值域为 \( \left\lbrack  {0,\frac{3\sqrt{41}}{8}}\right\rbrack \) ,而 \( {\left( \frac{3\sqrt{41}}{8}\right) }^{2} < 9 \) ,即 \( \frac{3\sqrt{41}}{8} < 3 \) ,

所以 \( f\left( t\right) \) 在 \( \left\lbrack  {{t}_{1},1}\right\rbrack \) 上的最大值没有超过 3 .

21. 已知椭圆 \( {x}^{2} + 2{y}^{2} = 1 \) ,过原点的两条直线 \( {l}_{1} \) 和 \( {l}_{2} \) 分别与椭圆交于点 \( {AB} \) 和 \( {CD} \) ,记得到的平行四边形 \( {ACBD} \) 的面积为 \( S \) .

(1)设 \( A\left( {{x}_{1},{y}_{1}}\right) \) ， \( C\left( {{x}_{2},{y}_{2}}\right) \) . 用 \( {AC} \) 坐标表示点 \( C \) 到直线 \( {l}_{1} \) 的距离，并证明 \( S = 2\left| {{x}_{1}{y}_{2} - {x}_{2}{y}_{1}}\right| \) ；

【答案】 \( \frac{\left| {y}_{1}{x}_{2} - {y}_{2}{x}_{1}\right| }{\sqrt{{x}_{1}^{2} + {y}_{1}^{2}}} \) ；证明见解析；

由题易知 \( {AC} \) 两点的横坐标不能同时为零,下面分两种情况

① 当 \( {AC} \) 两点的横坐标有一个为零时，不妨设 \( {x}_{1} = 0,{x}_{2} \neq  0 \) 不失一般性,此时 \( {l}_{1} \) 与 \( y \) 轴重合, \( C \) 到直线 \( {l}_{1} \) 的距离为 \( \left| {x}_{2}\right| \) ,平行四边形 \( {ACBD} \) 的面积为 \( S = 2\left| {{x}_{2}{y}_{1}}\right| \) ;

②当 \( {AC} \) 两点的横坐标均不为 0 时，即 \( {l}_{1} \) 和 \( {l}_{2} \) 的斜率均存在时，设 \( {l}_{1} \) 的方程为 \( y = \; {kx} \) ,其中 \( k = \frac{{y}_{1}}{{x}_{1}} \) ,由 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} y = {kx} \\  {x}^{2} + 2{y}^{2} = 1 \end{array}\right. \) 可得 \( \left( {2{k}^{2} + 1}\right) {x}^{2} - 1 = 0 \) ,

所以弦长 \( \left| {AB}\right|  = \sqrt{1 + {k}^{2}}\frac{\sqrt{\Delta }}{\left| A\right| } = \sqrt{1 + {k}^{2}}\frac{\sqrt{4\left( {2{k}^{2} + 1}\right) }}{2{k}^{2} + 1} = 2\sqrt{\frac{1 + {k}^{2}}{2{k}^{2} + 1}} = 2\sqrt{\frac{{x}_{1}^{2} + {y}_{1}^{2}}{2{y}_{1}^{2} + {x}_{1}}} = \; 2\sqrt{{x}_{1}^{2} + {y}_{1}^{2}} \)

点 \( C \) 到直线 \( {l}_{1} \) 的距离 \( d = \frac{\left| k{x}_{2} - {y}_{2}\right| }{\sqrt{1 + {k}^{2}}} = \frac{\left| {y}_{1}{x}_{2} - {y}_{2}{x}_{1}\right| }{\sqrt{{x}_{1}^{2} + {y}_{1}^{2}}} \)

所以四边形 \( {ACBD} \) 的面积为 \( S = \left| {AB}\right|  \cdot  d = 2\left| {{x}_{1}{y}_{2} - {x}_{2}{y}_{1}}\right| \)

综合①②点 \( C \) 到直线 \( {l}_{1} \) 的距离为 \( \frac{\left| {y}_{1}{x}_{2} - {y}_{2}{x}_{1}\right| }{\sqrt{{x}_{1}^{2} + {y}_{1}^{2}}} \) ，平行四边形 \( {ACBD} \) 的面积为

\( 2\left| {{x}_{1}{y}_{2} - {x}_{2}{y}_{1}}\right| \) .

(2)设 \( {l}_{1} \) 与 \( {l}_{2} \) 的斜率之积为 \( - \frac{1}{2} \) ，求面积 \( S \) 的值.

【答案】 \( \sqrt{2} \)

易知两直线的斜率分别为: \( {k}_{{l}_{1}} = \frac{{y}_{1}}{{x}_{1}},{k}_{{l}_{2}} = \frac{{y}_{2}}{{x}_{2}} \) ,由 \( {l}_{1} \) 与 \( {l}_{2} \) 的斜率之积为 \( - \frac{1}{2} \) 可得: \( {x}_{1}{x}_{2} =  - 2{y}_{1}{y}_{2} \) ,又 \( {x}_{1}^{2} = 1 - 2{y}_{1}^{2},{x}_{2}^{2} = 1 - 2{y}_{2}^{2} \) ,

所以 \( {x}_{1}^{2}{x}_{2}^{2} = {\left( -2{y}_{1}{y}_{2}\right) }^{2} = 1 - 2\left( {{y}_{1}^{2} + {y}_{2}^{2}}\right)  + 4{y}_{1}^{2}{y}_{2}^{2} \) ,即 \( {y}_{1}^{2} + {y}_{2}^{2} = \frac{1}{2} \) ,

\( {S}^{2} = {\left( 2\left| {x}_{1}{y}_{2} - {x}_{2}{y}_{1}\right| \right) }^{2} = 4\left( {{x}_{1}^{2}{y}_{2}^{2} + {x}_{2}^{2}{y}_{1}^{2} - 2{x}_{1}{y}_{2}{x}_{2}{y}_{1}}\right)  = 4\left\lbrack  {{y}_{2}^{2}\left( {1 - 2{y}_{1}^{2}}\right)  + {y}_{1}^{2}\left( {1 - 2{y}_{2}^{2}}\right)  + 4{y}_{1}^{2}{y}_{2}^{2}}\right\rbrack \) 化简得 \( {S}^{2} = 4\left( {{y}_{1}^{2} + {y}_{2}^{2}}\right)  = 2 \) ,所以平行四边形的面积为 \( \sqrt{2} \) .

22. 已知数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 与 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 满足 \( {a}_{n + 1} - {a}_{n} = 2\left( {{b}_{n + 1} - {b}_{n}}\right) , n \in  {N}^{ * } \) .

(1)若 \( {b}_{n} = {3n} + 5 \) ，且 \( {a}_{1} = 1 \) ，求 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的通项公式；

【答案】 \( {a}_{n} = {6n} - 5\left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \)

由 \( {b}_{n} = {3n} + 5 \) 可得: \( {a}_{n + 1} - {a}_{n} = 2\left( {{b}_{n + 1} - {b}_{n}}\right)  = 6\left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) ,又 \( {a}_{1} = 1 \) ,所以数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 为以 1 为首项， 6 为公差的等差数列， 即有 \( {a}_{n} = {6n} - 5\left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) ；

(2)设 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的第 \( {n}_{0} \) 项是最大项，即 \( {a}_{{n}_{0}} \geq  {a}_{n}\left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) ，求证: \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 的第 \( {n}_{0} \) 项是最大项；

【答案】证明过程见解析

由 \( {a}_{n + 1} - {a}_{n} = 2\left( {{b}_{n + 1} - {b}_{n}}\right) , n \in  {N}^{ * } \) 可得:

\( {a}_{2} - {a}_{1} = 2\left( {{b}_{2} - {b}_{1}}\right) \)

\( {a}_{3} - {a}_{2} = 2\left( {{b}_{3} - {b}_{2}}\right) \)

...

\( {a}_{n} - {a}_{n - 1} = 2\left( {{b}_{n} - {b}_{n - 1}}\right) \left( {n \geq  2}\right) \)

将上述式子累加可得

\( {a}_{n} - {a}_{1} = 2\left( {{b}_{n} - {b}_{1}}\right) \left( {n \geq  2}\right) , \)

当 \( n = 1 \) 时,也成立,所以 \( {a}_{n} - {a}_{1} = 2\left( {{b}_{n} - {b}_{1}}\right) \left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) ,

由此可得

\( {b}_{n} = \frac{1}{2}{a}_{n} + {b}_{1} - \frac{1}{2}{a}_{1} \) ,由于 \( {b}_{1} - \frac{1}{2}{a}_{1} \) 为常数,

所以当 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的第 \( {n}_{0} \) 项是最大项时, \( \frac{1}{2}{a}_{n} + {b}_{1} - \frac{1}{2}{a}_{1} \) 最大,

即 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 的第 \( {n}_{0} \) 项是最大项;

(3)设 \( {a}_{1} = \lambda  < 0 \) ， \( {b}_{n} = {\lambda }^{n}\left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) ，求 \( \lambda \) 的取值范围，使得 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 有最大值 \( M \) 与最小值 \( m \) ,且 \( \frac{M}{m} \in  \left( {-2,2}\right) \) .

\( \left( {-\frac{1}{2},0}\right) \)

由 (2) 可知 \( {a}_{n} - {a}_{1} = 2\left( {{b}_{n} - {b}_{1}}\right) \left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) ,即 \( {a}_{n} = 2{b}_{n} + {a}_{1} - 2{b}_{1} \) ,结合 \( {a}_{1} = \lambda ,{b}_{n} = {\lambda }^{n} \) 可得

\( {a}_{n} = 2 \cdot  {\lambda }^{n} - \lambda \) ,分三种情况进行讨论:

① 当 \( \lambda  =  - 1 \) 时,则 \( n \) 为偶数时 \( {a}_{n} = 3, n \) 为奇数时 \( {a}_{n} =  - 1 \) ,即有 \( M = 3, m =  - 1 \) , 此时 \( \frac{M}{m} =  - 3 \notin  \left( {-2,2}\right) \) ,由此,此情况不符合条件;

②当 \( \lambda  \in  \left( {-1,0}\right) \) 时，则 \( n \) 为偶数时， \( {\lambda }^{n} = {\left( -\lambda \right) }^{n} \) ，由于 \( \lambda  \in  \left( {-1,0}\right) \) ，所以 \( - \lambda  \in \)

\( \left( {0,1}\right) \) ,从而 \( {\lambda }^{n} \) 随着 \( n \) 增大而减小,此时 \( {\lambda }^{n} > 0,{\left( {\lambda }^{n}\right) }_{\max } = {\lambda }^{2} \) ,无最小值 (无限靠近 \( 0) \) ; \( n \) 为奇数时, \( {\lambda }^{n} < 0 \) ,此时 \( {\lambda }^{n} =  - {\left( -\lambda \right) }^{n} \) ,由于 \( \lambda  \in  \left( {-1,0}\right) \) ,所以 \( - \lambda  \in  \left( {0,1}\right) \) , 从而 \( {\left( -\lambda \right) }^{n} \) 随着 \( n \) 增大而减小,结合 \( {\lambda }^{n} =  - {\left( -\lambda \right) }^{n} \) ,可知随着 \( n \) 增大 \( {\lambda }^{n} \) 值增大,此时 \( {\left( {\lambda }^{n}\right) }_{\min } = \lambda \) ,无最大值 (无限靠近 0 ); 由此可知数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的最大值 \( M = 2{\lambda }^{2} - \lambda \) ,最小值 \( m = {2\lambda } - \lambda  = \lambda ,\frac{M}{m} = \frac{2{\lambda }^{2} - \lambda }{\lambda } = {2\lambda } - 1 \) ,又 \( \frac{M}{m} \in  \left( {-2,2}\right) \) ,所以 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {2\lambda } - 1 < 2 \\  {2\lambda } - 1 >  - 2 \\   - 1 < \lambda  < 0 \end{array}\right. \) , 解之 \( - \frac{1}{2} < \lambda  < 0 \) ;

③ 当 \( \lambda  <  - 1 \) 时，则 \( n \) 为偶数时， \( {\lambda }^{n} = {\left( -\lambda \right) }^{n} \) ，由于 \( \lambda  <  - 1 \) ，所以 \( - \lambda  \in  \left( {1, + \infty }\right) \) ，从而 \( {\lambda }^{n} \) 随着 \( n \) 增大而增大,此时 \( {\lambda }^{n} > 0,{\left( {\lambda }^{n}\right) }_{\min } = {\lambda }^{2} \) ,无最大值 (无限靠近 \( + \infty \) ); \( n \) 为奇数时, \( {\lambda }^{n} < 0 \) ,此时 \( {\lambda }^{n} =  - {\left( -\lambda \right) }^{n} \) ,由于 \( \lambda  <  - 1 \) ,所以 \( - \lambda  > 1 \) ,从而 \( {\left( -\lambda \right) }^{n} \) 随着 \( n \) 增大而增大,结合 \( {\lambda }^{n} =  - {\left( -\lambda \right) }^{n} \) ,可知随着 \( n \) 增大 \( {\lambda }^{n} \) 值减小,此时 \( {\left( {\lambda }^{n}\right) }_{\max } = \lambda \) ,无最小值 (无限靠近 \( - \infty \) ); 由此可知,在 \( \lambda  <  - 1 \) 条件下,数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 无最值,显然不符合条件;

综上,符合条件的实数 \( \lambda \) 的取值范围为 \( \left( {-\frac{1}{2},0}\right) \) .

23. 对于定义域为 \( R \) 的函数 \( g\left( x\right) \) ,若存在正常数 \( T \) ,使得 \( \cos g\left( x\right) \) 是以 \( T \) 为周期的函数,则称 \( g\left( x\right) \) 为余弦周期函数,且称 \( T \) 为其余弦周期. 已知 \( f\left( x\right) \) 是以 \( T \) 为余弦周期的余弦周期函数,其值域为 \( R \) ,设 \( f\left( x\right) \) 单调递增, \( f\left( 0\right)  = 0, f\left( T\right)  = {4\pi } \) .

(1)验证 \( h\left( x\right)  = x + \sin \frac{x}{3} \) 是以 \( {6\pi } \) 为余弦周期的余弦周期函数；

【答案】证明过程见解析

证明: \( \cosh \left( x\right)  = \cos \left( {x + \sin \frac{x}{3}}\right) \) ,

\( \cosh \left( {x + {6\pi }}\right)  = \cos \left( {x + {6\pi } + \sin \frac{x + {6\pi }}{3}}\right)  = \cos \left( {x + {6\pi } + \sin \frac{x}{3}}\right)  = \cos \left( {x + \sin \frac{x}{3}}\right)  = \; \cosh \left( x\right) \)

所以 \( h\left( x\right)  = x + \sin \frac{x}{3} \) 是以 \( {6\pi } \) 为余弦周期的余弦周期函数;

(2) 设 \( a < b \) ,证明对任意 \( c \in  \left\lbrack  {f\left( a\right) , f\left( b\right) }\right\rbrack \) ,存在 \( {x}_{0} \in  \left\lbrack  {a, b}\right\rbrack \) ,使得 \( f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = c \) ;

证明过程见解析

当 \( c = f\left( a\right) \) 或者 \( c = f\left( b\right) \) 时,由于 \( f\left( x\right) \) 单调递增,所以存在 \( {x}_{0} = a \) 或 \( {x}_{0} = b \) 使得

\( f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = a \) 成立; 当 \( c \in  \left( {f\left( x\right) , f\left( b\right) }\right) \) ,构造函数,则 \( p\left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right)  - c, p\left( a\right)  < 0 \) ,

\( p\left( b\right)  > 0 \) ,从而 \( p\left( a\right) p\left( b\right)  < 0 \) ,所以存在 \( {x}_{0} \in  \left( {a, b}\right) \) ,使得 \( p\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = 0 \) ,即存在 \( {x}_{0} \)

\( \in  \left\lbrack  {a, b}\right\rbrack \) ,使得 \( f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = c \) 成立,证毕.

(3) 证明: “ \( {u}_{0} \) 为方程 \( \cos f\left( x\right)  = 1 \) 在 \( \left\lbrack  {0, T}\right\rbrack \) 上的解” 的充要条件是 “ \( {u}_{0} + T \) 为方程 \( \cos f\left( x\right)  = 1 \) 在 \( \left\lbrack  {T,{2T}}\right\rbrack \) 上的解”,并证明对任意 \( x \in  \left\lbrack  {0, T}\right\rbrack \) 都有 \( f\left( {x + T}\right)  = f\left( x\right)  + f\left( T\right) \) .

【答案】证明过程见解析

先证明必要性

\( {u}_{0} \) 为方程 \( \cos f\left( x\right)  = 1 \) 在 \( \left\lbrack  {0, T}\right\rbrack \) 上的解,即 \( \cos f\left( {u}_{0}\right)  = 1 \) ,由 \( {u}_{0} \in  \left\lbrack  {0, T}\right\rbrack \) 可得 \( {u}_{0} + T \; \in  \left\lbrack  {T,{2T}}\right\rbrack \) ,由于函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 是以 \( T \) 为余弦周期的余弦周期函数,所以 \( \cos f\left( {{u}_{0} + T}\right) \; = \cos f\left( {u}_{0}\right)  = 1 \) ,即 \( {u}_{0} + T \) 为方程 \( \cos f\left( x\right)  = 1 \) 在 \( \left\lbrack  {T,{2T}}\right\rbrack \) 上的解;

再证充分性

\( {u}_{0} + T \) 为方程 \( \cos f\left( x\right)  = 1 \) 在 \( \left\lbrack  {T,{2T}}\right\rbrack \) 上的解,即 \( \cos f\left( {{u}_{0} + T}\right)  = 1 \) ,由 \( {u}_{0} + T \in \; \left\lbrack  {T,{2T}}\right\rbrack \) 可得 \( {u}_{0} \in  \left\lbrack  {0, T}\right\rbrack \) ,由于函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 是以 \( T \) 为余弦周期的余弦周期函数,所以

\( \cos f\left( {u}_{0}\right)  = \cos f\left( {{u}_{0} + T}\right)  = 1 \) ,即 \( {u}_{0} \) 为方程 \( \cos f\left( x\right)  = 1 \) 在 \( \left\lbrack  {0, T}\right\rbrack \) 上的解;

下证: 对任意 \( x \in  \left\lbrack  {0, T}\right\rbrack \) 都有 \( f\left( {x + T}\right)  = f\left( x\right)  + f\left( T\right) \) .

由于函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 是以 \( T \) 为余弦周期的余弦周期函数,所以 \( \cos f\left( x\right)  = \cos f\left( {x + T}\right) \) ,即有

\( \cos f\left( x\right)  - \cos f\left( {x + T}\right)  = 0 \) ,所以 \( - 2\sin \frac{f\left( x\right)  + f\left( {x + T}\right) }{2}\sin \frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( {x + T}\right) }{2} = 0 \) ,

即 \( \frac{f\left( x\right)  + f\left( {x + T}\right) }{2} = {k\pi } \) 或 \( \frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( {x + T}\right) }{2} = {k\pi }\left( {k \in  Z}\right) \)

所以 \( f\left( {x + T}\right)  + f\left( x\right)  = {2k\pi } \) 或 \( f\left( {x + T}\right)  = {2k\pi } + f\left( x\right) \left( {k \in  Z}\right) \)

①若 \( f\left( {x + T}\right)  + f\left( x\right)  = {2k\pi } \) ，由 \( f\left( 0\right)  = 0, f\left( T\right)  = {4\pi } \) ，可得 \( k = 2 \) .

所以 \( f\left( {x + T}\right)  + f\left( x\right)  = {4\pi } \) ,这与函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 为增函数矛盾,舍去;

②若 \( f\left( {x + T}\right)  = {2k\pi } + f\left( x\right) \left( {k \in  Z}\right) \) ，由 \( f\left( 0\right)  = 0 \) ， \( f\left( T\right)  = {4\pi } \) ，可得 \( k = 2 \) ，

所以 \( f\left( {x + T}\right)  = {4\pi } + f\left( x\right) \) ,即 \( f\left( {x + T}\right)  = f\left( x\right)  + f\left( T\right) \) .

由此,对任意 \( x \in  \left\lbrack  {0, T}\right\rbrack \) 都有 \( f\left( {x + T}\right)  = f\left( x\right)  + f\left( T\right) \) .

2015 春考

一、填空题(每小题 3 分，满分 36 分)

1. 设全集 \( U = \{ 1,2,3\} , A = \{ 1,2\} \) ，则 \( {\complement }_{U}A = \) ___.

【答案】 \( \{ 3\} \)

全集 \( U = \{ 1,2,3\} ,\;A = \{ 1,2\} \) ,则 \( {\complement }_{U}A = \{ 3\} \) .

\( \{ 3\} \) .

2. 计算: \( \frac{1 + i}{i} = \) ___(其中 \( \mathrm{i} \) 为虚数单位).

【答案】 \( 1 - \mathrm{i} \)

\( \frac{1 + i}{i} = \frac{\left( {1 + \mathrm{i}}\right) \left( {-\mathrm{i}}\right) }{-{i}^{2}} = 1 - \mathrm{i}. \)

\( 1 - \mathrm{i} \) .

3. 函数 \( y = \sin \left( {{2x} + \frac{\pi }{4}}\right) \) 的最小正周期是___.

【答案】 \( \pi \)

函数 \( y = \sin \left( {{2x} + \frac{\pi }{4}}\right) \) 的最小正周期是 \( \frac{2\pi }{2} = \pi \) ,

\( \pi \) .

4. 计算: \( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{{n}^{2} - 3}{2{n}^{2} + n} = \) ___.

【答案】0.5

\( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{{n}^{2} - 3}{2{n}^{2} + n} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{1 - \frac{3}{{n}^{2}}}{2 + \frac{1}{n}} = \frac{1 - 0}{2 + 0} = \frac{1}{2} = {0.5}. \)

0.5 .

5. 以 \( \left( {2,6}\right) \) 为圆心，1 为半径的圆的标准方程为___.

【答案】 \( {\left( x - 2\right) }^{2} + {\left( y - 6\right) }^{2} = 1 \)

以 \( \left( {2,6}\right) \) 为圆心,1 为半径的圆的标准方程为: \( {\left( x - 2\right) }^{2} + {\left( y - 6\right) }^{2} = 1 \) .

\( {\left( x - 2\right) }^{2} + {\left( y - 6\right) }^{2} = 1. \)

6. 已知向量 \( \overrightarrow{a} = \left( {1,3}\right) ,\overrightarrow{b} = \left( {m, - 1}\right) \) ，若 \( \overrightarrow{a}\bot \overrightarrow{b} \) ，则 \( m = \) ___.

【答案】 3

向量 \( \overrightarrow{a} = \left( {1,3}\right) ,\;\overrightarrow{b} = \left( {m, - 1}\right) \) ，若 \( \overrightarrow{a} \bot  \overrightarrow{b} \) ，

则 \( 1 \cdot  m - 3 \times  1 = 0 \)

【解析】得 \( m = 3 \) .

【答案】3.

7. 函数 \( y = {x}^{2} - {2x} + 4, x \in  \left\lbrack  {0,2}\right\rbrack \) 的值域为___.

【答案】 \( \left\lbrack  {3,4}\right\rbrack \)

\( \because y = {x}^{2} - {2x} + 4 = {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2} + 3,\;x \in  \left\lbrack  {0,2}\right\rbrack \)

\( \therefore \) 当 \( x = 1 \) 时, \( {y}_{\min } = 3 \) ; 当 \( x = 2 \) 时, \( {y}_{\max } = 4 \) ,

\( \therefore \) 函数的值域为 \( \left\lbrack  {3,4}\right\rbrack \)

\( \left\lbrack  \begin{array}{ll} 3, & 4 \end{array}\right\rbrack \)

8. 若线性方程组的增广矩阵为 \( \left( \begin{array}{l} a \\  0 \end{array}\right) \) ,解为 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = 2 \\  y = 1 \end{array}\right. \) ,则 \( a + b = \) ___.

## 【答案】 2

由题意知 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = 2 \\  y = 1 \end{array}\right. \) 是方程组 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {ax} = 2 \\  y = b \end{array}\right. \) 的解,

即 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {2a} = 2 \\  1 = b \end{array}\right. \)

则 \( a + b = 1 + 1 = 2 \) ,

2.

9. 方程 \( \lg \left( {{2x} + 1}\right)  + \lg x = 1 \) 的解集为___.

【答案】 \( \{ 2\} \)

\( \because \lg \left( {{2x} + 1}\right)  + \lg x = 1 \) ,

\( \therefore \lg \left( {x\left( {{2x} + 1}\right) }\right)  = \lg {10} \) ,

\( \therefore \left\{  \begin{array}{l} x > 0 \\  {2x} + 1 > 0 \\  x\left( {{2x} + 1}\right)  = {10} \end{array}\right. \) ,

【解析】得: \( x = 2 \) .

【答案】 \( \{ 2\} \) .

10. \( {\left( x + \frac{1}{{x}^{2}}\right) }^{9} \) 的二项展开式中常数项是___(用数字作答).

## 【答案】 84

二项式展开式通项是: \( {T}_{r + 1} = {C}_{9}^{r}{x}^{9 - r}{x}^{-{2r}} = {C}_{9}^{r}{x}^{9 - {3r}} \) ,

令 \( 9 - {3r} = 0 \) 得 \( r = 3 \) ,

故有: \( {C}_{9}^{3} = {84} \)

故答案为 84

11. 用数字 1、2、3、4、5 组成无重复数字的三位数，其中奇数的个数为___. (结果用数值表示)

## 【答案】36

从 1,3,5 中选一个为个位数字, 再从剩下的 4 个数字选 2 个排在前 2 位, 共有 \( {C}_{3}^{1}{A}_{4}^{2} = {36}, \)

36.

12. 已知点 \( A\left( {1,0}\right) \) ,直线 \( l : x =  - 1 \) ,两个动圆均过点 \( A \) 且与 \( l \) 相切,其圆心分别为 \( {C}_{1}\text{ 、 }{C}_{2} \) ,若动点 \( M \) 满足 \( 2\overrightarrow{{C}_{2}M} = \overrightarrow{{C}_{2}{C}_{1}} + \overrightarrow{{C}_{2}A} \) ，则 \( M \) 的轨迹方程为___.

【答案】 \( {y}^{2} = {2x} - 1 \)

由抛物线的定义可得动圆的圆心轨迹方程为 \( {y}^{2} = {4x} \) ,

设 \( {C}_{1}\left( {a, b}\right) ,{C}_{2}\left( {m, n}\right) , M\left( {x, y}\right) \) ,则

\( \because \) 动点 \( M \) 满足 \( 2\overrightarrow{{C}_{2}M} = \overrightarrow{{C}_{2}{C}_{1}} + \overrightarrow{{C}_{2}A} \) ,

\( \therefore 2\left( {x - m,\;y - n}\right)  = \left( {a - m,\;b - n}\right)  + \left( {1 - m,\; - n}\right) \) ,

\( \therefore {2x} = a + 1,\;{2y} = b \) ,

\( \therefore a = {2x} - 1,\;b = {2y} \) ,

\( \because {b}^{2} = {4a} \) ,

\( \therefore {\left( 2y\right) }^{2} = 4\left( {{2x} - 1}\right) \) ,即 \( {y}^{2} = {2x} - 1 \) .

\( {y}^{2} = {2x} - 1. \)

## 二、选择题 (每小题 3 分, 满分 36 分)

13. 若 \( a < 0 < b \) ,则下列不等式恒成立的是 ( )

A. \( \frac{1}{a} > \frac{1}{b} \) B. \( - a > b \) C. \( {a}^{2} > {b}^{2} \) D. \( {a}^{3} < {b}^{3} \)

## 【答案】 \( D \)

\( \because a < 0 < b \) ,

若 \( a =  - 1, b = 1 \) ,

则 \( A, B, C \) 不正确,

对于 \( D \) ,根据幂函数的性质即可判断正确,

\( D \) .

14. 函数 \( y = {x}^{2}\left( {x \geq  1}\right) \) 的反函数为 ( )

A. \( y = \sqrt{x}\left( {x \geq  1}\right) \) B. \( y = \sqrt{-x}\left( {x \leq   - 1}\right) \)

C. \( y = \sqrt{x}\left( {x \geq  0}\right) \) D. \( y = \sqrt{-x}\left( {x \leq  0}\right) \)

【答案】 \( A \)

由 \( y = {x}^{2}\left( {x \geq  1}\right) \) ,得 \( x = \sqrt{y}\left( {y \geq  1}\right) \) ,

\( x, y \) 互换,得 \( y = \sqrt{x}\left( {x \geq  1}\right) \) .

\( \therefore \) 函数 \( y = {x}^{2}\left( {x \geq  1}\right) \) 的反函数为 \( y = \sqrt{x}\left( {x \geq  1}\right) \) .

A.

15. 不等式 \( \frac{2 - {3x}}{x - 1} > 0 \) 的解集为 ( )

A. \( \left( {-\infty ,\frac{3}{4}}\right) \) B. \( \left( {-\infty ,\frac{2}{3}}\right) \)

C. \( \left( {-\infty ,\frac{2}{3}}\right)  \cup  \left( {1, + \infty }\right) \) D. \( \left( {\frac{2}{3},1}\right) \)

【答案】 \( D \)

不等式 \( \frac{2 - {3x}}{x - 1} > 0 \) 的解集就是 \( \left( {x - 1}\right) \left( {{3x} - 2}\right)  < 0 \) ,

【解析】得 \( \frac{2}{3} < x < 1 \) .

【答案】 \( D \) .

16. 下列函数中,是奇函数且在 \( \left( {0, + \infty }\right) \) 上单调递增的为 ( )

A. \( y = {x}^{2} \) B. \( y = {x}^{\frac{1}{3}} \) C. \( y = {x}^{-1} \) D. \( y = {x}^{-\frac{1}{2}} \)

## 【答案】 \( B \)

\( y = {x}^{2} \) 是偶函数，不成立；

\( y = {x}^{\frac{1}{3}} \) 是奇函数在 \( \left( {0, + \infty }\right) \) 上单调递增,所以 \( B \) 成立.

\( C\text{ 、 }D \) 两个选项的函数都是减函数,

B.

17. 直线 \( {3x} - {4y} - 5 = 0 \) 的倾斜角为 ( )

A. \( \arctan \frac{3}{4} \) B. \( \pi  - \arctan \frac{3}{4} \) C. \( \arctan \frac{4}{3} \) D. \( \pi  - \arctan \frac{4}{3} \)

【答案】 \( A \)

直线 \( {3x} - {4y} - 5 = 0 \) 的斜率为: \( \frac{3}{4} \) ,

直线的倾斜角为: \( \theta \) ,则 \( \tan \theta  = \frac{3}{4} \) .

可得 \( \theta  = \arctan \frac{3}{4} \) .

A.

18. 底面半径为 1,母线长为 2 的圆锥的体积为 ( )

A. \( {2\pi } \) B. \( \sqrt{3}\pi \) C. \( \frac{2\pi }{3} \) D. \( \frac{\sqrt{3}\pi }{3} \)

## 【答案】 \( D \)

底面半径为 1,母线长为 2 的圆锥的高为: \( \sqrt{3} \) .

底面半径为 1,母线长为 2 的圆锥的体积为: \( \frac{1}{3} \times  {1}^{2} \cdot  \pi  \cdot  \sqrt{3} = \frac{\sqrt{3}\pi }{3} \) .

故选 \( D \)

19. 以 \( \left( {-3,0}\right) \) 和 \( \left( {3,0}\right) \) 为焦点,长轴长为 8 的椭圆方程为 ( )

A. \( \frac{{x}^{2}}{16} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{25} = 1 \) B. \( \frac{{x}^{2}}{16} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{7} = 1 \) C. \( \frac{{x}^{2}}{25} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{16} = 1 \) D. \( \frac{{x}^{2}}{7} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{16} = 1 \)

## 【答案】 \( B \)

以 \( \left( {-3,0}\right) \) 和 \( \left( {3,0}\right) \) 为焦点,长轴长为 8 的椭圆,可知 \( a = 4, c = 3 \) ,则 \( b = \sqrt{7} \) ,

椭圆的标准方程为: \( \frac{{x}^{2}}{16} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{7} = 1 \) .

B.

20. 在复平面上,满足 \( \left| {z - 1}\right|  = \left| {z + \mathrm{i}}\right| \) ( \( \mathrm{i} \) 为虚数单位) 的复数 \( z \) 对应的点的轨迹为 ( )

A. 椭圆 B. 圆 C. 线段 D. 直线

## 【答案】 \( D \)

设 \( z = x + {yi} \) ,满足 \( \left| {z - 1}\right|  = \left| {z + \mathrm{i}}\right| \) ,

\( \sqrt{{\left( x - 1\right) }^{2} + {y}^{2}} = \sqrt{{x}^{2} + {\left( y + 1\right) }^{2}}, \)

化简可得: \( - {2x} = {2y} \) ,即 \( x + y = 0 \) .

轨迹方程为: 直线.

D.

21. 若无穷等差数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的首项 \( {a}_{1} > 0 \) ,公差 \( d < 0,\left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的前 \( n \) 项和为 \( {S}_{n} \) ,则 ( )

A. \( {S}_{n} \) 单调递减 B. \( {S}_{n} \) 单调递增 C. \( {S}_{n} \) 有最大值 D. \( {S}_{n} \) 有最小值

## 【答案】 \( C \)

\( \because \) 无穷等差数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的首项 \( {a}_{1} > 0 \) ,公差 \( d < 0 \) ,

\( \therefore \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 是递减数列,且先正值,后负值;

\( \therefore \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的前 \( n \) 项和为 \( {S}_{n} \) 先增加,后减小;

\( \therefore {S}_{n} \) 有最大值;

\( C \) .

( )

A. \( {a}^{2} + {b}^{2} \) 有最小值 B. \( \sqrt{ab} \) 有最小值

C. \( \frac{1}{a} + \frac{1}{b} \) 有最大值 D. \( \frac{1}{\sqrt{a} + \sqrt{b}} \) 有最大值

【答案】 \( A \)

\( \because a > 0, b > 0 \) ,且 \( a + b = 4 \) ,

\( {a}^{2} + {b}^{2} = {\left( a + b\right) }^{2} - {2ab} = {16} - {2ab} \geq  {16} - 2{\left( \frac{a + b}{2}\right) }^{2} = {16} - 8 = 8, \)

有最小值,

A.

23. 组合数 \( {C}_{n}^{m} + 2{C}_{n}^{m - 1} + {C}_{n}^{m - 2}\left( {n \geq  m \geq  2, m, n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) 恒等于 ( )

A. \( {C}_{n + 2}^{m} \) B. \( {C}_{n + 2}^{m + 1} \) C. \( {C}_{n + 1}^{m} \) D. \( {C}_{n + 1}^{m + 1} \)

## 【答案】 \( A \)

组合数 \( {C}_{n}^{m} + 2{C}_{n}^{m - 1} + {C}_{n}^{m - 2} = {C}_{n}^{m} + {C}_{n}^{m - 1} + {C}_{n}^{m - 1} + {C}_{n}^{m - 2} = {C}_{n + 1}^{m} + {C}_{n + 1}^{m - 1} = {C}_{n + 2}^{m} \) .

A.

24. 设集合 \( {P}_{1} = \left\{  {x \mid  {x}^{2} + {ax} + {10}}\right\}  ,{P}_{2} = \left\{  {x \mid  {x}^{2} + {ax} + {20}}\right\}  ,{Q}_{1} = \left\{  {x \mid  {x}^{2} + x + {b0}}\right\}  ,{Q}_{2} = \; \left\{  {x \mid  {x}^{2} + {2x} + {b0}}\right\} \) ,其中 \( a, b \in  R \) ,下列说法正确的是 ( )

A. 对任意 \( a,{P}_{1} \) 是 \( {P}_{2} \) 的子集,对任意 \( b,{Q}_{1} \) 不是 \( {Q}_{2} \) 的子集

B. 对任意 \( a,{P}_{1} \) 是 \( {P}_{2} \) 的子集,存在 \( b \) ,使得 \( {Q}_{1} \) 是 \( {Q}_{2} \) 的子集

C. 存在 \( a,{P}_{1} \) 不是 \( {P}_{2} \) 的子集,对任意 \( b,{Q}_{1} \) 不是 \( {Q}_{2} \) 的子集

D. 存在 \( a,{P}_{1} \) 不是 \( {P}_{2} \) 的子集,存在 \( b \) ,使得 \( {Q}_{1} \) 是 \( {Q}_{2} \) 的子集

## 【答案】 \( B \)

对于集合 \( {P}_{1} = \left\{  {x \mid  {x}^{2} + {ax} + {10}}\right\}  ,{P}_{2} = \left\{  {x \mid  {x}^{2} + {ax} + {20}}\right\} \) ,

可得当 \( m \in  {P}_{1} \) ,即 \( {m}^{2} + {am} + 1 > 0 \) ,可得 \( {m}^{2} + {am} + 2 > 0 \) ,

即有 \( m \in  {P}_{2} \) ,可得对任意 \( a,{P}_{1} \) 是 \( {P}_{2} \) 的子集;

当 \( b = 5 \) 时, \( {Q}_{1} = \left\{  {x \mid  {x}^{2} + x + {50}}\right\}   = R,{Q}_{2} = \left\{  {x \mid  {x}^{2} + {2x} + {50}}\right\}   = R \) ,

可得 \( {Q}_{1} \) 是 \( {Q}_{2} \) 的子集；

当 \( b = 1 \) 时, \( {Q}_{1} = \left\{  {x \mid  {x}^{2} + x + {10}}\right\}   = R,{Q}_{2} = \left\{  {x \mid  {x}^{2} + {2x} + {10}}\right\}   = \{ x \mid  x \neq   - 1 \) 且 \( x \in  R\} \) ,

可得 \( {Q}_{1} \) 不是 \( {Q}_{2} \) 的子集.

综上可得,对任意 \( a,{P}_{1} \) 是 \( {P}_{2} \) 的子集,存在 \( b \) ,使得 \( {Q}_{1} \) 是 \( {Q}_{2} \) 的子集.

B.

## 三、解答题(共 5 大题，满分 48 分)

25. 如图,在正四棱柱中 \( {ABCD} - {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1}{D}_{1},{AB} = 1,{D}_{1}B \) 和平面 \( {ABCD} \) 所成的角的大小为 \( \arctan \f![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_205_267_868_286_331_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_205_267_868_286_331_0.jpg)39b5b00_205_267_868_286_331_0.jpg)

## 【答案】 8

\( \because \) 正四棱柱 \( {ABCD} - {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 的侧棱 \( {D}_{1}D \bot \) 底面 \( {ABCD} \) ,连结 \( {BD} \) ,

\( \therefore \angle {D}_{1}{BD} \) 为直线 \( B{D}_{1} \) 与底面 \( {ABCD} \) 所成的角,

\( {D}_{1}B \) 和平面 \( {ABCD} \) 所成的角的大小为 \( \arctan \frac{3\sqrt{2}}{4} \) ,

\( \therefore \tan \angle {D}_{1}{BD} = \frac{D{D}_{1}}{\sqrt{2}}, D{D}_{1} = \sqrt{2} \times  \frac{3\sqrt{2}}{4} = \frac{3}{2} \) ,

\( \therefore \) 正四棱柱 \( {ABCD} - {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 的侧面积 \( S = 4 \times  1 \times  \frac{3}{2} = 6 \) ,

底面积为 \( ![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_205_421_1734_286_337_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_205_421_1734_286_337_0.jpg)9b5b00_205_421_1734_286_337_0.jpg)

26. 已知 \( a \) 是实数,函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = \frac{{x}^{2} + {ax} + 4}{x} \) 是奇函数,求 \( f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( \left( {0, + \infty }\right) \) 上的最小值及取到最小值时 \( x \) 的值.

## 【答案】 4

\( \because \) 函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = \frac{{x}^{2} + {ax} + 4}{x} \) 是奇函数,

\( \therefore \frac{{x}^{2} - {ax} + 4}{-x} =  - \frac{{x}^{2} + {ax} + 4}{x} \) ,

\( \therefore a = 0 \) ,

\( \therefore f\left( x\right)  = x + \frac{4}{x} \) ,

\( \because x > 0 \) ,

\( \therefore f\left( x\right)  = x + \frac{4}{x} \geq  2\sqrt{x\frac{4}{x}} = 4 \) ,

当且仅当 \( x = 2 \) 时, \( f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( \left( {0, + \infty }\right) \) 上的最小值为 4 .

27. 某船在海平面 \( A \) 处测得灯塔 \( B \) 在北偏东 30 。方向,与 \( A \) 相距 6.0 海里. 船由 \( A \) 向正北方向航行 8.1 海里达到 \( C \) 处,这时灯塔 \( B \) 与船相距多少海里 (精确到 0.1 海里)? \( B \) 在船的什么方向 (精确到 1 。)?

## 【答案】 46

由余弦定理可得 \( {BC} = \sqrt{{6}^{2} + {8.1}^{2} - 2 \times  6 \times  {8.1} \times  \cos {30}^{ \circ  }} \approx  {4.2} \) 海里,

由正弦定理可得 \( \frac{6}{\sin \angle {BCA}} = \frac{4.2}{\frac{1}{2}} \) ,

结合图形,可得 \( \angle {BCA} \approx  {46} \circ \) ,

![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_207_416_224_187_312_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_207_416_224_187_312_0.jpg)39b5b00_207_416_224_187_312_0.jpg)

28. 已知点 \( {F}_{1}\text{ 、 }{F}_{2} \) 依次为双曲线 \( C : \frac{{x}^{2}}{{a}^{2}} - \frac{{y}^{2}}{{b}^{2}} = 1\left( {a,{b0}}\right) \) 的左右焦点， \( \left| {{F}_{1}{F}_{2}}\right|  = 6 \) ， \( {B}_{1}\left( {0, - b}\right) \) ， \( {B}_{2}\left( {0, b}\right) \) .

(1)若 \( a = \sqrt{5} \) ，以 \( \overrightarrow{d} = \left( {3, - 4}\right) \) 为方向向量的直线 \( l \) 经过 \( {B}_{1} \) ，求 \( {F}_{2} \) 到 \( l \) 的距离；

【答案】 \( \frac{18}{5} \)

由题意可知: \( c = 3,{F}_{2}\left( {3,0}\right) \) ,

\( {c}^{2} = {a}^{2} + {b}^{2},\;a = \sqrt{5},\;\therefore b = 2, \)

设直线 \( l \) 的方程为 \( y = {kx} + m \) ,

\( \overrightarrow{d} = \left( {3, - 4}\right) \) 为方向向量的直线 \( l,\therefore k =  - \frac{4}{3} \) ,

点 \( {B}_{1}\left( {0, - 2}\right) \) 在直线 \( l \) 上, \( m =  - 2 \) ,

\( \therefore \) 直线方程为 \( {4x} + {3y} + 6 = 0 \) ,

\( {F}_{2} \) 到 \( l \) 的距离 \( d = \frac{\left| 4 \times  3 + 4 \times  0 + 6\right| }{\sqrt{{4}^{2} + {3}^{2}}} = \frac{18}{5} \)

(2)若双曲线 \( C \) 上存在点 \( P \) ，使得 \( \overrightarrow{P{B}_{1}}\overrightarrow{P{B}_{2}} =  - 2 \) ，求实数 \( b \) 的取值范围.

\( \left\lbrack  {\frac{\sqrt{22}}{2},3}\right) \)

由题意可知: \( c = 3 \) ,设 \( P\left( {{x}_{0},{y}_{0}}\right) \) ,

\( {c}^{2} = {a}^{2} + {b}^{2} \) ,得 \( {a}^{2} = {c}^{2} - {b}^{2} = 9 - {b}^{2} \) ,①

\( \overrightarrow{P{B}_{1}} = \left( {{x}_{0},\;{y}_{0} + b}\right) ,\;\overrightarrow{P{B}_{2}} = \left( {{x}_{0},\;{y}_{0} - b}\right) , \)

\( \overrightarrow{P{B}_{1}}\overrightarrow{P{B}_{2}} =  - 2 \) ，整理得: \( {x}_{0}^{2} + {y}_{0}^{2} - {b}^{2} =  - 2 \) ，

则: \( {x}_{0}^{2} = {b}^{2} - {y}_{0}^{2} - 2 \) ,②

由点 \( P \) 在双曲线上: \( \therefore \frac{{x}_{0}^{2}}{{a}^{2}} - \frac{{y}_{0}^{2}}{{b}^{2}} = 1 \) ,③

将①②代入③整理得: \( \frac{{b}^{2} - {y}_{0}^{2} - 2}{9 - {b}^{2}} - \frac{{y}_{0}^{2}}{{b}^{2}} = 1 \) ，

\( \therefore \left( {{b}^{2} - {y}_{0}^{2} - 2}\right)  \times  {b}^{2} - {y}_{0}^{2} \times  \left( {9 - {b}^{2}}\right)  = \left( {9 - {b}^{2}}\right)  \times  {b}^{2} \) ,

整理得: \( 2{b}^{4} - {11}{b}^{2} = 9{y}_{0}^{2} \) ,

\( \because {y}_{0}^{2} \geq  0,\;\therefore 2{b}^{4} - {11}{b}^{2} \geq  0 \) ,

【解析】得: \( b \geq  \frac{\sqrt{22}}{2},\because b < 3 \) ,

实数 \( b \) 的取值范围 \( \left\lbrack  {\frac{\sqrt{22}}{2},3}\right) \) .

29. 已知函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = \left| {{2}^{x - 2} - 2}\right| \left( {x \in  R}\right) \) .

(1)解不等式 \( f\left( x\right)  < 2 \) ;

【答案】 \( x < 4 \)

\( f\left( x\right)  = \left| {{2}^{x - 2} - 2}\right|  < 2, \)

即 \( - 2 < {2}^{x - 2} - 2 < 2 \) ,

即 \( 0 < {2}^{x - 2} < 4 \) ,

故 \( x < 4 \) ；

( 2 )数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 满足 \( {a}_{n} = f\left( n\right) \left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) ， \( {S}_{n} \) 为 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的前 \( n \) 项和，对任意的 \( n \geq  4 \) ，不等式 \( {S}_{n} + \frac{1}{2} \geq  k{a}_{n} \) 恒成立,求实数 \( k \) 的取值范围.

\( k \leq  \frac{25}{14} \)

\( {a}_{n} = \left| {{2}^{n - 2} - 2}\right| \)

\( n \geq  4 \) 时, \( {S}_{n} = {a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + \cdots  + {a}_{n} \)

\( = \left( {2 - {2}^{-1}}\right)  + \left( {2 - {2}^{0}}\right)  + \left( {{2}^{1} - 2}\right)  + \left( {{2}^{2} - 2}\right)  + \cdots  + \left( {{2}^{n - 2} - 2}\right) \)

\( = \frac{5}{2} + \frac{2\left( {{2}^{n - 2} - 1}\right) }{2 - 1} - 2\left( {n - 2}\right) \)

\( = \frac{9}{2} + {2}^{n - 1} - {2n},\;{S}_{n} + \frac{1}{2} = 5 + {2}^{n - 1} - {2n}; \)

\( \because {S}_{n} + \frac{1}{2} \geq  k{a}_{n}, \)

\( \therefore k \leq  \frac{{2}^{n - 1} + 5 - {2n}}{{2}^{n - 2} - 2} \) ,

\( {y}_{n} = g\left( n\right)  = \frac{{2}^{n - 1} + 5 - {2n}}{{2}^{n - 2} - 2} = \frac{2\left( {{2}^{n - 2} - 2}\right)  + 9 - {2n}}{{2}^{n - 2} - 2} \)

\( = 2 + \frac{9 - {2n}}{{2}^{n - 2} - 2}g\left( {n + 1}\right)  - g\left( n\right)  = \frac{9 - 2\left( {n + 1}\right) }{{2}^{n - 1} - 2} - \frac{9 - {2n}}{{2}^{n - 2} - 2} \)

\[
= \frac{\left( {7 - {2n}}\right) \left( {{2}^{n - 2} - 2}\right)  - \left( {9 - {2n}}\right) \left( {{2}^{n - 1} - 2}\right) }{\left( {{2}^{n - 1} - 2}\right) \left( {{2}^{n - 2} - 2}\right) }
\]

\( = \frac{\left( {{2n} - {11}}\right) {2}^{n - 2} + 4}{\left( {{2}^{n - 1} - 2}\right) \left( {{2}^{n - 2} - 2}\right) }, \)

故当 \( n \geq  6, g\left( {n + 1}\right)  - g\left( n\right)  > 0 \) ,

即 \( g\left( 6\right)  < g\left( 7\right)  < g\left( 8\right)  < \cdots  < g\left( n\right) ,\;\left( {n \geq  6}\right) \) ;

又 \( \because g\left( 4\right)  = \frac{5}{2} > g\left( 5\right)  = \frac{11}{6} > g\left( 6\right)  = \frac{25}{14} \) ,

\( \therefore {g}_{\min }\left( n\right)  = g\left( 6\right)  = \frac{25}{14} \) ,

故 \( k \leq  \frac{25}{14} \) .

一、选择题 (本大题满分 9 分) 本大题共有 4 题, 每题有且只有一个正确答案, 考生应在答题纸的相应编号上, 将代表答案的小方格涂黑, 选对得 3 分, 否则一律得 0 分.

30. 对于集合 \( A\text{ 、 }B, \) “ \( A \neq  B \) ” 是 “ \( A \cap  B \subsetneqq  A \cup  B \) ” 的 ( )

A. 充分非必要条件 B. 必要非充分条件

C. 充要条件 D. 既非充分也非必要条件

## 【答案】 \( C \)

\( \because A \cap  B \subset  A \subset  A \cup  B \) ,

\( \therefore A \neq  B \) ” 是 “ \( A \cap  B \subsetneqq  A \cup  B \) ” 的充要条件,

\( C \) .

31. 对于任意实数 \( a\text{ 、 }b,{\left( a - b\right) }^{2} \geq  {kab} \) 均成立,则实数 \( k \) 的取值范围是 ( )

A. \( \{  - 4,0\} \) B. \( \left\lbrack  {-4,0}\right\rbrack \)

C. \( ( - \infty ,0\rbrack \) D. \( \left( {-\infty , - 4\rbrack \cup \lbrack 0, + \infty }\right) \)

【答案】 \( B \)

\( \because {\left( a - b\right) }^{2} \geq  {kab} \) ,

\( \therefore {a}^{2} + {b}^{2} \geq  {kab} + {2ab} \) ,

即 \( {a}^{2} + {b}^{2} \geq  \left( {2 + k}\right) {ab} \) 恒成立,

故 \( - 2 \leq  2 + k \leq  2 \) ,

故 \( k \in  \left\lbrack  {-4,0}\right\rbrack \) ,

B.

32. 已知数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 满足 \( {a}_{n} + {a}_{n + 4} = {a}_{n + 1} + {a}_{n + 3}\left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) ,那么必有 ( )

A. \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 是等差数列 B. \( \left\{  {a}_{{2n} - 1}\right\} \) 是等差数列

C. \( \left\{  {a}_{2n}\right\} \) 是等差数列 D. \( \left\{  {a}_{3n}\right\} \) 是等差数列

## 【答案】 \( D \)

\( \because {a}_{n} + {a}_{n + 4} = {a}_{n + 1} + {a}_{n + 3}\left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) ,

\( \therefore {a}_{n + 4} - {a}_{n + 1} = {a}_{n + 3} - {a}_{n} \) ,

\( \therefore {a}_{n + 5} - {a}_{n + 2} = {a}_{n + 4} - {a}_{n + 1},{a}_{n + 6} - {a}_{n + 3} = {a}_{n + 5} - {a}_{n + 2} \) ,

\( \therefore {a}_{n + 6} - {a}_{n + 3} = {a}_{n + 3} - {a}_{n} \) ,

\( \therefore \) 数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{3n}\right\} \) 是等差数列,

D.

二、填空题(本大题满分 9 分)本大题共有 3 小题，考生应在答题纸相应编号的空格内直接填写结果, 每个空格填对得 3 分, 否则一律得 0 分.

33. 关于 \( x \) 的实系数一元二次方程 \( {x}^{2} + {px} + 2 = 0 \) 的两个虚数根为 \( {z}_{1}\text{ 、 }{z}_{2} \) ，若 \( {z}_{1}\text{ 、 }{z}_{2} \) 在复平面上对应的点是经过原点的椭圆的两个焦点, 则该椭圆的长轴长为___.

【答案】 \( 2\sqrt{2} \)

因为 \( p \) 为实数， \( p \neq  0 \) ， \( {z}_{1} \) ， \( {z}_{2} \) 为虚数，

所以 \( {p}^{2} - 4 \times  2 < 0 \) ,即 \( {p}^{2} < 8 \) ,

【解析】得 \( - 2\sqrt{2} < p < 2\sqrt{2} \) .

由 \( {z}_{1},{z}_{2} \) 为共轭复数,知 \( {Z}_{1},{Z}_{2} \) 关于 \( x \) 轴对称,

所以椭圆短轴在 \( x \) 轴上,又由椭圆经过原点,

可知原点为椭圆短轴的一端点,

根据椭圆的性质, 复数加, 减法几何意义及一元二次方程根与系数的关系,

可得椭圆的短轴长 \( = {2b} = \left| {{z}_{1} + {z}_{2}}\right|  = \left| p\right| \) ,

焦距 \( {2c} = \left| {{z}_{1} - {z}_{2}}\right|  = \sqrt{8 - {p}^{2}} \) ,

长轴长 \( {2a} = \sqrt{8 - {p}^{2} + {p}^{2}} = 2\sqrt{2} \) ,

【答案】 \( 2\sqrt{2} \) .

34. 已知圆心为 \( O \) ,半径为 1 的圆上有三点 \( A\text{ 、 }B\text{ 、 }C \) ,若 \( 7\overrightarrow{OA} + 5\overrightarrow{OB} + 8\overrightarrow{OC} = \overrightarrow{0} \) ,则 \( \left| \overrightarrow{BC}\right|  = \) ___.

## 【答案】 \( \sqrt{3} \)

\( 7\overrightarrow{OA} + 5\overrightarrow{OB} + 8\overrightarrow{OC} = \overrightarrow{0} \) ,可得 \( 7\overrightarrow{OA} =  - \left( {5\overrightarrow{OB} + 8\overrightarrow{OC}}\right) \) ,

两边平方可得, \( {49} = {25} + {64} + 2 \times  5 \times  8\overrightarrow{OB}\overrightarrow{OC} \) ,

【解析】得 \( \overrightarrow{OB}\overrightarrow{OC} =  - \frac{1}{2} \) ,

由 \( \overrightarrow{OB}\overrightarrow{OC} = \left| \overrightarrow{OB}\right| \left| \overrightarrow{OC}\right| \cos \angle {BOC} = \cos \angle {BOC} =  - \frac{1}{2} \) ，

即有 \( \left| \overrightarrow{BC}\right|  = \sqrt{1 + 1 - 2 \times  1 \times  1 \times  \left( {-\frac{1}{2}}\right) } = \sqrt{3} \) .

【答案】 \( \sqrt{3} \) .

35. 函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 与 \( g\left( x\right) \) 的图象拼成如图所示的 “ \( Z \) ” 字形折线段 \( {ABOCD} \) ,不含 \( A\left( {0,1}\right) \) , \( B\left( {1,1}\right) , O\left( {0,0}\right) , C\left( {-1, - 1}\right) , D\left( {0, - 1}\right) \) 五个点,若 \( f\left( x\right) \) 的图象关于原点对称的图形即为 \( g\left( x\![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_211_275_1575_341_353_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_211_275_1575_341_353_0.jpg)9b5b00_211_275_1575_341_353_0.jpg)

【答案】 \( f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} x, &  - 1 < x < 0 \\  1, & 0 < x < 1 \end{array}\right. \)

由图可知,线段 \( {OC} \) 与线段 \( {OB} \) 是关于原点对称的,

线段 \( {CD} \) 与线段 \( {BA} \) 也是关于原点对称的,

根据题意, \( f\left( x\right) \) 与 \( g\left( x\right) \) 的图象关于原点对称,

所以 \( f\left( x\right) \) 的图象可以在 \( {OC} \) 或 \( {CD} \) 中选取一个,再在 \( {AB} \) 或 \( {OB} \) 中选取一个,

比如其组合形式为: \( {OC} \) 和 \( {AB},{CD} \) 和 \( {OB} \) ,

且 \( {OC} \) 的方程为: \( y = x\left( {-1 < x < 0}\right) ,{OB} \) 的方程为: \( y = x\left( {0 < x < 1}\right) \) ,

所以, \( f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  {\begin{array}{ll} x, &  - 1 < x < 0 \\  1, & 0 < x < 1 \end{array}, g\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll}  - 1, &  - 1 < x < 0 \\  x, & 0 < x < 1 \end{array}\right. }\right. \) ,

或 \( f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  {\begin{array}{ll}  - 1, &  - 1 < x < 0 \\  x, & 0 < x < 1 \end{array}, g\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} x, &  - 1 < x < 0 \\  1, & 0 < x < 1 \end{array}\right. }\right. \) ,

\( f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} x, &  - 1 < x < 0 \\  1, & 0 < x < 1 \end{array}\right. \)

三、解答题 (本大题满分 12 分) 解答本题必须在答题纸相应编号的规定区域内写出必要的步骤.

36. 对于函数 \( f\left( x\right) \text{ 、 }g\left( x\right) \) ,存在函数 \( h\left( x\right) \) ,使得 \( f\left( x\right)  = g\left( x\right) h\left( x\right) \) ,则称 \( f\left( x\right) \) 是 \( g\left( x\right) \) 的 “ \( h\left( x\right) \) 关联函数”.

(1)已知 \( f\left( x\right)  = \sin x, g\left( x\right)  = \cos x \) ,是否存在定义域为 \( R \) 的函数 \( h\left( x\right) \) ,使得 \( f\left( x\right) \) 是 \( g\left( x\right) \) 的 “ \( h\left( x\right) \) 关联函数”? 若存在,写出 \( h\left( x\right) \) 的解析式; 若不存在,请说明理由;

【答案】不存在

假设存在定义域为 \( R \) 的函数 \( h\left( x\right) \) ,

使得 \( f\left( x\right) \) 是 \( g\left( x\right) \) 的 “ \( h\left( x\right) \) 关联函数”.

即有 \( \sin x = \cos {xh}\left( x\right) \) ,解得 \( h\left( x\right)  = \tan x \) ,

由 \( \tan x \) 的定义域为 \( \left\{  {x\left| {\;x \neq  {k\pi } + \frac{\pi }{2}}\right. , k \in  Z}\right\} \) ,

故不存在定义域为 \( R \) 的函数 \( h\left( x\right) \) ；

(2)已知函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 、 \( g\left( x\right) \) 的定义域为 \( \lbrack 1, + \infty ) \) ，当 \( x \in  \lbrack n \) ， \( n + 1) \) 时， \( f\left( x\right)  = \; {2}^{n - 1}\sin \frac{x}{n} - 1 \) ,若存在函数 \( {h}_{1}\left( x\right) \) 及 \( {h}_{2}\left( x\right) \) ,使得 \( f\left( x\right) \) 是 \( g\left( x\right) \) 的 “ \( {h}_{1}\left( x\right) \) 关联函数”, 且 \( g\left( x\right) \) 是 \( f\left( x\right) \) 的 “ \( {h}_{2}\left( x\right) \) 关联函数”,求方程 \( g\left( x\right)  = 0 \) 的解.

\( x = \frac{\pi }{2} \) ,当且仅当 \( n = 1 \) shi

由题意可得 \( f\left( x\right)  = g\left( x\right) {h}_{1}\left( x\right) , g\left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right) {h}_{2}\left( x\right) \) , 相乘可得, \( {h}_{1}\left( x\right) {h}_{2}\left( x\right)  = 1 \) , 即有 \( g\left( x\right)  = 0 \) ,即为 \( f\left( x\right)  = 0 \) ,

即 \( {2}^{n - 1}\sin \frac{x}{n} - 1 = 0 \) ,即 \( \sin \frac{x}{n} = \frac{1}{{2}^{n - 1}} \) ,

由 \( x \in  \lbrack n, n + 1) \) ,可得 \( \frac{x}{n} \in  \lbrack 1,1 + \frac{1}{n}) \) ,

可得 \( \sin \frac{x}{n} \in  \left\lbrack  {\sin 1,1}\right\rbrack  ,\left( {\sin 1\frac{1}{2}}\right) \) ,

\( n = 1,\;x = \frac{\pi }{2} \) 时取得最大值 1,

\( {2}^{1 - n} \in  (0,1\rbrack \) ,仅在 \( n = 1 \) 取得 1,

当 \( n \geq  2 \) 时， \( {2}^{1 - n} \in  \left( {0,\frac{1}{2}}\right\rbrack \) ,

与 \( \sin \frac{x}{n} \) 的值域无交集,

只有 \( n = 1, x = \frac{\pi }{2} \) 有解.

## 2016 秋考

## 填空

1. 设 \( x \in  R \) ，则不等式 \( \left| {x - 3}\right|  < 1 \) 的解集为___.

【答案】 \( \left( {2,4}\right) \)

\( - 1 < x - 3 < 1 \) ,即 \( 2 < x < 4 \) ,故解集为 \( \left( {2,4}\right) \) .

2. 设 \( z = \frac{3 + {2i}}{i} \) ，其中 \( \mathrm{i} \) 为虚数单位，则 \( \operatorname{Im}z = \) ___.

【答案】 -3

\( z =  - \mathrm{i}\left( {3 + 2\mathrm{i}}\right)  = 2 - 3\mathrm{i} \) ,故 \( \operatorname{Im}z =  - 3 \) .

3. \( {l}_{1} : {{2x} + y - 1} = 0,\;{l}_{2} : {{2x} + y + 1} = 0 \) ，则 \( {l}_{1},{l}_{2} \) 的距离为___.

【答案】 \( \frac{2\sqrt{5}}{5} \)

\( d = \frac{\left| 1 + 1\right| }{\sqrt{{2}^{2} + {1}^{2}}} = \frac{2\sqrt{5}}{5}. \)

4. 某次体检, 6 位同学的身高 (单位: 米) 分别为 1.72, 1.78, 1.75, 1.80, 1.69, 1.77, 则这组数据的中位数是___(米).

【答案】 1.76

这组数最中间的两个数为 1.75,1.77,所以 \( \frac{{1.75} + {1.77}}{2} = {1.76} \) .

5. 已知点 \( \left( {3,9}\right) \) 在函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = 1 + {a}^{x} \) 的图像上，则 \( f\left( x\right) \) 的反函数 \( {f}^{-1}\left( x\right)  = \) ___.

【答案】 \( {\log }_{2}\left( {x - 1}\right) \)

\( {a}^{3} + 1 = 9 \) ,故 \( a = 2, f\left( x\right)  = 1 + {2}^{x} \)

\( \therefore x = {\log }_{2}\left( {y - 1}\right) \)

\( \therefore {f}^{-1}\left( x\right)  = {\log }_{2}\left( {x - 1}\right) \) .

6. 如图,在正四棱柱 \( {ABCD} - {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 中,底面 \( {ABCD} \) 的边长为 \( 3, B{D}_{1} \) 与底面所成角的大小为 \( \arcta![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_215_262_220_487_361_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_215_262_220_487_361_0.jpg)39b5b00_215_262_220_487_361_0.jpg)

【答案】 \( 2\sqrt{2} \)

\( {BD} = 3\sqrt{2},\;D{D}_{1} = {BD} \cdot  \frac{2}{3} = 2\sqrt{2}. \)

7. 方程 \( 3\sin x = 1 + \cos {2x} \) 在区间 \( \left\lbrack  {0,{2\pi }}\right\rbrack \) 上的解为___.

【答案】 \( x = \frac{\pi }{6},\;x = \frac{5\pi }{6} \)

\( 3\sin x = 2 - 2{\sin }^{2}x \) ,即 \( 2{\sin }^{2}x + 3\sin x - 2 = 0 \)

\( \therefore \left( {2\sin x - 1}\right) \left( {\sin x + 2}\right)  = 0 \)

\( \therefore \sin x = \frac{1}{2} \)

\( \therefore x = \frac{\pi }{6},\frac{5\pi }{6} \) .

8. 在 \( {\left( \sqrt[3]{x} - \frac{2}{x}\right) }^{n} \) 的二项式中，所有项的二项式系数之和为 256，则常数项等于___.

【答案】 112

\( {2}^{n} = {256},\;n = 8 \)

通项 \( {C}_{8}^{r} \cdot  {x}^{\frac{8 - r}{3}} \cdot  {\left( -\frac{2}{x}\right) }^{r} = {C}_{8}^{r}{\left( -2\right) }^{r} \cdot  {x}^{\frac{8 - {4r}}{3}} \)

取 \( r = 2 \)

常数项为 \( {C}_{8}^{2}{\left( -2\right) }^{2} = {112} \) .

9. 已知 \( {ABC} \) 的三边长为3，5，7，则该三角形的外接圆半径等于___.

【答案】 \( \frac{7\sqrt{3}}{3} \)

\( a = 3,\;b = 5,\;c = 7,\;\cos C = \frac{{a}^{2} + {b}^{2} - {c}^{2}}{2ab} =  - \frac{1}{2} \)

\( \therefore \sin C = \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \)

\( \therefore R = \frac{c}{2\sin C} = \frac{7\sqrt{3}}{3} \) .

10. 设 \( a > 0, b > 0 \) ,若关于 \( x, y \) 的方程组 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {ax} + y = 1 \\  x + {by} = 1 \end{array}\right. \) 无解,则 \( a + b \) 的取值范围是___.

【答案】 \( \left( {2, + \infty }\right) \)

由已知, \( {ab} = 1 \) ,且 \( a \neq  b,\therefore a + b > 2\sqrt{ab} = 2 \) .

11. 无穷数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 由 \( k \) 个不同的数组成, \( {S}_{n} \) 为 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的前 \( n \) 项和,若对任意 \( n \in  {N}^{ * },{S}_{n} \in \; \{ 2,3\} \) ，则 \( k \) 的最大值为___.

## 【答案】 4

当 \( n = 1 \) 时， \( {a}_{1} = 2 \) 或 \( {a}_{1} = 3 \) ；

当 \( {n2} \) 时,若 \( {S}_{n} = 2 \) ,则 \( {S}_{n - 1} = 2 \) ,于是 \( {a}_{n} = 0 \) ,

若 \( {S}_{n} = 3 \) ,则 \( {S}_{n - 1} = 3 \) ,于是 \( {a}_{n} = 0 \) . 从而存在 \( k \in  {N}^{ * } \) ,

当 \( {nk} \) 时， \( {a}_{k} = 0 \) . 其中数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}   : 2,1, - 1,0,0,\cdots \) 满足条件，

所以 \( {k}_{\max } = 4 \) .

12. 在平面直角坐标系中,已知 \( A\left( {1,0}\right) , B\left( {0, - 1}\right) , P \) 是曲线 \( y = \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}} \) 上一个动点,则 \( \overrightarrow{BP} \cdot  \overrightarrow{BA} \) 的取值范围是___.

【答案】 \( \left\lbrack  {0,1 + \sqrt{2}}\right\rbrack \)

设 \( P\left( {\cos \alpha ,\sin \alpha }\right) ,\;\alpha  \in  \left\lbrack  {0,\pi }\right\rbrack  ,\;\overrightarrow{BA} = \left( {1,1}\right) ,\;\overrightarrow{BP} = \left( {\cos \alpha ,\sin \alpha  + 1}\right) \) ,

\( \overrightarrow{BP} \cdot  \overrightarrow{BA} = \cos \alpha  + \sin \alpha  + 1 = \sqrt{2}\sin \left( {\alpha  + \frac{\pi }{4}}\right)  + 1 \in  \left\lbrack  {0,1 + \sqrt{2}}\right\rbrack  . \)

13. 设 \( a, b \in  R, c \in  \lbrack 0,{2\pi }) \) ,若对任意实数 \( x \) 都有 \( 2\sin \left( {{3x} - \frac{\pi }{3}}\right)  = a\sin \left( {{bx} + c}\right) \) ,则满足条件的有序实数 \( \left( {a, b, c}\right) \) 的组数为___.

## 【答案】 4

(i) 若 \( a = 2 \) ,若 \( b = 3 \) ,则 \( c = \frac{5\pi }{3} \) ; 若 \( b =  - 3 \) ,则 \( c = \frac{4\pi }{3} \) ,

(ii) 若 \( a =  - 2 \) ,若 \( b =  - 3 \) ,则 \( c = \frac{\pi }{3} \) ; 若 \( b = 3 \) ,则 \( c = \frac{2\pi }{3} \) ,

共 4 组.

14. 如图,在平面直角坐标系 \( {xOy} \) 中, \( O \) 为正八边形 \( {A}_{1}{A}_{2}\cdots {A}_{8} \) 的中心, \( {A}_{1}\left( {1,0}\right) \) ,任取不同的两点 \( {A}_{i},{A}_{j} \) ,点 \( P \) 满足 \( \overrightarrow{OP} + \overrightarrow{O{A}_{i}} + \overrightarrow{O{A}_{j}} = \overrightarrow{![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_217_262_1548_503_499_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_217_262_1548_503_499_0.jpg)9b5b00_217_262_1548_503_499_0.jpg)

【答案】 \( \frac{5}{28} \)

\( \frac{5}{{C}_{8}^{2}} = \frac{5}{28} \)

选择

15. 设 \( a \in  R \) ,则 “ \( a > 1 \) ” 是 “ \( {a}^{2} > 1 \) ” 的 ( ).

A. 充分非必要条件 B. 必要非充分条件

C. 充要条件 D. 既非充分也非必要条件

【答案】 \( A \)

由 \( {a}^{2} > 1 \) 得 \( a > 1 \) 或 \( a <  - 1 \) ,

即 “ \( a > 1 \) ” 是 “ \( {a}^{2} > 1 \) ” 的充分不必要条件.

故选 \( A \)![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_218_269_1402_530_421_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_218_269_1402_530_421_0.jpg)9b5b00_218_269_1402_530_421_0.jpg)

A. \( \rho  = 6 + 5\cos \theta \) B. \( \rho  = 6 + 5\sin \theta \) C. \( \rho  = 6 - 5\cos \theta \) D. \( \rho  = 6 - 5\sin \theta \)

【答案】 \( D \)

\( \theta  =  - \frac{\pi }{2} \) 时, \( \rho \) 达到最大.

17. 已知无穷等比数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的公比为 \( q \) ,前 \( n \) 项和为 \( {S}_{n} \) ,且 \( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{S}_{n} = S \) ,下列条件中,使得 \( 2{S}_{n} \; < S\left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) 恒成立的是 ( ).

A. \( {a}_{1} > 0,\;{0.6} < q < {0.7} \) B. \( {a}_{1} < 0,\; - {0.7} < q <  - {0.6} \)

C. \( {a}_{1} > 0,\;{0.7} < q < {0.8} \) D. \( {a}_{1} < 0,\; - {0.8} < q <  - {0.7} \)

## 【答案】 \( B \)

\( {S}_{n} = \frac{{a}_{1}\left( {1 - {q}^{n}}\right) }{1 - q},\;S = \frac{{a}_{1}}{1 - q},\; - 1 < q < 1, \)

\( 2{S}_{n} < S \) ,即 \( {a}_{1}\left( {2{q}^{n} - 1}\right)  > 0 \) ,

若 \( {a}_{1} > 0 \) ,则 \( {q}^{n} > \frac{1}{2} \) ,不可能成立,

若 \( {a}_{1} < 0 \) ,则 \( {q}^{n} < \frac{1}{2}, B \) 成立.

18. 设 \( f\left( x\right) , g\left( x\right) , h\left( x\right) \) 是定义域为 \( R \) 的三个函数,对于命题: ①若 \( f\left( x\right)  + g\left( x\right) , f\left( x\right)  + \; h\left( x\right) , g\left( x\right)  + h\left( x\right) \) 均为增函数,则 \( f\left( x\right) , g\left( x\right) , h\left( x\right) \) 中至少有一个为增函数; ②若 \( f\left( x\right) \; + g\left( x\right) , f\left( x\right)  + h\left( x\right) , g\left( x\right)  + h\left( x\right) \) 均是以 \( T \) 为周期的函数,则 \( f\left( x\right) , g\left( x\right) , h\left( x\right) \) 均是以 \( T \) 为周期的函数,下列判断正确的是 ( ).

A. ①和②均为真命题 B. ①和②均为假命题

C. ①为真命题，②为假命题 D. ①为假命题，②为真命题

## 【答案】 \( D \)

①不成立，可举反例

\( f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  {\begin{array}{ll} {2x}, & x \leq  1 \\   - x + 3, & x > 1 \end{array},\;g\left( x\right)  = \left\{  {\begin{array}{ll} {2x} + 3, & x \leq  0 \\   - x + 3, & 0 < x < 1 \\  {2x}, & x \geq  1 \end{array},\;h\left( x\right)  = \left\{  {\begin{array}{ll}  - x, & x \leq  0 \\  {2x}, & x > 0 \end{array},}\right. }\right. }\right. \)

② \( f\left( x\right)  + g\left( x\right)  = f\left( {x + T}\right)  + g\left( {x + T}\right) \) ，

\( f\left( x\right)  + h\left( x\right)  = f\left( {x + T}\right)  + h\left( {x + T}\right) , \)

\( g\left( x\right)  + h\left( x\right)  = g\left( {x + T}\right)  + h\left( {x + T}\right) , \)

前两式作差,可得 \( g\left( x\right)  - h\left( x\right)  = g\left( {x + T}\right)  - h\left( {x + T}\right) \) ,

结合第三式,可得 \( g\left( x\right)  = g\left( {x + T}\right) ,\;h\left( x\right)  = h\left( {x + T}\right) \) ,

也有 \( f\left( x\right)  = f\left( {x + T}\right) \) ,

\( \therefore \) ②正确.

故选 \( D \) .

【解析】答

19. 将边长为 1 的正方形 \( A{A}_{1}{O}_{1}O \) (及其内部) 绕 \( O{O}_{1} \) 旋转一周形成圆柱,如图, \( - {AC} \) 长为 \( \frac{2}{3}\pi , - {A}_{1}{B}_{1} \) 长为 \( \frac{\pi }{3} \) ,其中 \( {B}_{1} \) 与 \( C \)![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_220_283_789_428_507_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_220_283_789_428_507_0.jpg)39b5b00_220_283_789_428_507_0.jpg)

(1)求三棱锥 \( C - {O}_{1}{A}_{1}{B}_{1} \) 的体积;

【答案】 \( \frac{\sqrt{3}}{12} \) .

连 \( {O}_{1}{B}_{1} \) ,则 \( - {A}_{1}{B}_{1} = \angle {A}_{1}{O}_{1}{B}_{1} = \frac{\pi }{3} \) ,

\( \therefore {O}_{1}{A}_{1}{B}_{1} \) 为正三角形,

\( \therefore {S}_{{O}_{1}{A}_{1}{B}_{1}} = \frac{\sqrt{3}}{4} \) ,

\( \therefore {V}_{C - {O}_{1}{A}_{1}{B}_{1}} = \frac{1}{3}O{O}_{1} \cdot  {S}_{{O}_{1}{A}_{1}{B}_{1}} = \frac{\sqrt{3}}{12} \) .

(2)求异面直线 \( {B}_{1}C \) 与 \( A{A}_{1} \) 所成角的大小.

\( {45}^{ \circ  } \) .

设点 \( {B}_{1} \) 在下底面圆周的射影为 \( B \) ,连 \( B{B}_{1} \) ,则 \( B{B}_{1}//A{A}_{1} \) ,

\( \therefore \angle B{B}_{1}C \) 为直线 \( {B}_{1}C \) 与 \( A{A}_{1} \) 所成角 (或补角),

\( B{B}_{1} = A{A}_{1} = 1, \)

连 \( {BC},{BO},{OC} \) ,

\( - {AB} =  - {A}_{1}{B}_{1} = \frac{\pi }{3},\; - {AC} = \frac{2\pi }{3}, \)

\( \therefore  - {BC} = \frac{\pi }{3} \) ,

\( \therefore \angle {BOC} = \frac{\pi }{3} \) ,

\( \therefore {BOC} \) 为正三角形,

\( \therefore {BC} = {BO} = 1 \) ,

\( \therefore \tan \angle B{B}_{1}C = \frac{BC}{B{B}_{1}} = 1 \) ,

\( \therefore \angle B{B}_{1}C = {45}^{ \circ  } \) ,

\( \therefore \) 直线 \( {B}_{1}C \) 与 \( A{A}_{1} \) 所成角大小为 \( {45}^{ \circ  } \) .

20. 有一块正方形菜地 EFGH， \( {EH} \) 所在直线是一条小河，收货的蔬菜可送到 \( F \) 点或河边运走. 于是,菜地分为两个区域 \( {S}_{1} \) 和 \( {S}_{2} \) ,其中 \( {S}_{1} \) 中的蔬菜运到河边较近, \( {S}_{2} \) 中的蔬菜运到 \( F \) 点较近,而菜地内 \( {S}_{1} \) 和 \( {S}_{2} \) 的分界线 \( C \) 上的点到河边与到 \( F \) 点的距离相等,现建立平面直角坐标系,其中原点 \( O \) 为 \( {EF} \) 的中点,点 \( F \) 的坐![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_221_268_1116_418_373_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_221_268_1116_418_373_0.jpg)9b5b00_221_268_1116_418_373_0.jpg)

(1)求菜地内的分界线 \( C \) 的方程；

【答案】 \( y = 2\sqrt{x}\left( {0 \leq  x \leq  1}\right) \)

设分界线上任一点为 \( \left( {x, y}\right) \) ,依题意

\[
\left| {x + 1}\right|  = \sqrt{{\left( x - 1\right) }^{2} + {y}^{2}},
\]

可得 \( y = 2\sqrt{x}\left( {0 \leq  x \leq  1}\right) \) .

(2)菜农从蔬菜运量估计出 \( {S}_{1} \) 面积是 \( {S}_{2} \) 面积的两倍，由此得到 \( {S}_{1} \) 面积的 “经验值” 为 \( \frac{8}{3} \) . 设 \( M \) 是 \( C \) 上纵坐标为 1 的点,请计算以 \( {EH} \) 为一边,另一边过点 \( M \) 的矩形的面积,及五边形 \( {EOMGH} \) 的面积,并判断哪一个更接近于 \( {S}_{1} \) 面积的经验值.

五边形 \( {EOMGH} \) 的面积更接近 \( {S}_{1} \) 的面积.

设 \( M\left( {{x}_{0},{y}_{0}}\right) \) ,则 \( {y}_{0} = 1 \) ,

\( \therefore {x}_{0} = \frac{{y}_{0}^{2}}{4} = \frac{1}{4} \) ,

\( \therefore \) 设所表述的矩形面积为 \( {S}_{3} \) ,则 \( {S}_{3} = 2 \times  \left( {\frac{1}{4} + 1}\right)  = \frac{5}{2} \) ,

设五边形 \( {EMOGH} \) 面积为 \( {S}_{4} \) ,

则 \( {S}_{4} = {S}_{3} - {S}_{OMP} + {S}_{MGQ} = \frac{5}{2} - \frac{1}{2} \times  \frac{1}{4} \times  1 + \frac{1}{2} \times  \frac{3}{4} \times  1 = \frac{11}{4} \) ,

\( {S}_{1} - {S}_{3} = \frac{8}{3} - \frac{5}{2} = \frac{1}{6},\;{S}_{4} - {S}_{1} = \frac{11}{4} - \frac{8}{3} = \frac{1}{12} < \frac{1}{6}, \)

\( \therefore \) 五边形 \( {EOMGH} \) 的面积更接近 \( {S}_{1} \) 的面积.

21. 双曲线 \( {x}^{2} - \frac{{y}^{2}}{{b}^{2}} = 1\left( {b0}\right) \) 的左、右焦点分别为 \( {F}_{1}\text{ 、 }{F}_{2} \) ,直线 \( l \) 过 \( {F}_{2} \) 且与双曲线交于 \( A, B \) 两点

(1)若 \( l \) 的倾斜角为 \( \frac{\pi }{2} \) ， \( {F}_{1}{AB} \) 是等边三角形，求双曲线的渐近线方程；

【答案】 \( y =  \pm  \sqrt{2}x \) .

由已知 \( {F}_{1}\left( {-\sqrt{{b}^{2} + 1},0}\right) ,{F}_{2}\left( {\sqrt{{b}^{2} + 1},0}\right) \) ,

取 \( x = \sqrt{{b}^{2} + 1} \) ,得 \( y = {b}^{2} \) ,

\( \left| {{F}_{1}{F}_{2}}\right|  = \sqrt{3}\left| {{F}_{2}A}\right| \)

\( \because \left| {{F}_{1}{F}_{2}}\right|  = 2\sqrt{{b}^{2} + 1},\;\left| {{F}_{2}A}\right|  = {b}^{2}, \)

\( \therefore 2\sqrt{{b}^{2} + 1} = \sqrt{3}{b}^{2} \) ,

即 \( 3{b}^{4} - 4{b}^{2} - 4 = \left( {3{b}^{2} + 2}\right) \left( {{b}^{2} - 2}\right)  = 0 \) ,

\( \therefore b = \sqrt{2} \) ,

\( \therefore \) 渐近线方程为 \( y =  \pm  \sqrt{2}x \) .

(2) 设 \( b = \sqrt{3} \) ,若 \( l \) 的斜率存在,且 \( \left( {\overrightarrow{{F}_{1}A} + \overrightarrow{{F}_{1}B}}\right)  \cdot  \overrightarrow{AB} = 0 \) ,求 \( l \) 的斜率.

\( \pm  \frac{\sqrt{15}}{5}. \)

若 \( b = \sqrt{3} \) ,则双曲线为 \( {x}^{2} - \frac{{y}^{2}}{3} = 1 \) ,

\( \therefore {F}_{1}\left( {-2,0}\right) ,\;{F}_{2}\left( {2,0}\right) \) ,

设 \( A\left( {{x}_{1},{y}_{1}}\right) ,\;B\left( {{x}_{2},{y}_{2}}\right) \) ,则

\( \overrightarrow{{F}_{1}A} = \left( {{x}_{1} + 2,{y}_{1}}\right) ,\;\overrightarrow{{F}_{1}B} = \left( {{x}_{2} + 2,{y}_{2}}\right) ,\;\overrightarrow{AB} = \left( {{x}_{2} - {x}_{1},{y}_{2} - {y}_{1}}\right) , \)

\( \therefore \overrightarrow{{F}_{1}A} + \overrightarrow{{F}_{1}B} = \left( {{x}_{1} + {x}_{2} + 4,{y}_{1} + {y}_{2}}\right) \) ,

\( \left( {\overrightarrow{{F}_{1}A} + \overrightarrow{{F}_{1}B}}\right)  \cdot  \overrightarrow{AB} = {x}_{2}^{2} - {x}_{1}^{2} + 4\left( {{x}_{2} - {x}_{1}}\right)  + {y}_{2}^{2} - {y}_{1}^{2} = 0 \) (*),

\( \because {x}_{1}^{2} - \frac{{y}_{1}^{2}}{3} = {x}_{2}^{2} - \frac{{y}_{2}^{2}}{3} = 1 \) ,

\( \therefore {y}_{2}^{2} - {y}_{1}^{2} = 3\left( {{x}_{2}^{2} - {x}_{1}^{2}}\right) \) ,

\( \therefore \) 代入 (*) 式,可得 \( 4\left( {{x}_{2}^{2} - {x}_{1}^{2}}\right)  + 4\left( {{x}_{2} - {x}_{1}}\right)  = 0 \) ,

直线 \( l \) 的斜率存在,故 \( {x}_{1} \neq  {x}_{2} \) ,

\( \therefore {x}_{1} + {x}_{2} =  - 1 \) ,

设直线 \( l \) 为 \( y = k\left( {x - 2}\right) \) ,代入 \( 3{x}^{2} - {y}^{2} = 3 \) ,

得 \( \left( {3 - {k}^{2}}\right) {x}^{2} + 4{k}^{2}x - \left( {4{k}^{2} + 3}\right)  = 0 \) ,

\( \therefore 3 - {k}^{2} \neq  0 \) ,且 \( \Delta  = {16}{k}^{4} + 4\left( {3 - {k}^{2}}\right) \left( {4{k}^{2} + 3}\right)  = {36}\left( {{k}^{2} + 1}\right)  > 0 \) ,

\( {x}_{1} + {x}_{2} =  - \frac{4{k}^{2}}{3 - {k}^{2}} =  - 1, \)

\( \therefore {k}^{2} = \frac{3}{5} \) ,

\( \therefore k =  \pm  \frac{\sqrt{15}}{5} \) ,

\( \therefore \) 直线 \( l \) 的斜率为 \( \pm  \frac{\sqrt{15}}{5} \) .

22. 已知 \( a \in  R \) ,函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = {\log }_{2}\left( {\frac{1}{x} + a}\right) \)

(1)当 \( a = 5 \) 时，解不等式 \( f\left( x\right)  > 0 \) ；

【答案】 \( \{ x \mid  {x0} \) 或 \( x <  - \frac{1}{4}\} \) .

\( {\log }_{2}\left( {\frac{1}{x} + 5}\right)  > 0 \Leftrightarrow  \frac{1}{x} + 5 > 1 \Leftrightarrow  \frac{{4x} + 1}{x} > 0 \Leftrightarrow  x\left( {{4x} + 1}\right)  > 0 \) ,

\( \therefore \) 不等式的解为 \( \left\{  {x \mid  {x0}}\right. \) 或 \( \left. {x <  - \frac{1}{4}}\right\} \) .

( 2 )若关于 \( x \) 的方程 \( f\left( x\right)  - {\log }_{2}\left\lbrack  {\left( {a - 4}\right) x + {2a} - 5}\right\rbrack   = 0 \) 的解集中恰有一个元素，求 \( a \) 的取值范围;

\( 1 < a \leq  2 \) 或 \( a = 3 \) 或 \( a = 4 \) .

依题意, \( {\log }_{2}\left( {\frac{1}{x} + a}\right)  = {\log }_{2}\left\lbrack  {\left( {a - 4}\right) x + {2a} - 5}\right\rbrack \) ,

\( \therefore \frac{1}{x} + a = \left( {a - 4}\right) x + {2a} - 5 > 0 \) ①

可得 \( \left( {a - 4}\right) {x}^{2} + \left( {a - 5}\right) x - 1 = 0 \)

即 \( \left( {x + 1}\right) \left\lbrack  {\left( {a - 4}\right) x - 1}\right\rbrack   = 0 \) ②

当 \( a = 4 \) 时,方程②的解为 \( x =  - 1 \) ,代入①式，成立，

当 \( a = 3 \) 时,方程②的解为 \( x =  - 1 \) ,代入①式，成立，

当 \( a \neq  3 \) 且 \( a \neq  4 \) 时,方程②的解为 \( x =  - 1,\frac{1}{a - 4} \) ,

若 \( x =  - 1 \) 为方程①的解,则 \( \frac{1}{x} + a = a - 1 > 0 \) ,即 \( a > 1 \) .

若 \( x = \frac{1}{a - 4} \) 为方程①的解,则 \( \frac{1}{x} + a = {2a} - 4 > 0 \) ,即 \( a > 2 \) .

要使得方程①有且仅有一个解，则 \( 1 < a \leq  2 \) .

综上,若原方程的解集有且只有一个元素,则 \( a \) 的取值范围为 \( 1 < a \leq  2 \) 或 \( a = 3 \) 或 \( a = 4 \) .

(3) 设 \( a > 0 \) ,若对任意 \( t \in  \left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{2},1}\right\rbrack \) ,函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 在区间 \( \left\lbrack  {t, t + 1}\right\rbrack \) 上的最大值和最小值的差不超过

1,求 \( a \) 的取值范围.

【答案】 \( a \geq  \frac{2}{3} \) .

\( f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( \left\lbrack  {t, t + 1}\right\rbrack \) 上单调递减

依题意, \( f\left( t\right)  - f\left( {t + 1}\right)  \leq  1 \) ,

即 \( {\log }_{2}\left( {\frac{1}{t} + a}\right)  - {\log }_{2}\left( {\frac{1}{t + 1} + a}\right)  \leq  1 \) ,

\( \therefore \frac{1}{t} + a \leq  2\left( {\frac{1}{t + 1} + a}\right) \) ,即 \( a \geq  \frac{1}{t} - \frac{2}{t + 1} = \frac{1 - t}{t\left( {t + 1}\right) } \) .

设 \( 1 - t = r \) ,则 \( r \in  \left\lbrack  {0,\frac{1}{2}}\right\rbrack \) .

\( \frac{1 - t}{t\left( {t + 1}\right) } = \frac{r}{\left( {1 - r}\right) \left( {2 - r}\right) } = \frac{r}{{r}^{2} - {3r} + 2}, \)

当 \( r = 0 \) 时, \( \frac{r}{{r}^{2} - {3r} + 2} = 0 \) ,

当 \( 0 < r \leq  \frac{1}{2} \) 时, \( \frac{r}{{r}^{2} - {3r} + 2} = \frac{1}{r + \frac{2}{r} - 3} \) ,

\( \because \) 函数 \( y = x + \frac{2}{x} \) 在 \( \left( {0,\sqrt{2}}\right) \) 递减,

\( \therefore r + \frac{2}{r} \geq  \frac{1}{2} + 4 = \frac{9}{2} \) ,

\( \therefore \frac{1}{r + \frac{2}{r} - 3} \leq  \frac{1}{\frac{9}{2} - 3} = \frac{2}{3} \) ,

\( \therefore a \) 的取值范围为 \( a \geq  \frac{2}{3} \) .

23. 若无穷数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 满足: 只要 \( {a}_{p} = {a}_{q}\left( {p, q \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) ,必有 \( {a}_{p + 1} = {a}_{q + 1} \) ,则称 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 具有性质 \( P \) .

(1)若 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 具有性质 \( P \) . 且 \( {a}_{1} = 1,{a}_{2} = 2,{a}_{4} = 3,{a}_{5} = 2,{a}_{6} + {a}_{7} + {a}_{8} = {21} \) ，求 \( {a}_{3} \) .

【答案】 \( {a}_{3} = {16} \) .

\[
{a}_{2} = {a}_{5} = 2,
\]

\[
\therefore {a}_{3} = {a}_{6}\text{ , }
\]

\[
\therefore {a}_{4} = {a}_{7} = 3\text{ , }
\]

\[
\therefore {a}_{5} = {a}_{8} = 2\text{ , }
\]

\[
\therefore {a}_{6} = {21} - {a}_{7} - {a}_{8} = {16}\text{ , }
\]

\[
\therefore {a}_{3} = {16}\text{ . }
\]

( 2 )若无穷数列 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 是等差数列，无穷数列 \( \left\{  {c}_{n}\right\} \) 是公比为正数的等比数列， \( {b}_{1} = {c}_{5} \; = 1,{b}_{5} = {c}_{1} = {81},{a}_{n} = {b}_{n} + {c}_{n} \) ,判断 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 是否具有性质 \( P \) ,并说明理由.

不具有性质 \( P \) ,理由见解析.

设 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 的公差为 \( d,\left\{  {c}_{n}\right\} \) 的公差为 \( q \) ,则 \( q > 0 \) .

\( {b}_{5} - {b}_{1} = {4d} = {80}, \)

\( \therefore d = {20} \) ,

\( \therefore {b}_{n} = {20n} - {19} \) ,

\( \frac{{c}_{5}}{{c}_{1}} = {q}^{4} = \frac{1}{81}, \)

\[
\therefore q = \frac{1}{3},
\]

\( \therefore {c}_{n} = {\left( \frac{1}{3}\right) }^{n - 5} \) ,

\( \therefore {a}_{n} = {b}_{n} + {c}_{n} = {20n} - {19} + {\left( \frac{1}{3}\right) }^{n - 5} \) ,

\( \because {a}_{1} = {82},\;{a}_{5} = {82}, \)

而 \( {a}_{2} = {21} + {27} = {48},\;{a}_{6} = {101} + \frac{1}{3} = \frac{304}{3} \) .

\( {a}_{1} = {a}_{5} \) 但 \( {a}_{2} \neq  {a}_{6} \) ,

故 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 不具有性质 \( P \) .

(3)设 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 是无穷数列，已知 \( {a}_{n + 1} = {b}_{n} + \sin {a}_{n}\left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) ，求证:“对任意 \( {a}_{1} \) ， \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 都具有性质 \( P \) ” 的充要条件为 “ \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 是常数列”.

【答案】证明见解析.

充分性: 若 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 为常数列,设 \( {b}_{n} = C \) ,

则 \( {a}_{n + 1} = C + \sin {a}_{n} \) ,

若存在 \( p, q \) 使得 \( {a}_{p} = {a}_{q} \) ,

则 \( {a}_{p + 1} = C + \sin {a}_{p} = C + \sin {a}_{q} = {a}_{q + 1} \) ,

故 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 具有性质 \( P \) .

必要性: 若对任意 \( {a}_{1},\left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 具有性质 \( P \) ,

则 \( {a}_{2} = {b}_{1} + \sin {a}_{1} \) ,

设函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = x - {b}_{1},\;g\left( x\right)  = \sin x \) ,

由 \( f\left( x\right) \) ， \( g\left( x\right) \) 图像可得，对任意的 \( {b}_{1} \) ，二者图像必有一个交点，

\( \therefore \) 一定能找到一个 \( {a}_{1} \) ,使得 \( {a}_{1} - {b}_{1} = \sin {a}_{1} \) ,

\( \therefore {a}_{2} = {b}_{1} + \sin {a}_{1} = {a}_{1} \) ,

\( \therefore {a}_{n} = {a}_{n + 1} \) ,

故 \( {b}_{n + 1} = {a}_{n + 2} - \sin {a}_{n + 1} = {a}_{n + 1} - \sin {a}_{n} = {b}_{n} \) ,

\( \therefore \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 是常数列.

## 2017 秋考

## 填空

1. 已知集合 \( A = \{ 1,2,3,4\} \) ，集合 \( B = \{ 3,4,5\} \) ，则 \( A \cap  B = \) ___.

【答案】 \( \{ 3,4\} \)

\( A \cap  B = \{ 3,4\} \) .

2. 若排列数 \( {A}_{6}^{m} = 6 \times  5 \times  4 \) ，则 \( m = \) ___

【答案】 3

\( {A}_{n}^{m} = n \times  \left( {n - 1}\right)  \times  \cdots  \times  \left( {n - m + 1}\right) \) ,所以 \( 6 - m + 1 = 4 \) ,所以 \( m = 3 \) .

3. 不等式 \( \frac{x - 1}{x} > 1 \) 的解集为___

【答案】 \( \{ x \mid  x < 0\} \)

\( 1 - \frac{1}{x} > 1 \Rightarrow  \frac{1}{x} < 0 \Rightarrow  x < 0 \) ,解集为 \( \left( {-\infty ,0}\right) \) .

4. 已知球的体积为 \( {36\pi } \) ，则该球主视图的面积等于___.

【答案】 \( {9\pi } \)

\[
\frac{4}{3}\pi {r}^{3} = {36\pi } \Rightarrow  r = 3 \Rightarrow  S = {9\pi }.
\]

5. 已知复数 \( z \) 满足 \( z + \frac{3}{z} = 0 \) ,则 \( \left| z\right|  = \) ___

【答案】 \( \sqrt{3} \)

\[
z + \frac{3}{z} = 0 \Rightarrow  \frac{{z}^{2} + 3}{z} = 0 \Rightarrow  {z}^{2} =  - 3 \Rightarrow  z =  \pm  \sqrt{3}\mathrm{i} \Rightarrow  \left| z\right|  = \sqrt{3}.
\]

6. 设双曲线 \( \frac{{x}^{2}}{9} - \frac{{y}^{2}}{{b}^{2}} = 1\left( {b0}\right) \) 的焦点为 \( {F}_{1}\text{ 、 }{F}_{2}, P \) 为该双曲线上的一点,若 \( \left| {P{F}_{1}}\right|  = 5 \) ,则 \( \left| {P{F}_{2}}\right|  = \) ___

【答案】 11

\[
\left| {P{F}_{1}}\right|  + \left| {P{F}_{2}}\right|  = {2a} = 6 \Rightarrow  \left| {P{F}_{2}}\right|  = {11}.
\]

7. 如图,以长方体 \( {ABCD} - {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 的顶点 \( D \) 为坐标原点,过 \( D \) 的三条棱所在的直线为坐标轴,建立空间直角坐标系,若 \( \overrightarrow{D{B}_{1}} \) 的坐标为 \( \left( {4,3,2}\right) \) ,则 \( \ove![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_228_278_238_383_303_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_228_278_238_383_303_0.jpg)39b5b00_228_278_238_383_303_0.jpg)

【答案】 \( \left( {-4,3,2}\right) \)

\( A\left( {4,0,0}\right) ,\;{C}_{1}\left( {0,3,2}\right) ,\;\overrightarrow{A{C}_{1}} = \left( {-4,3,2}\right) . \)

8. 定义在 \( \left( {0, + \infty }\right) \) 上的函数 \( y = f\left( x\right) \) 的反函数为 \( y = {f}^{-1}\left( x\right) \) ,若 \( g\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} {3}^{x} - 1 & x \leq  0 \\  f\left( x\right) & x > 0 \end{array}\right. \) 为奇函数,则 \( {f}^{-1}\left( x\right)  = 2 \) 的解为___

【答案】 \( x = \frac{8}{9} \)

\( f\left( 2\right)  =  - f\left( {-2}\right)  = \frac{8}{9}, \)

\( \therefore {f}^{-1}\left( x\right)  = 2 \) 的解为 \( x = \frac{8}{9} \) .

9. 已知四个函数:① \( y =  - x \) ; ② \( y =  - \frac{1}{x} \) ; ③ \( y = {x}^{3} \) ；④ \( y = {x}^{\frac{1}{2}} \) . 从中任选 2 个，则事件 “所选 2 个函数的图像有且仅有一个公共点” 的概率为___

【答案】 \( \frac{1}{3} \)

①③、①④的图像有一个公共点，

\( \therefore \) 概率为 \( \frac{2}{{C}_{4}^{2}} = \frac{1}{3} \) .

10. 已知数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 和 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) ,其中 \( {a}_{n} = {n}^{2}, n \in  {N}^{ * },\left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 的项是互不相等的正整数,若对于任意 \( n \in  {N}^{ * },\left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 的第 \( {a}_{n} \) 项等于 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的第 \( {b}_{n} \) 项，则 \( \frac{\lg \left( {{b}_{1}{b}_{4}{b}_{9}{b}_{16}}\right) }{\lg \left( {{b}_{1}{b}_{2}{b}_{3}{b}_{4}}\right) } = \) ___

【答案】 2

\[
{b}_{{a}_{n}} = {a}_{{b}_{n}} \Rightarrow  {b}_{{n}^{2}} = {b}_{n}^{2} \Rightarrow  {b}_{1}{b}_{4}{b}_{9}{b}_{16} = {\left( {b}_{1}{b}_{2}{b}_{3}{b}_{4}\right) }^{2} \Rightarrow  \frac{\lg \left( {{b}_{1}{b}_{4}{b}_{9}{b}_{16}}\right) }{\lg \left( {{b}_{1}{b}_{2}{b}_{3}{b}_{4}}\right) } = 2.
\]

11. 设 \( {\alpha }_{1}\text{ 、 }{\alpha }_{2} \in  R \) ,且 \( \frac{1}{2 + \sin {\alpha }_{1}} + \frac{1}{2 + \sin \left( {2{\alpha }_{2}}\right) } = 2 \) ,则 \( \left| {{10\pi } - {\alpha }_{1} - {\alpha }_{2}}\right| \) 的最小值等于___

【答案】 \( \frac{\pi }{4} \)

\[
\frac{1}{2 + \sin {\alpha }_{1}} \in  \left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{3},1}\right\rbrack  ,\;\frac{1}{2 + \sin \left( {2{\alpha }_{2}}\right) } \in  \left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{3},1}\right\rbrack
\]

\[
\therefore \frac{1}{2 + \sin {\alpha }_{1}} = \frac{1}{2 + \sin \left( {2{\alpha }_{2}}\right) } = 1\text{ , }
\]

\[
\text{ 即 }\sin {\alpha }_{1} = \sin \left( {2{\alpha }_{2}}\right)  =  - 1\text{ , }
\]

\[
\therefore {\alpha }_{1} =  - \frac{\pi }{2} + {2k\pi },\;{\alpha }_{2} =  - \frac{\pi }{4} + {k\pi },
\]

\( {\left| {10}\pi  - {\alpha }_{1} - {\alpha }_{2}\right| }_{\min } = \frac{\pi }{4}. \)

12. 如图,用 35 个单位正方形拼成一个矩形,点 \( {P}_{1}\text{ 、 }{P}_{2}\text{ 、 }{P}_{3}\text{ 、 }{P}_{4} \) 以及四个标记为 “#” 的点在正方形的顶点处,设集合 \( \Omega  = \left\{  {{P}_{1},{P}_{2},{P}_{3},{P}_{4}}\right\} \) ,点 \( P \in  \Omega \) ,过 \( P \) 作直线 \( {l}_{P} \) ,使得不在 \( {l}_{P} \) 上的 “#” 的点分布在 \( {l}_{P} \) 的两侧. 用 \( {D}_{1}\left( {l}_{P}\right) \) 和 \( {D}_{2}\left( {l}_{P}\right) \) 分别表示 \( {l}_{P} \) 一侧和另一侧的 “#” 的点到 \( {l}_{P} \) 的距离之和. 若过 \( P \) 的直线 \( {l}_{P} \) 中有且只有一条满足 \( {D}_{1}\left( {l}_{P}\right)  = {D}_{2}\left( {l}_{P}\right) \) ,则 \![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_229_440_1788_332_252_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_229_440_1788_332_252_0.jpg)9b5b00_229_440_1788_332_252_0.jpg)

【答案】 \( {P}_{1},{P}_{3},{P}_{4} \)

设记为 “ \( \Delta \) ” 的四个点为 \( A, B, C, D \) ,

线段 \( {AB},{BC},{CD},{DA} \) 的中点分别为 \( E, F, G, H \) ,

易知 \( {EFGH} \) 为平行四边形,且 \( {EFGH} \) 对角线交点为 \( {P}_{2} \) ,

不妨记点 \( A, B, C, D, E, F, G, H \) 到直线 \( {l}_{P} \) 的距离为 \( h\left( A\right) \) ,

\( h\left( B\right) , \sim  h\left( C\right) ,\;h\left( D\right) ,\;h\left( E\right) ,\;h\left( F\right) ,\;h\left( G![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_230_408_463_500_390_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_230_408_463_500_390_0.jpg)39b5b00_230_408_463_500_390_0.jpg)

图 1

四个点不在 \( {l}_{P} \) 的同一侧,有两种可能:

(1)若 \( {l}_{P} \) 的两侧分别有二个点: 如图 1,点 \( A, B \) 和 \( C, D \) 分别在直线 \( {l}_{P} \) 的两侧, 若 \( h\left( A\right)  + h\left( B\right) h\left( C\right)  + h\left( D\right) \) ,则有 \( h\left( E\right)  = h\left( G\right) \) ,即 \( h\left( E\right) \) 和 \( h\left( G\right) \) 所在的线段平行且相等，

所以可构成相应的平行四边形,因此直线 \( {l}_{P} \) 必过 \( {EG} \) 的中点.

若点 \( A, D \) 和 \( B, C \) 分别在直线 \( {l}_{P} \) 的两侧,同理可知直线 \( {l}_{P} \) 必过 \( {FH} \) 的中点.

于是,直线 \( {l}_{P} \) 必过 \( {EFGH} \) 的对角线的交点 \( {P}_{2} \) .

( 2 )若 \( {l}_{P} \) 的一侧有三个点，另一侧有一个点:如图 2，点 \( B \) ， \( A \) ， \( D \) 和 \( C \) 分别在直线 \( {l}_{P} \) 的两侧，

若 \( h\left( A\right)  + h\left( B\right)  + h\left( D\right) h\left( C\right) \) ,

即 \( h\left( A\right)  +  \sim  h\left( D\right) h\left![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_230_815_1381_496_426_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_230_815_1381_496_426_0.jpg)9b5b00_230_815_1381_496_426_0.jpg)

由平面几何知识易得, \( h\left( A\right)  + h\left( D\right) {2h}\left( H\right) \) ,

且 \( h\left( C\right)  - h\left( B\right) {2h}\left( F\right) \) ,

则有 \( h\left( H\right)  = h\left( F\right) \) ,即 \( h\left( H\right) \) 和 \( h\left( F\right) \) 所在的线段平行且相等,

所以可构成相应的平行四边形,因此直线 \( {l}_{P} \) 必过 \( {FH} \) 的中点.

若点 \( A, D, C \) 和 \( B \) 分别在直线 \( {l}_{P} \) 的两侧,同理可知直线 \( {l}_{P} \) 必过 \( {EG} \) 的中点.

于是,直线 \( {l}_{P} \) 必过 \( {EFGH} \) 的对角线的交点 \( {P}_{2} \) .

综合以上两种情况,即满足已知条件的直线必然经过 \( {EG} \) 和 \( {FH} \) 的交点 \( {P}_{2} \) , 因此: 经过点 \( {P}_{2} \) 的直线有无数条; 同时经过点 \( {P}_{1} \) 和 \( {P}_{2} \) 的直线仅有一条; 同时经过点 \( {P}_{3} \) 和 \( {P}_{2} \) 的直线仅有一条; 同时经过点 \( {P}_{4} \) 和 \( {P}_{2} \) 的直线仅有一条; 所以符合条件的点为 \( {P}_{1},{P}_{3},{P}_{4} \) .

13. 关于 \( x\text{ 、 }y \) 的二元一次方程组 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} x + {5y} = 0 \\  {2x} + {3y} = 4 \end{array}\right. \) 的系数行列式 \( D \) 为( )

A. \( \left| \begin{array}{ll} 0 & 5 \\  4 & 3 \end{array}\right| \) B. \( \left| \begin{array}{ll} 1 & 0 \\  2 & 4 \end{array}\right| \) C. \( \left| \begin{array}{ll} 1 & 5 \\  2 & 3 \end{array}\right| \) D. \( \left| \begin{array}{ll} 6 & 0 \\  5 & 4 \end{array}\right| \)

## 【答案】 \( C \)

系数矩阵为 \( \left\lbrack  \begin{array}{ll} 1 & 5 \\  2 & 3 \end{array}\right\rbrack \) ,所以系数行列式为 \( \left| \begin{array}{ll} 1 & 5 \\  2 & 3 \end{array}\right| \) .

14. 在数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 中, \( {a}_{n} = {\left( -\frac{1}{2}\right) }^{n}, n \in  {N}^{ * } \) ,则 \( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n\infty }}{a}_{n} \) (   )

A. 等于 \( - \frac{1}{2} \) B. 等于 0 C. 等于 \( \frac{1}{2} \) D. 不存在

【答案】 \( B \)

当 \( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n\infty }}{\left( \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{n} = 0,\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n\infty }}{a}_{n} = 0 \) .

15. 已知 \( a\text{ 、 }b\text{ 、 }c \) 为实常数,数列 \( \left\{  {x}_{n}\right\} \) 的通项 \( {x}_{n} = a{n}^{2} + {bn} + c, n \in  {N}^{ * } \) ,则 “存在 \( k \in  {N}^{ * } \) , 使得 \( {x}_{{100} + k}\text{ 、 }{x}_{{200} + k}\text{ 、 }{x}_{{300} + k} \) 成等差数列” 的一个必要条件是 ( )

A. \( a \geq  0 \) B. \( b \leq  0 \) C. \( c = 0 \) D. \( a - {2b} + c = 0 \)

【答案】 \( A \)

由二次函数的图像可知,不可能 “存在 \( k \in  {N}^{ * } \) ,使得 \( {x}_{{100} + k}\text{ 、 }{x}_{{200} + k}\text{ 、 }{x}_{{300} + k} \) 成等差数列”,

所以若 “存在 \( k \in  {N}^{ * } \) ,使得 \( {x}_{{100} + k}\text{ 、 }{x}_{{200} + k}\text{ 、 }{x}_{{300} + k} \) 成等差数列”,则必然有 \( a = 0 \) , 故选 \( A \) .

16. 在平面直角坐标系 \( {xOy} \) 中,已知椭圆 \( {C}_{1} : \frac{{x}^{2}}{36} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{4} = 1 \) 和 \( {C}_{2} : {x}^{2} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{9} = 1.P \) 为 \( {C}_{1} \) 上的动点, \( Q \) 为 \( {C}_{2} \) 上的动点, \( w \) 是 \( \overrightarrow{OP} \cdot  \overrightarrow{OQ} \) 的最大值. 记 \( \Omega  = \{ \left( {P, Q}\right)  \mid  P \) 在 \( {C}_{1} \) 上, \( Q \) 在 \( {C}_{2} \) 上，且 \( \overrightarrow{OP} \cdot  \overrightarrow{OQ} = w \) ，则 \( \Omega \) 中元素个数为( )

A. 2 个 B. 4 个 C. 8 个 D. 无穷个

## 【答案】 \( D \)

设 \( P\left( {6\cos \alpha ,2\sin \alpha }\right) , Q\left( {\cos \beta ,3\sin \beta }\right) \) ,

则 \( w = \overrightarrow{OP} \cdot  \overrightarrow{OQ} = 6\left( {\cos \alpha \cos \beta  + \sin \alpha \sin \beta }\right)  = 6\cos \left( {\alpha  - \beta }\right)  \leq  6 \) ,

当等号当且仅当 \( \alpha  - \beta  = {2k\pi }\left( {k \in  Z}\right) \) 时成立,

\( \therefore \left( {P, Q}\right) \) 有无数个,故选 \( D \) .

17. 如图,直三棱柱 \( {ABC} - {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1} \) 的底面为直角三角形,两直角边 \( {AB} \) 和 \( {AC} \) 的长分别为 ![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_232_638_1599_247_274_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_232_638_1599_247_274_0.jpg)9b5b00_232_638_1599_247_274_0.jpg)

(1)求三棱柱 \( {ABC} - {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1} \) 的体积.

【答案】 20 .

\[
V = {Sh} = \frac{1}{2} \times  2 \times  4 \times  5 = {20}.
\]

(2)设 \( M \) 是 \( {BC} \) 中点，求直线 \( {A}_{1}M \) 与平面 \( {ABC} \) 所成角的大小.

【答案】 \( \arctan \sqrt{5} \) .

连接 \( {A}_{1}M,{AM} \) ,直三棱柱 \( {ABC} - {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1} \) 中 \( {A}_{1} \) 到底面![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_233_420_381_268_275_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_233_420_381_268_275_0.jpg)39b5b00_233_420_381_268_275_0.jpg)

则直线 \( {A}_{1}M \) 与平面 \( {ABC} \) 所成角的即为 \( \angle {A}_{1}{MA} \) .

由题意易知 \( {BC} = \sqrt{{2}^{2} + {4}^{2}} = 2\sqrt{5},{AM} = \frac{1}{2}{BC} = \sqrt{5} \) ,

所以 \( \tan \angle {A}_{1}{MA} = \frac{5}{\sqrt{5}} = \sqrt{5} \) ,

所以直线 \( {A}_{1}M \) 与平面 \( {ABC} \) 所成角为 \( \arctan \sqrt{5} \) .

18. 已知函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = {\cos }^{2}x - {\sin }^{2}x + \frac{1}{2}, x \in  \left( {0,\pi }\right) \) .

(1)求 \( f\left( x\right) \) 的单调递增区间.

【答案】 \( \left\lbrack  {\frac{\pi }{2},\pi }\right) \) .

\( f\left( x\right)  = \cos {2x} + \frac{1}{2},\;x \in  \left( {0,\pi }\right) \) ,单调递增区间为 \( \left\lbrack  {\frac{\pi }{2},\pi }\right) \) .

(2)设 \( {ABC} \) 为锐角三角形，角 \( A \) 所对边 \( a = \sqrt{19} \) ，角 \( B \) 所对边 \( b = 5 \) ，若 \( f\left( A\right)  = 0 \) ，求 \( {ABC} \) 的面积.

【答案】 \( \frac{15}{4}\sqrt{3} \)

\( \cos {2A} =  - \frac{1}{2} \Rightarrow  A = \frac{\pi }{3} \) ,

\( \therefore \cos A = \frac{{25} + {c}^{2} - {19}}{2 \cdot  5 \cdot  c} = \frac{1}{2} \Rightarrow  c = 2 \) 或 \( c = 3 \) ,

根据锐角三角形, \( \cos B > 0 \) ,

\( \therefore c = 3, S = \frac{1}{2}{bc}\sin A = \frac{15}{4}\sqrt{3} \) .

19. 根据预测,某地第 \( n\left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) 个月共享单车的投放量和损失量分别为 \( {a}_{n} \) 和 \( {b}_{n} \) (单位: 辆),其中 \( {a}_{n} = \left\{  {\begin{array}{ll} 5{n}^{4} + {15}, & 1 \leq  n \leq  3 \\   - {10n} + {470}, & n \geq  4 \end{array},\;{b}_{n} = n + 5}\right. \) ,第 \( n \) 个月底的共享单车的保有量是前 \( n \) 个月的累计投放量与累计损失量的差.

(1)求该地区第 4 个月底的共享单车的保有量.

【答案】 935.

\[
\left( {{a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + {a}_{3} + {a}_{4}}\right)  - \left( {{b}_{1} + {b}_{2} + {b}_{3} + {b}_{4}}\right)  = {965} - {30} = {935}.
\]

(2)已知该地共享单车停放点第 \( n \) 个月底的单车容纳量 \( {S}_{n} =  - 4{\left( n - {46}\right) }^{2} + {8800} \) (单位:辆). 设在某月底, 共享单车保有量达到最大, 问该保有量是否超出了此时停放点的单车容纳量?

【答案】保有量超过了容纳量.

\( - {10n} + {470} > n + 5 \Rightarrow  n \leq  {42} \) ,即第 42 个月底,保有量达到最大,

\[
\left( {{a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + {a}_{3} + \cdots  + {a}_{42}}\right)  - \left( {{b}_{1} + {b}_{2} + {b}_{3} + \cdots  + {b}_{42}}\right)
\]

\[
= \left\lbrack  {{965} + \frac{\left( {{420} + {50}}\right)  \times  {38}}{2}}\right\rbrack   - \frac{\left( {6 + {47}}\right)  \times  {42}}{2} = {8782},
\]

\[
{S}_{42} =  - 4{\left( {42} - {46}\right) }^{2} + {8800} = {8736},
\]

\( \therefore \) 此时保有量超过了容纳量.

20. 在平面直角坐标系 \( {xOy} \) 中,已知椭圆 \( \Gamma  : \frac{{x}^{2}}{4} + {y}^{2} = 1, A \) 为 \( \Gamma \) 的上顶点, \( P \) 为 \( \Gamma \) 上异于上、下顶点的动点, \( M \) 为 \( x \) 正半轴上的动点.

(1)若 \( P \) 在第一象限，且 \( \left| {OP}\right|  = \sqrt{2} \) ，求 \( P \) 的坐标.

【答案】 \( \left( {\frac{2\sqrt{3}}{3},\frac{\sqrt{6}}{3}}\right) \) .

联立 \( \Gamma  : \frac{{x}^{2}}{4} + {y}^{2} = 1 \) 与 \( {x}^{2} + {y}^{2} = 2 \) ,可得 \( P\left( {\frac{2\sqrt{3}}{3},\frac{\sqrt{6}}{3}}\right) \) .

( 2 )设 \( P\left( {\frac{8}{5},\frac{3}{5}}\right) \) ，若以 \( A \) 、 \( P \) 、 \( M \) 为顶点的三角形是直角三角形，求 \( M \) 的横坐标.

【答案】35,1, \( \frac{29}{20} \)

设 \( M\left( {m,0}\right) ,\overrightarrow{MA} \cdot  \overrightarrow{MP} = \left( {-m,1}\right)  \cdot  \left( {\frac{8}{5} - m,\frac{3}{5}}\right)  = {m}^{2} - \frac{8}{5}m + \frac{3}{5} = 0 \Rightarrow  m = \frac{3}{5} \) 或

\( m = 1, \)

\[
\overrightarrow{PA} \cdot  \overrightarrow{MP} = \left( {-\frac{8}{5},\frac{2}{5}}\right)  \cdot  \left( {\frac{8}{5} - m,\frac{3}{5}}\right)  = \frac{8}{5}m - \frac{64}{25} + \frac{6}{25} = 0 \Rightarrow  m = \frac{29}{20}.
\]

(3)若 \( \left| {MA}\right|  = \left| {MP}\right| \) ，直线 \( {AQ} \) 与 \( \Gamma \) 交于另一点 \( C \) ，且 \( \overrightarrow{AQ} = 2\overrightarrow{AC} \) ， \( \overrightarrow{PQ} = 4\overrightarrow{PM} \) ，求直线 \( {AQ} \) 的方程.

【答案】 \( y = \frac{\sqrt{5}}{10}x + 1 \) .

设 \( P\left( {{x}_{0},{y}_{0}}\right) \) ,线段 \( {AP} \) 的中垂线与 \( x \) 轴的交点即 \( M\left( {\frac{3}{8}{x}_{0},0}\right) \) ,

\( \because \overrightarrow{PQ} = 4\overrightarrow{PM} \) ,

\( \therefore Q\left( {-\frac{3}{2}{x}_{0}, - 3{y}_{0}}\right) ,\because \overrightarrow{AQ} = 2\overrightarrow{AC},\therefore C\left( {-\frac{3}{4}{x}_{0},\frac{1 - 3{y}_{0}}{2}}\right) \) ,代入并联立椭圆方程,

【解析】得 \( {x}_{0} = \frac{8\sqrt{5}}{9},{y}_{0} =  - \frac{1}{9},\therefore Q\left( {-\frac{4}{3}\sqrt{5},\frac{1}{3}}\right) \) ,

\( \therefore \) 直线 \( {AQ} \) 的方程为 \( y = \frac{\sqrt{5}}{10}x + 1 \) .

21. 设定义在 \( R \) 上的函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 满足: 对于任意的 \( {x}_{1}\text{ 、 }{x}_{2} \in  R \) ,当 \( {x}_{1} < {x}_{2} \) 时,都有 \( f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  \leq \; f\left( {x}_{2}\right) \) .

(1)若 \( f\left( x\right)  = a{x}^{3} + 1 \) ，求 \( a \) 的取值范围.

【答案】 \( a \geq  0 \) .

由题意有 \( {f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {3a}{x}^{2} \geq  0 \) 恒成立,所以 \( a \geq  0 \) .

( 2 )若 \( f\left( x\right) \) 为周期函数，证明: \( f\left( x\right) \) 是常值函数.

【答案】证明见解析.

不妨设周期为 \( T \) ,任取 \( {x}_{0} \in  R \) ,则有 \( f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = f\left( {{x}_{0} + T}\right) \) ,

由题意可知对任意的 \( x \in  \left\lbrack  {{x}_{0},{x}_{0} + T}\right\rbrack  , f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  \leq  f\left( x\right)  \leq  f\left( {{x}_{0} + T}\right) \) ,

所以 \( f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = f\left( x\right)  = f\left( {{x}_{0} + T}\right) \) ,

又 \( f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = f\left( {{x}_{0} + {nT}}\right) \left( {n \in  Z}\right) \) ,

且 \( \cdots  \cup  \left\lbrack  {{x}_{0} - {2T},{x}_{0} - T}\right\rbrack   \cup  \left\lbrack  {{x}_{0} - T,{x}_{0}}\right\rbrack   \cup  \left\lbrack  {{x}_{0},{x}_{0} + T}\right\rbrack   \cup  \left\lbrack  {{x}_{0} + T,{x}_{0} + {2T}}\right\rbrack   \cup  \cdots  = R \) ,

所以对任意的 \( x \in  R, f\left( x\right)  = f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = C \) ,为常数.

(3) 设 \( f\left( x\right) \) 恒大于零, \( g\left( x\right) \) 是定义在 \( R \) 上、恒大于零的周期函数， \( M \) 是 \( g\left( x\right) \) 的最大值. 函数 \( h\left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right) g\left( x\right) \) . 证明: “ \( h\left( x\right) \) 是周期函数” 的充要条件是 “ \( f\left( x\right) \) 是常值函数”.

【答案】证明见解析.

证明:

充分性: 若 \( f\left( x\right) \) 是常值函数,记 \( f\left( x\right)  = {c}_{1} \) ,设 \( g\left( x\right) \) 的一个周期为 \( {T}_{1} \) ,

则 \( h\left( x\right)  = {c}_{1} \cdot  g\left( x\right) \) ,则对任意 \( {x}_{0} \in  R \) ,

\[
h\left( {{x}_{0} + {T}_{1}}\right)  = {c}_{1} \cdot  g\left( {{x}_{0} + {T}_{1}}\right)  = {c}_{1} \cdot  g\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = h\left( {x}_{0}\right) ,
\]

故 \( h\left( x\right) \) 是周期函数;

必要性: 若 \( h\left( x\right) \) 是周期函数,记其一个周期为 \( {T}_{2} \) .

设集合 \( A = \{ x \mid  g\left( x\right)  = m\} , f\left( x\right)  > 0 \) 恒成立,

任取 \( {x}_{0} \in  A \) ,则必存在 \( {N}_{2} \in  N \) ,使得 \( {x}_{0} - {N}_{2}{T}_{2} \leq  {x}_{0} - {T}_{1} \) ,

即 \( \left\lbrack  {{x}_{0} - {T}_{1}{x}_{0}}\right\rbrack   \subseteq  \left\lbrack  {{x}_{0} - {N}_{2}{T}_{2}{x}_{0}}\right\rbrack \) ,
