(2) 设 \( t = 1 \) 表示 1978 年,第 \( n \) 年卫生总费用与年份 \( t \) 之间拟合函数 \( f\left( t\right)  = \frac{357876.6053}{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{{6.4420} - {0.1136t}}} \) 研究函数 \( f\left( t\right) \) 的单调性,并预测我国卫生总费用首次超过 12 万亿的年份.

【答案】我国到 2028 年我国卫生总费用首次超过 12 万亿

\( \because y = {\mathrm{e}}^{{6.4420} - {0.1136t}} \) 是减函数,且 \( y = {\mathrm{e}}^{{6.4420} - {0.1136t}} > 0 \) ,

\( \therefore f\left( t\right)  = \frac{357876.6053}{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{{6.4420} - {0.1136t}}} \) 在 \( N \) 上单调递增,

令 \( \frac{357876.6053}{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{{6.4420} - {0.1136t}}} > {120000} \) ,解得 \( t > {50.68} \) ,

\( \therefore \) 当 \( t \geq  {51} \) 时,我国卫生总费用超过 12 万亿,

\( \therefore \) 预测我国到 2028 年我国卫生总费用首次超过 12 万亿.

20. 已知抛物线方程 \( {y}^{2} = {4x} \) ， \( F \) 为焦点， \( P \) 为抛物线准线上一点， \( Q \) 为线段 \( {PF} \) 与抛物线的交点,定义: \( d\left( P\right)  = \frac{\left| PF\right| }{\left| FQ\right| } \) .

(1)当 \( P\left( {-1, - {83}}\right) \) 时，求 \( d\left( P\right) \) ；

## 【答案】83

抛物线方程 \( {y}^{2} = {4x} \) 的焦点 \( F\left( {1,0}\right) , P\left( {-1, - {83}}\right) \) ，

\( {K}_{PF} = 2 = {43},\;{PF} \) 的方程为 \( y = {43}\left( {x - 1}\right) \) ,代入抛物线的方程,解得 \( {x}_{Q} = {14} \) ,

抛物线的准线方程为 \( x =  - 1 \) ,可得 \( \left| {PF}\right|  = \sqrt{{2}^{2} + 9} = 3 \) ,

\( \left| {QF}\right|  = {14} + 1 = {54},\;d\left( P\right)  = \frac{\left| PF\right| }{\left| FQ\right| } = {83}. \)

(2)证明:存在常数 \( a \) ，使得 \( {2d}\left( P\right)  = \left| {PF}\right|  + a \) ；

【答案】见解析

当 \( P\left( {-1,0}\right) \) 时, \( a = {2d}\left( P\right)  - \left| {PF}\right|  = 2 \times  2 - 2 = 2 \) ,

设 \( P\left( {-1,{y}_{P}}\right) ,{y}_{P} > 0,{PF} : x = {my} + 1 \) ,则 \( m{y}_{P} =  - 2 \) ,

联立 \( x = {my} + 1 \) 和 \( {y}^{2} = {4x} \) ,可得 \( {y}^{2} - {4my} - 4 = 0,{y}_{Q} = 2 = {2m} + 2\sqrt{1 + {m}^{2}} \) ,

\( {2d}\left( P\right)  - \left| {PF}\right|  = 2\frac{{y}_{P}}{{y}_{Q}} - \sqrt{1 + {m}^{2}}{y}_{P} = 2 \cdot  \frac{-2}{m\left( {{2m} + 2\sqrt{1 + {m}^{2}}}\right) } + m =  - 2 \cdot  m + m = 2 \)

则存在常数 \( a \) ,使得 \( {2d}\left( P\right)  = \left| {PF}\right|  + a \) ;

另解: \( d\left( P\right)  = \frac{\left| PF\right| }{\left| FQ\right| } = \frac{\left| {PQ}\right|  + \left| {FQ}\right| }{\left| FQ\right| } = 1 + \frac{\left| PQ\right| }{\left| FQ\right| } = 1 + \frac{\left| PQ\right| }{t} = 1 + \frac{\left| PF\right| }{2} \) ,

可得 \( {2d}\left( P\right)  = \left| {PF}\right|  + 2 \) .

(3) \( {P}_{1},{P}_{2},{P}_{3} \) 为抛物线准线上三点，且 \( \left| {{P}_{1}{P}_{2}}\right|  = \left| {{P}_{2}{P}_{3}}\right| \) ，判断 \( d\left( {P}_{1}\right)  + d\left( {P}_{3}\right) \) 与 \( {2d}\left( {P}_{2}\right) \) 的关系. 【答案】 \( d\left( {P}_{1}\right)  + d\left( {P}_{3}\right)![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_292_402_213_401_491_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_292_402_213_401_491_0.jpg)39b5b00_292_402_213_401_491_0.jpg)

设 \( {P}_{1}\left( {-1,{y}_{1}}\right) ,{P}_{2}\left( {-1,{y}_{2}}\right) ,{P}_{3}\left( {-1,{y}_{3}}\right) \) ,

则 \( 2\left\lbrack  {d\left( {P}_{1}\right)  + d\left( {P}_{3}\right) }\right\rbrack   - {4d}\left( {P}_{2}\right)  = \left| {{P}_{1}F}\right|  + \left| {{P}_{3}F}\right|  - 2\left| {{P}_{2}F}\right|  = \sqrt{4 + {y}_{1}^{2}} + \sqrt{4 + {y}_{3}^{2}} - 2\sqrt{4 + {y}_{2}^{2}} \)

\( = \sqrt{4 + {y}_{1}^{2}} + \sqrt{4 + {y}_{3}^{2}} - 2\sqrt{{\left( 2\right) }^{2} + 4} = \sqrt{4 + {y}_{1}^{2}} + \sqrt{4 + {y}_{3}^{2}} - \sqrt{{\left( {y}_{1} + {y}_{3}\right) }^{2} + {16}} \)

由 \( {\left( \sqrt{4 + {y}_{1}^{2}} + \sqrt{4 + {y}_{3}^{2}}\right) }^{2} - \left\lbrack  {{\left( {y}_{1} + {y}_{3}\right) }^{2} + {16}}\right\rbrack   = 2\sqrt{4 + {y}_{1}^{2}}\sqrt{4 + {y}_{3}^{2}} - 2{y}_{1}{y}_{3} - 8 \) ,

\( \left( {4 + {y}_{1}^{2}}\right) \left( {4 + {y}_{3}^{2}}\right)  - {\left( {y}_{1}{y}_{3} + 4\right) }^{2} = 4\left( {{y}_{1}^{2} + {y}_{3}^{2}}\right)  - 8{y}_{1}{y}_{3} = 4{\left( {y}_{1} - {y}_{3}\right) }^{2} > 0, \)

则 \( d\left( {P}_{1}\right)  + d\left( {P}_{3}\right)  > {2d}\left( {P}_{2}\right) \) .

21. 已知等差数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的公差 \( d \in  (0,\pi \rbrack \) ,数列 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 满足 \( {b}_{n} = \sin \left( {a}_{n}\right) \) ,集合 \( S = \; \left\{  {x \mid  x = {b}_{n}, n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right\}  . \)

(1) 若 \( {a}_{1} = 0, d = 3 \) 求集合 \( S \) ;

【答案】 \( S = \{  - 2,0,2\} \)

\( \because \) 等差数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的公差 \( d \in  (0,\pi \rbrack \) ,数列 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 满足 \( {b}_{n} = \sin \left( {a}_{n}\right) \) ,集合 \( S = \)

\( \left\{  {x \mid  x = {b}_{n}, n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right\}  . \)

\( \therefore \) 当 \( {a}_{1} = 0, d = 3 \) ,

集合 \( S = \{  - 2,0,2\} \) .

( 2 )若 \( {a}_{1} = {\pi 2} \) ，求 \( d \) 使得集合 \( S \) 恰好有两个元素；

【答案】 \( d = \pi \) 或者 \( d = 3 \)

\( \because {a}_{1} = {\pi 2} \) ,数列 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 满足 \( {b}_{n} = \sin \left( {a}_{n}\right) \) ,集合 \( S = \left\{  {x \mid  x = {b}_{n}, n \in  {N![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_293_407_219_411_410_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_293_407_219_411_410_0.jpg)39b5b00_293_407_219_411_410_0.jpg)

根据三角函数线，①等差数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的终边落在 \( y \) 轴的正负半轴上时，集合 \( S \) 恰好有两个元素,此时 \( d = \pi \) ,

② \( {a}_{1} \) 终边落在 \( {OA} \) 上，要使得集合 \( S \) 恰好有两个元素，可以使 \( {a}_{2} \) ， \( {a}_{3} \) 的终边关于 \( y \) 轴对称,如图 \( {OB},{OC} \) ,此时 \( d = 3 \) ,

综上, \( d = \pi \) 或者 \( d = 3 \) .

(3)若集合 \( S \) 恰好有三个元素: \( {b}_{n + T} = {b}_{n} \) ， \( T \) 是不超过 7 的正整数，求 \( T \) 的所有可能的值.

【答案】 \( T = 3,4,5,6 \)

① 当 \( T = 3 \) 时， \( {b}_{n + 3} = {b}_{n} \) ，集合 \( S = \left\{  {{b}_{1},{b}_{2},{b}_{3}}\right\} \) ，符合题意；

② 当 \( T = 4 \) 时， \( {b}_{n + 4} = {b}_{n} \) ， \( \sin \left( {{a}_{n} + {4d}}\right)  = \sin {a}_{n} \) ， \( {a}_{n} + {4d} = {a}_{n} + {2k\pi } \) ，或者 \( {a}_{n} + {4d} \)

\[
= \left( {{2k![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_293_796_1168_361_360_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_293_796_1168_361_360_0.jpg)9b5b00_293_796_1168_361_360_0.jpg)

等差数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的公差, \( d \in  (0,\pi \rbrack \) ,故 \( {a}_{n} + {4d} = {a}_{n} + {2k\pi }, d = 2 \) ,

\[
\therefore k = 1,2\text{ , }
\]

当 \( k = 1 \) 时满足条件,此时 \( S = \{ 0,1, - 1\} \) ;

③ 当 \( T = 5 \) 时， \( {b}_{n + 5} = {b}_{n} \) ， \( \sin \left( {{a}_{n} + {5d}}\right)  = \sin {a}_{n} \) ， \( {a}_{n} + {5d} = {a}_{n} + {2k\pi } \) ，或者 \( {a}_{n} + {5d} \; = \left( {{2k} + 1}\right) \pi  - {a}_{n} \) ,因为 \( d \in  (0,\![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_294_805_225_345_341_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_294_805_225_345_341_0.jpg)39b5b00_294_805_225_345_341_0.jpg)

当 \( k = 1 \) 时， \( S = \{ \sin 5,1, - \sin 5\} \) 满足题意；

④ 当 \( T = 6 \) 时, \( {b}_{n + 6} = {b}_{n},\sin \left( {{a}_{n} + {6d}}\right)  = \sin {a}_{n} \) ,

所以 \( {a}_{n} + {6d} = {a}_{n} + {2k\pi } \) ,或者 \( {a}_{n} + {6d} = \left( {{2k} + 1}\right) \pi  - {a}_{n}, d \in  (0,\![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_294_791_724_370_415_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_294_791_724_370_415_0.jpg)39b5b00_294_791_724_370_415_0.jpg)

当 \( k = 1 \) 时， \( S = \{ 2,0, - 2\} \) ，满足题意；

⑤ 当 \( T = 7 \) 时， \( {b}_{n + 7} = {b}_{n} \) ， \( \sin \left( {{a}_{n} + {7d}}\right)  = \sin {a}_{n} \) ，所以 \( {a}_{n} + {7d} = {a}_{n} + {2k\pi } \) ，或者 \( {a}_{n} + \; {7d} = \left( {{2k} + 1}\right) \pi  - {a}_{n},\;d \in  (0,\pi \rbrack , \) 故 \( k = 1,2,3. \)

当 \( k = 1 \) 时,因为 \( {b}_{1} \sim  {b}_{7} \) 对应着 3 个正弦值,故必有一个正弦值对应着 3 个点,必然

有 \( {a}_{m} - {a}_{n} = {2\pi }, d = \frac{2\pi }{m - n} = 7, m - n = 7, m > 7 \) ,不符合条件.

当 \( k = 2 \) 时,因为 \( {b}_{1} \sim  {b}_{7} \) 对应着 3 个正弦值,故必有一个正弦值对应着 3 个点,必然

有 \( {a}_{m} - {a}_{n} = {2\pi }, d = \frac{2\pi }{![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_294_428_1540_1099_263_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_294_428_1540_1099_263_0.jpg)b5b00_294_428_1540_1099_263_0.jpg)

当 \( k = 3 \) 时,因为 \( {b}_{1} \sim  {b}_{7} \) 对应着 3 个正弦值,故必有一个正弦值对应着 3 个点,必然有 \( {a}_{m} - {a}_{n} = {2\pi } \) 或者 \( {4\pi }, d = \frac{2\pi }{m - n} = 7 \) ,或者 \( d = \frac{4\pi }{m - n} = 7 \) ,此时, \( m - n \) 均不是整数, 不符合题意.

综上, \( T = 3,4,5,6 \) .

## 2020 秋考

一、填空题(本题共 12 小题，满分 54 分，其中 1-6 题每题 4 分，7-12 题每题 5 分) 1. 已知集合 \( A = \{ 1,2,4\} , B = \{ 2,3,4\} \) ，求 \( A \cap  B = \) ___.

【答案】 \( \{ 2,4\} \)

因为 \( A = \{ 1,2,3\} , B = \{ 2,4,5\} \) ,

则 \( A \cap  B = \{ 2,4\} \) .

\( \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} 2, & 4 \end{array}\right\} \) .

2. \( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{n + 1}{{3n} - 1} = \) ___.

【答案】 \( \frac{1}{3} \)

\( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{n + 1}{{3n} - 1} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{1 + \frac{1}{n}}{3 - \frac{1}{n}} = \frac{1 + \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{1}{n}}{3 - \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{1}{n}} = \frac{1 + 0}{3 - 0} = \frac{1}{3} \) ,

3. 已知复数 \( z \) 满足 \( z = 1 - 2\mathrm{i} \) ( \( \mathrm{i} \) 为虚数单位),则 \( \left| z\right|  = \) ___.

【答案】 \( \sqrt{5} \)

由 \( z = 1 - 2\mathrm{i} \) ,得 \( \left| z\right|  = \sqrt{{1}^{2} + {\left( -2\right) }^{2}} = \sqrt{5} \) .

4. 已知行列式 \( \left| \begin{array}{l} 1 \\  2 \\  3 \end{array}\right|  = 6 \) ,则行列式 \( \left| \begin{array}{l} a \\  d \end{array}\right|  = \) ___.

【答案】 2

行列式 \( \left| \begin{array}{l} 1 \\  2 \\  3 \end{array}\right|  = 6 \) ,

可得 \( 3\left| \begin{array}{l} a \\  c \end{array}\right|  = 6 \) ,解得 \( \left| \begin{array}{l} a \\  c \end{array}\right|  = 2 \) .

5. 已知 \( f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{3} \) ,则 \( {f}^{-1}\left( x\right)  = \) ___.

【答案】 \( {x}^{\frac{1}{3}}\left( {x \in  R}\right) \)

由 \( y = f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{3} \) ,得 \( x = \sqrt[3]{y} \) ,

把 \( x \) 与 \( y \) 互换,可得 \( f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{3} \) 的反函数为 \( {f}^{-1}\left( x\right)  = \sqrt[3]{x} = {x}^{\frac{1}{3}}\left( {x \in  R}\right) \) .

6. 已知 \( a \) 、 \( b \) 、1、2的中位数为3，平均数为4，则 \( {ab} = \) ___.

【答案】36

因为四个数的平均数为 4 , 所以 \( a + b = 4 \times  4 - 1 - 2 = {13} \) ,

因为中位数是 3,所以 \( \frac{2 + a}{2} = 3 \) ,解得 \( a = 4 \) ,代入上式得 \( b = {13} - 4 = 9 \) ,

所以 \( {ab} = {36} \) ,

7. 已知 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} x + y \geq  2 \\  y \geq  0 \\  x + {2y} - 3 \leq  0 \end{array}\right. \) 则 \( z = y - {2x} \) 的最大值为___.

【答案】-1

由约束条件 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} x + y - 2 \geq  0 \\  x + {2y} - 3 \leq  0 \\  y \geq  0 \e![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_298_410_226_552_410_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_298_410_226_552_410_0.jpg)39b5b00_298_410_226_552_410_0.jpg)

化目标函数 \( z = y - {2x} \) 为 \( y = {2x} + z \) ,

由图可知,当直线 \( y = {2x} + z \) 过 \( A \) 时,直线在 \( y \) 轴上的截距最大,

联立 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} x + y - 2 = 0 \\  x + {2y} - 3 = 0 \end{array}\right. \) ,解得 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = 1 \\  y = 1 \end{array}\right. \) ,即 \( A\left( {1,1}\right) \) .

\( z \) 有最大值为 \( 1 - 2 \times  1 =  - 1 \) .

8. 已知 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 是公差不为零的等差数列,且 \( {a}_{1} + {a}_{10} = {a}_{9} \) ,则 \( \frac{{a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + \cdots  + {a}_{9}}{{a}_{10}} = \) ___.

【答案】 \( \frac{27}{8} \)

根据题意，等差数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 满足 \( {a}_{1} + {a}_{10} = {a}_{9} \) ,即 \( {a}_{1} + {a}_{1} + {9d} = {a}_{1} + {8d} \) ,变形可得 \( {a}_{1} \; =  - d \) ,

所以 \( \frac{{a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + \cdots  + {a}_{9}}{{a}_{10}} = \frac{9{a}_{1} + \frac{9 \times  {8d}}{2}}{{a}_{1} + {9d}} = \frac{9{a}_{1} + {36d}}{{a}_{1} + {9d}} = \frac{-{9d} + {36d}}{-d + {9d}} = \frac{27}{8} \) .

9. 从 6 人中挑选 4 人去值班, 每人值班 1 天, 第一天需要 1 人, 第二天需要 1 人, 第三天需要 2 人，则有___种排法.

【答案】180

根据题意,可得排法共有 \( {C}_{6}^{1}{C}_{5}^{1}{C}_{4}^{2} = {180} \) 种.

10. 椭圆 \( \frac{{x}^{2}}{4} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{3} = 1 \) ,过右焦点 \( F \) 作直线 \( l \) 交椭圆于 \( P\text{ 、 }Q \) 两点, \( P \) 在第二象限已知 \( Q\left( {{x}_{Q},{y}_{Q}}\right) ,{Q}^{\prime }\left( {{x}_{Q}^{\prime },{y}_{Q}^{\prime }}\right) \) 都在椭圆上,且 \( {y}_{Q} + {y}_{Q}^{\prime } = 0, F{Q}^{\prime } \bot  {PQ} \) ,则直线 \( l \) 的方程为 ___.

【答案】 \( x + y - 1 = 0 \)

椭圆 \( C : \frac{{x}^{2}}{4} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{3} = 1 \) 的右焦点为 \( F\left( {1,0}\right) \) ,

直线 \( l \) 经过椭圆右焦点 \( F \) ,交椭圆 \( C \) 于 \( P\text{ 、 }Q \) 两点 (点 \( P \) 在第二象限),

若点 \( Q \) 关于 \( x \) 轴对称点为 \( {Q}^{\prime } \) ,且满足 \( {PQ} \bot  F{Q}^{\prime } \) ,

可知直线 \( l \) 的斜率为 -1,所以直线 \( l \) 的方程是: \( y =  - \left( {x - 1}\righ![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_299_423_927_424_407_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_299_423_927_424_407_0.jpg)39b5b00_299_423_927_424_407_0.jpg)

11. 设 \( a \in  R \) ,若存在定义域 \( R \) 的函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 既满足 “对于任意 \( {x}_{0} \in  R, f\left( {x}_{0}\right) \) 的值为 \( {x}_{0}^{2} \) 或 \( {x}_{0} \) ” 又满足 “关于 \( x \) 的方程 \( f\left( x\right)  = a \) 无实数解”,则 \( a \) 的取值范围为___.

【答案】 \( \left( {-\infty ,0}\right)  \cup  \left( {0,1}\right)  \cup  \left( {1, + \infty }\right) \)

题目转换为是否为实数 \( a \) ,使得存在函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 满足 “对于任意 \( {x}_{0} \in  R, f\left( {x}_{0}\right) \) 的值为 \( {x}_{0}^{2} \) 或 \( {x}_{0} \) ”,

又满足 “关于的方程 \( f\left( x\right)  = a \) 无实数解” 构造函数,

\( f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{l} x, \\  {x}^{2}, \end{array}\right. \) ,则方程 \( f\left( x\right)  = a \) 只有0,1两个实数解.

12. 已知 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{1},{\overrightarrow{a}}_{2},{\overrightarrow{b}}_{1},{\overrightarrow{b}}_{2},\cdots ,{\overrightarrow{b}}_{k}\left( {k \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) 是平面内两两互不相等的向量,满足 \( \left| {{\overrightarrow{a}}_{1} - {\overrightarrow{a}}_{2}}\right|  = 1 \) , 且 \( \left| {{\overrightarrow{a}}_{i} - {\overrightarrow{b}}_{j}}\right|  \in  \{ 1,2\} \) (其中 \( \mathrm{i} = 1,2, j = 1,2,\cdots , k)![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_300_412_577_398_322_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_300_412_577_398_322_0.jpg)39b5b00_300_412_577_398_322_0.jpg)

根据向量减法的运算规律, \( \left| {{\overrightarrow{a}}_{i} - {\overrightarrow{b}}_{j}}\right|  \in  \{ 1,2\} \) 可转化为以向量 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{1} \) 和 \( {\overrightarrow{a}}_{2} \) 终点为圆心,

作半径 \( {r}_{1} = 1 \) 和 \( {r}_{2} = 2 \) 的圆,两圆交点即为满足题意的 \( \overrightarrow{b} \) ,由图知, \( k \) 的最大值为 6 .

## 二、选择题 (本题共有 4 小题, 每题 5 分, 共计 20 分)

13. 下列不等式恒成立的是( )

A. \( {a}^{2} + {b}^{2} \leq  {2ab} \) B. \( {a}^{2} + {b}^{2} \geq   - {2ab} \) C. \( a + b \geq   - 2\sqrt{\left| ab\right| } \) D. \( a + b \leq  2\sqrt{\left| ab\right| } \)

## 【答案】 \( B \)

A. 显然当 \( a < 0 \) ， \( b > 0 \) 时，不等式 \( {a}^{2} + {b}^{2} \leq  {2ab} \) 不成立，故 A 错误；

B. \( \because {\left( a + b\right) }^{2} \geq  0,\therefore {a}^{2} + {b}^{2} + {2ab} \geq  0,\therefore {a}^{2} + {b}^{2} \geq   - {2ab} \) ,故 \( B \) 正确；

\( C \) . 显然当 \( a < 0, b < 0 \) 时，不等式 \( a + b \geq  2\sqrt{\left| ab\right| } \) 不成立，故 \( C \) 错误；

D. 显然当 \( a > 0, b > 0 \) 时，不等式 \( {a}^{2} + {b}^{2} \leq   - {2ab} \) 不成立，故 \( D \) 错误.

B.

14. 已知直线 \( l \) 的解析式为 \( {3x} + {4y} + 1 = 0 \) ，则下列各式是 \( l \) 的参数方程的是 ( )

A. \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = 1 + {3t} \\  y =  - 1 - {4t} \end{array}\right. \) B. \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = 1 - {4t} \\  y =  - 1 + {3t} \end{array}\right. \) C. \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = 1 - {3t} \\  y =  - 1 + {4t} \end{array}\right. \) D. \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = 1 + {4t} \\  y = 1 - {3t} \end{array}\right. \)

## 【答案】 \( B \)

\( \left\{  {\begin{array}{l} x = 1 + {3t} \\  y =  - 1 - {4t} \end{array}\text{ ( }t}\right. \) 为参数) 的普通方程为: \( \frac{x - 1}{y + 1} =  - \frac{3}{4} \) ,即 \( {3x} + {3y} - 1 = 0 \) ,不正确;

\( \left\{  {\begin{array}{l} x = 1 - {4t} \\  y =  - 1 + {3t} \end{array}\text{ ( }t}\right. \) 为参数) 的普通方程为: \( \frac{x - 1}{y + 1} =  - \frac{4}{3} \) ,即 \( {3x} + {4y} + 1 = 0 \) ,正确;

\( \left\{  {\begin{array}{l} x = 1 - {3t} \\  y =  - 1 + {4t} \end{array}\left( {t\text{ 为参数 }}\right) \text{ 的普通方程为: }\frac{x - 1}{y + 1} =  - \frac{3}{4},\text{ 即 }{4x} + {3y} - 1 = 0,\text{ 不正确; }}\right. \)

\( \left\{  {\begin{array}{l} x = 1 + {4t} \\  y = 1 - {3t} \end{array}\text{ ( }t}\right. \) 为参数) 的普通方程为: \( \frac{x - 1}{y - 1} =  - \frac{4}{3} \) ,即 \( {3x} + {4y} - 7 = 0 \) ,不正确;

B.

15. 在棱长为 10 的正方体 \( {ABCD} - {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 中, \( P \) 为左侧面 \( {AD}{D}_{1}{A}_{1} \) 上一点,已知点 \( P \) 到 \( {A}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 的距离为 3,点 \( P \) 到 \( A{A}_{1} \) 的距离为 2,则过点 \( P \) 且与 \( {A}_{1}C \) 平行的直线交正方体于 \( P \) 、 \![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_301_282_1201_312_308_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_301_282_1201_312_308_0.jpg)9b5b00_301_282_1201_312_308_0.jpg)

A. \( A{A}_{1}{B}_{1}B \) B. \( B{B}_{1}{C}_{1}C \) C. \( C{C}_{1}{D}_{1}D ![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_301_426_1652_324_303_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_301_426_1652_324_303_0.jpg)9b5b00_301_426_1652_324_303_0.jpg)

延长 \( {BC} \) 至 \( M \) 点,使得 \( {CM} = 2 \) ,

延长 \( {C}_{1}C \) 至 \( N \) 点，使得 \( {CN} = 3 \) ，

以 \( C\text{ 、 }M\text{ 、 }N \) 为顶点作矩形,记矩形的另外一个顶点为 \( H \) ,

连接 \( {A}_{1}P\text{ 、 }{PH}\text{ 、 }{HC} \) ,则易得四边形 \( {A}_{1}{PHC} \) 为平行四边形,

因为点 \( P \) 在平面 \( {AD}{D}_{1}{A}_{1} \) 内,点 \( H \) 在平面 \( {BC}{C}_{1}{B}_{1} \) 内,

且点 \( P \) 在平面 \( {ABCD} \) 的上方,点 \( H \) 在平面 \( {ABCD} \) 下方,

所以线段 \( {PH} \) 必定会在和平面 \( {ABCD} \) 相交,

即点 \( Q \) 在平面 \( {ABCD} \) 内.

16. 若存在 \( a \in  R \) 且 \( a \neq  0 \) ,对任意的 \( x \in  R \) ,均有 \( f\left( {x + a}\right)  < f\left( x\right)  + f\left( a\right) \) 恒成立,则称函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 具有性质 \( P \) ,已知: \( {q}_{1} : f\left( x\right) \) 单调递减,且 \( f\left( x\right)  > 0 \) 恒成立; \( {q}_{2} : f\left( x\right) \) 单调递增,存在 \( {x}_{0} < 0 \) 使得 \( f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = 0 \) ,则是 \( f\left( x\right) \) 具有性质 \( P \) 的充分条件是 ( )

A. 只有 \( {q}_{1} \) B. 只有 \( {q}_{2} \) C. \( {q}_{1} \) 和 \( {q}_{2} \) D. \( {q}_{1} \) 和 \( {q}_{2} \) 都不是

## 【答案】 \( C \)

本题要看清楚一个函数具有性质 \( P \) 的条件是,存在 \( a \in  R \) 且 \( a \neq  0 \) ,

则对于 \( {q}_{1}, a > 0 \) 时,易得函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 具有性质 \( P \) ;

对于 \( {q}_{2} \) ,只需取 \( a = {x}_{0} \) ,则 \( x + a = x + {x}_{0} < x, f\left( a\right)  = f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = 0 \) ,

所以 \( f\left( {x + a}\right)  = f\left( {x + {x}_{0}}\right)  < f\left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right)  + f\left( a\right) \) ,所以此时函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 具有性质 \( P \) .

## 三、解答题 (本题共 5 小题, 共计 76 分)

17. 已知边长为 1 的正方形 \( {ABCD} \) ,沿 \( {BC} \) 旋转一周得到圆柱体.

(1)求圆柱体的表面积；

## 【答案】 \( {4\pi } \)

该圆柱的表面由上下两个半径为 1 的圆面和一个长为 \( {2\pi } \) 、宽为 1 的矩形组成，

\( \therefore S = 2 \times  \pi  \times  {1}^{2} + {2\pi } \times  1 = {4\pi } \) .

故该圆柱的表面积为 \( {4\pi } \) .

(2)正方形 \( {ABCD} \) 绕 \( {BC} \) 逆时针旋转 \( \frac{\pi }{2} \) 到 \( {A}_{1}{BC}{D}_{1} \) ，求 \( A{D}_{1} \) 与平面 \( {ABCD} \) 所成的角.

【答案】 \( \arccos \frac{\sqrt{6}}{3} \)

\( \because \) 正方形 \( {AB}{C}_{1}{D}_{1},\therefore A{D}_{1} \bot  {AB} \) ,

又 \( \angle {DA}{D}_{1} = \frac{\pi }{2},\therefore A{D}_{1} \bot  {AD} \) ,

\( \because {AD} \cap  {AB} = A \) ,且 \( {AD}\text{ 、 }{AB} \subset \) 平面 \( {ADB} \) ,

\( \therefore A{D}_{1} \bot \) 平面 \( {ADB} \) ,即 \( {D}_{1} \) 在面 \( {ADB} \) 上的投影为 \( A \) ,

连接 \( C{D}_{1} \) ,则 \( \angle {D}_{1}{CA} \) 即为线段 \( C{D}_{1} \) 与平面 \( {ABCD} \) 所成的角,

而 \( \cos \angle {D}_{1}{CA} = \frac{AC}{C{D}_{1}} = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{3}} = \frac{\sqrt{6}}{3} \) ,

\( \therefore \) 线段 \( C{D}_{1} \) 与平面 \( {ABCD} \) 所成的角为 \( \arccos \frac{\sqrt{6}}{3} \) .

18. 已知 \( f\left( x\right)  = \sin {\omega x}\left( {\omega 0}\right) \) .

(1)若 \( f\left( x\right) \) 的周期是 \( {4\pi } \) ,求 \( \omega \) ,并求此时 \( f\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{2} \) 的解集；

【答案】 \( \omega  = \frac{1}{2},\;x \in  \left\{  {x\left| {\;x = \frac{\pi }{3} + {4k\pi }\text{ 或 }x = \frac{5\pi }{3} + {4k\pi }}\right. , k \in  Z}\right\} \)

由于 \( f\left( x\right) \) 的周期是 \( {4\pi } \) ,所以 \( \omega  = \frac{2\pi }{4\pi } = \frac{1}{2} \) ,所以 \( f\left( x\right)  = \sin \frac{1}{2}x \) .

令 \( \sin \frac{1}{2}x = \frac{1}{2} \) ,故 \( \frac{1}{2}x = {2k\pi } + \frac{\pi }{6} \) 或 \( {2k\pi } + \frac{5\pi }{6} \) ,整理得 \( x = {4k\pi } + \frac{\pi }{3} \) 或 \( x = {4k\pi } + \; \frac{5\pi }{3} \) .

故解集为 \( \left\{  {x \mid  x = {4k\pi } + \frac{\pi }{3}}\right. \) 或 \( \left. {x = {4k\pi } + \frac{5\pi }{3}\text{ ， }k \in  Z}\right\} \) .

( 2 )已知 \( \omega  = 1, g\left( x\right)  = {f}^{2}\left( x\right)  + \sqrt{3}f\left( {-x}\right) f\left( {\frac{\pi }{2} - x}\right) , x \in  \left\lbrack  {0,\frac{\pi }{4}}\right\rbrack \) ，求 \( g\left( x\right) \) 的值域.

【答案】 \( \left\lbrack  {-\frac{1}{2},0}\right\rbrack \)

由于 \( \omega  = 1 \) ,

所以 \( f\left( x\right)  = \sin x \) .

所以 \( g\left( x\right)  = {\sin }^{2}x + \sqrt{3}\sin \left( {-x}\right) \sin \left( {\frac{\pi }{2} - x}\right)  = \frac{1 - \cos {2x}}{2} - \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\sin {2x} =  - \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\sin {2x} \)

\( - \frac{1}{2}\cos {2x} + \frac{1}{2} = \frac{1}{2} - \sin \left( {{2x} + \frac{\pi }{6}}\right) . \)

由于 \( x \in  \left\lbrack  {0,\frac{\pi }{4}}\right\rbrack \) ,

所以 \( \frac{\pi }{6} \leq  {2x} + \frac{\pi }{6} \leq  \frac{2\pi }{3} \) .

\( \frac{1}{2} \leq  \sin \left( {{2x} + \frac{\pi }{6}}\right)  \leq  1, \)

故 \( - 1 \leq   - \sin \left( {{2x} + \frac{\pi }{6}}\right)  \leq   - \frac{1}{2} \) ,

故 \( - \frac{1}{2} \leq  g\left( x\right)  \leq  0 \) .

所以函数 \( g\left( x\right) \) 的值域为 \( \left\lbrack  {-\frac{1}{2},0}\right\rbrack \) .

19. 已知: \( v = \frac{q}{x}, x \in  (0,{80}\rbrack \) ,且 \( v = \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {100} - {135}{\left( \frac{1}{3}\right) }^{\frac{80}{x}}, \\   - k\left( {x - {40}}\right)  + {85}, \end{array}\right. \left( {k0}\right) \)

(1)若 \( v > {95} \) ，求 \( x \) 的取值范围；

【答案】 \( x \in  \left( {0,\frac{80}{3}}\right) \)

\( \because v = \frac{q}{x},\therefore v \) 越大, \( x \) 越小,

\( \therefore v = f\left( x\right) \) 是单调递减函数, \( k > 0 \) ,

当 \( {40} \leq  x \leq  {80} \) 时, \( v \) 最大为 85,

于是只需令 \( {100} - {135}{\left( \frac{1}{3}\right) }^{x} > {95} \) ,解得 \( x > 3 \) ,

故道路密度 \( x \) 的取值范围为 \( \left( {3,{40}}\right) \) .

( 2 )已知 \( x = {80} \) 时， \( v = {50} \) ，求 \( x \) 为多少时， \( q \) 可以取得最大值，并求出该最大值.

【答案】 \( x = \frac{480}{7} \) 时, \( {q}_{\max } = \frac{28800}{7} \)

把 \( x = {80}, v = {50} \) 代入 \( v = f\left( x\right)  =  - k\left( {x - {40}}\right)  + {85} \) 中,

得 \( {50} =  - {k40} + {85} \) ,解得 \( k = \frac{7}{8} \) .

\( \therefore q = {vx} = \left\{  {\begin{array}{ll} {100x} - {135}{\left( \frac{1}{3}\right) }^{x}x, & 0 < x < {40} \\   - \frac{7}{8}\left( {x - {40}}\right) x + {85x}, & {40} \leq  x \leq  {80} \end{array},}\right. \)

当 \( 0 < x < {40} \) 时, \( q \) 单调递增, \( q < {100} \times  {40} - {135} \times  {\left( \frac{1}{3}\right) }^{40} \times  {40} \approx  {4000} \) ;

当 \( {40} \leq  x \leq  {80} \) 时, \( q \) 是关于 \( x \) 的二次函数,开口向下,对称轴为 \( x = \frac{480}{7} \) ,

此时 \( q \) 有最大值,为 \( - \frac{7}{8} \times  {\left( \frac{480}{7}\right) }^{2} + {120} \times  \frac{480}{7} = \frac{28800}{7} > {4000} \) .

故车辆密度 \( q \) 的最大值为 \( \frac{28800}{7} \) .

20. 双曲线 \( {C}_{1} : \frac{{x}^{2}}{4} - \frac{{y}^{2}}{{b}^{2}} = 1 \) ,圆 \( {C}_{2} : {x}^{2} + {y}^{2} = 4 + {b}^{2}\left( {b0}\right) \) 在第一象限交点为 \( A, A\left( {{x}_{A},{y}_{A}}\right) \) , 曲线 \( \Gamma \left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{{x}^{2}}{4} - \frac{{y}^{2}}{{b}^{2}} = 1, \\  {x}^{2} + {y}^{2} = 4 ![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_305_254_423_491_555_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_305_254_423_491_555_0.jpg)39b5b00_305_254_423_491_555_0.jpg)

(1) 若 \( {x}_{A} = \sqrt{6} \) ,求 \( b \) ;

## 【答案】 2

若 \( {x}_{A} = \sqrt{6} \) ,因为点 \( A \) 为曲线 \( {C}_{1} \) 与曲线 \( {C}_{2} \) 的交点,

\( \because \left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{{x}_{A}^{2}}{4} - \frac{{y}^{2}}{{b}^{2}} = 1 \\  {x}_{A}^{2} + {y}^{2} = 4 + {b}^{2} \end{array}\right. \) ,解得 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} y = \sqrt{2} \\  b = 2 \end{array}\right. \)

\( \therefore b = 2 \) .

( 2 )若 \( b = \sqrt{5} \) ， \( {C}_{2} \) 与 \( x \) 轴交点记为 \( {F}_{1} \) 、 \( {F}_{2} \) ， \( P \) 是曲线 \( \Gamma \) 上一点，且在第一象限，并满足 \( \left| {P{F}_{1}}\right| \; = 8 \) ,求 \( \angle {F}_{1}P{F}_{2} \) ;

【答案】 \( \frac{11}{16} \)

方法一:由题意易得 \( {F}_{1}{F}_{2} \) 为曲线的两焦点,

由双曲线定义知: \( \left| {P{F}_{2}}\right|  = \left| {P{F}_{1}}\right|  - {2a} \) ,

\( \left| {P{F}_{1}}\right|  = 8,\;{2a} = 4,\;\therefore \left| {P{F}_{2}}\right|  = 4 \) ,

又 \( \because b = \sqrt{5} \) ,

\( \therefore \left| {{F}_{1}{F}_{2}}\right|  = 6 \) ,

在 \( P{F}_{1}{F}_{2} \) 中由余弦定理可得:

\( \cos \angle {F}_{1}P{F}_{2} = \frac{{\left| P{F}_{1}\right| }^{2} + {\left| P{F}_{2}\right| }^{2} - {\left| {F}_{1}{F}_{2}\right| }^{2}}{2 \cdot  \left| {P{F}_{1}}\right|  \cdot  \left| {P{F}_{2}}\right| } = \frac{11}{16}, \)

方法二: \( \because b = \sqrt{5} \) ,可得 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{{x}^{2}}{4} - \frac{{y}^{2}}{5} = 1 \\  {\left( x + 3\right) }^{2} + {y}^{2} = {64} \end{array}\right. \) ,解得 \( P\left( {4,\sqrt{15}}\right) \) ,

\( \therefore \overrightarrow{P{F}_{1}} = \left( {-7, - \sqrt{15}}\right) ,\;\overrightarrow{P{F}_{2}} = \left( {-1, - \sqrt{15}}\right) \) ,

\( \therefore \cos \overrightarrow{P{F}_{1}},\overrightarrow{P{F}_{2}} = \frac{\overrightarrow{P{F}_{1}} \cdot  \overrightarrow{P{F}_{2}}}{\left| \overrightarrow{P{F}_{1}}\right|  \cdot  \left| \overrightarrow{P{F}_{2}}\right| } = \frac{11}{16} \) .

(3)过点 \( S\left( {0,2 + \frac{{b}^{2}}{2}}\right) \) 且斜率为 \( - \frac{b}{2} \) 的直线 \( l \) 交曲线 \( \Gamma \) 于 \( M\text{ 、 }N \) 两点，用 \( b \) 的代数式表示 \( \overrightarrow{OM} \) . \( \overrightarrow{ON} \) ,并求出 \( \overrightarrow{OM} \cdot  \overrightarrow{ON} \) 的取值范围.

【答案】 \( \left( {6 + 2\sqrt{5}, + \infty }\right) \)

设直线 \( l : y =  - \frac{b}{2}x + \frac{{b}^{2} + 4}{2} \) ,

可得原点 \( O \) 到直线 \( l \) 的距离 \( d = \frac{\left| \frac{{b}^{2} + 4}{2}\right| }{\sqrt{1 + \frac{{b}^{2}}{4}}} = \frac{\left| {b}^{2} + 4\right| }{\sqrt{{b}^{2} + 4}} = \sqrt{{b}^{2} + 4} \) ,

所以直线 \( l \) 是圆的切线,切点为 \( M \) ,

所以 \( {k}_{OM} = \frac{2}{b} \) ,并设 \( {l}_{OM} : y = \frac{2}{b}x \) ,与圆 \( {x}^{2} + {y}^{2} = 4 + {b}^{2} \) 联立可得 \( {x}^{2} + \frac{4}{{b}^{2}}{x}^{2} = 4 + \; {b}^{2} \) ,

所以得 \( x = b, y = 2 \) ,即 \( M\left( {b,2}\right) \) ,

注意到直线 \( l \) 与双曲线得斜率为负得渐近线平行,

所以只有当 \( {y}_{A} > 2 \) 时,直线 \( l \) 才能与曲线 \( \Gamma \) 有两个交点,

由 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{{x}^{2}}{4} - \frac{{y}^{2}}{{b}^{2}} = 1 \\  {x}_{A}^{2} + {y}^{2} = 4 + {b}^{2} \end{array}\right. \) ,得 \( {y}_{A}^{2} = \frac{{b}^{4}}{a + {b}^{2}} \) ,

所以有 \( 4 < \frac{{b}^{4}}{4 + {b}^{2}} \) ,解得 \( {b}^{2} > 2 + 2\sqrt{5} \) ,或 \( {b}^{2} < 2 - 2\sqrt{5} \) (舍),

又因为 \( \overrightarrow{OM} \cdot  \overrightarrow{ON} \) 由 \( \overrightarrow{ON} \) 在 \( \overrightarrow{OM} \) 上的投影可知: \( \overrightarrow{OM} \cdot  \overrightarrow{ON} = {b}^{2} + 4 \) ,

所以 \( \overrightarrow{OM} \cdot  \overrightarrow{ON} = {b}^{2} + 4 > 6 + 2\sqrt{5} \) ,

\( \overrightarrow{OM} \cdot  \overrightarrow{ON} \in  \left( {6 + 2\sqrt{5}, + \infty }\right) \) .

21. 有限数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) ,若满足 \( \left| {{a}_{1} - {a}_{2}}\right|  \leq  \left| {{a}_{1} - {a}_{3}}\right|  \leq  \cdots  \leq  \left| {{a}_{1} - {a}_{m}}\right| , m \) 是项数,则称 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 满足性质 \( p \) .

(1)判断数列3，2，5，1 和 4，3，2，5，1 是否具有性质 \( p \) ，请说明理由;

【答案】见解析

对于第一个数列有 \( \left| {2 - 3}\right|  = 1,\left| {5 - 3}\right|  = 2,\left| {1 - 3}\right|  = 2 \) ,满足题意,该数列满足性质 \( p \) ;

对于第二个数列有 \( \left| {3 - 4}\right|  = 1,\left| {2 - 4}\right|  = 2,\left| {5 - 4}\right|  = 1 \) 不满足题意,该数列不满足性质 \( p \) .

( 2 )若 \( {a}_{1} = 1 \) ，公比为 \( q \) 的等比数列，项数为 10，具有性质 \( p \) ，求 \( q \) 的取值范围；

【答案】 \( q \in  ( - \infty , - 2\rbrack  \cup  \left( {0, + \infty }\right) \)

由题意可得, \( \left| {{q}^{n} - 1}\right|  \geq  \left| {{q}^{n - 1} - 1}\right| ,\;n \in  \{ 2,3,\cdots ,9\} \) ,

两边平方得: \( {q}^{2n} - 2{q}^{n} + 1 \geq  {q}^{{2n} - 2} - 2{q}^{n - 1} + 1 \) ,

整理得: \( \left( {q - 1}\right) {q}^{n - 1}\left\lbrack  {{q}^{n - 1}\left( {q + 1}\right)  - 2}\right\rbrack   \geq  0 \) ,

当 \( q \geq  1 \) 时,得 \( {q}^{n - 1}\left( {q + 1}\right)  - 2 \geq  0 \) ,此时关于 \( n \) 恒成立,

所以等价于 \( n = 2 \) 时 \( q\left( {q + 1}\right)  - 2 \geq  0 \) ,所以 \( \left( {q + 2}\right) \left( {q - 1}\right)  \geq  0 \) ,

所以 \( q \leq   - 2 \) 或者 \( q \geq  1 \) ,所以取 \( q \geq  1 \) .

当 \( 0 < q \leq  1 \) 时,得 \( {q}^{n - 1}\left( {q + 1}\right)  - 2 \leq  0 \) ,此时关于 \( n \) 恒成立,

所以等价于 \( n = 2 \) 时 \( q\left( {q + 1}\right)  - 2 \leq  0 \) ,所以 \( \left( {q + 2}\right) \left( {q - 1}\right)  \leq  0 \) ,

所以 \( - 2 \leq  q \leq  1 \) ,所以取 \( 0 < q \leq  1 \) .

当 \( - 1 \leq  q < 0 \) 时,得 \( {q}^{n - 1}\left\lbrack  {{q}^{n - 1}\left( {q + 1}\right)  - 2}\right\rbrack   \leq  0 \) .

当 \( n \) 为奇数的时候,得 \( {q}^{n - 1}\left( {q + 1}\right)  - 2 \leq  0 \) ,很明显成立,

当 \( n \) 为偶数的时候,得 \( {q}^{n - 1}\left( {q + 1}\right)  - 2 \geq  0 \) ,很明显不成立,

故当 \( - 1 \leq  q < 0 \) 时,矛盾,舍去.

当 \( q <  - 1 \) 时,得 \( {q}^{n - 1}\left\lbrack  {{q}^{n - 1}\left( {q + 1}\right)  - 2}\right\rbrack   \leq  0 \) .

当 \( n \) 为奇数的时候,得 \( {q}^{n - 1}\left( {q + 1}\right)  - 2 \leq  0 \) ,很明显成立,

当 \( n \) 为偶数的时候,要使 \( {q}^{n - 1}\left( {q + 1}\right)  - 2 \geq  0 \) 恒成立,

所以等价于 \( n = 2 \) 时 \( q\left( {q + 1}\right)  - 2 \geq  0 \) ,所以 \( \left( {q + 2}\right) \left( {q - 1}\right)  \geq  0 \) ,

所以 \( q \leq   - 2 \) 或者 \( q \geq  1 \) ,所以取 \( q \leq   - 2 \) .

综上可得, \( q \in  ( - \infty , - 2\rbrack  \cup  \left( {0, + \infty }\right) \) .

(3)若 \( {a}_{n} \) 是 1, \( 2,\cdots , m \) 的一个排列 \( \left( {m \geq  4}\right) ,{b}_{k} = {a}_{k + 1}\left( {k = 1,2\cdots , m - 1}\right) ,\left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}  ,\left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 都具有性质 \( p \) ,求所有满足条件的 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) .

【答案】见解析

\[
\text{ 设 }{a}_{1} = p, p \in  \{ 3,4,\cdots , m - 3, m - 2\} \text{ , }
\]

因为 \( {a}_{1} = p,{a}_{2} \) 可以取 \( p - 1 \) 或者 \( p + 1,{a}_{3} \) 可以取 \( p - 2 \) 或者 \( p + 2 \) .

如果 \( {a}_{2} \) 或者 \( {a}_{3} \) 取了 \( p - 3 \) 或者 \( p + 3 \) ,将使 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 不满足性质 \( p \) ,

所以, \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的前五项有以下组合:

① \( {a}_{1} = p,\;{a}_{2} = p - 1,\;{a}_{3} = p + 1,\;{a}_{4} = p - 2,\;{a}_{5} = p + 2 \) ,

② \( {a}_{1} = p,\;{a}_{2} = p - 1,\;{a}_{3} = p + 1,\;{a}_{4} = p + 2,\;{a}_{5} = p - 2 \) ,

③ \( {a}_{1} = p,{a}_{2} = p + 1,{a}_{3} = p - 1,{a}_{4} = p - 2,{a}_{5} = p + 2 \) ，

④ \( {a}_{1} = p,\;{a}_{2} = p + 1,\;{a}_{3} = p - 1,\;{a}_{4} = p + 2,\;{a}_{5} = p - 2 \) ,

对于①， \( {b}_{1} = p - 1 \) ， \( \left| {{b}_{2} - {b}_{1}}\right|  = 2 \) ， \( \left| {{b}_{3} - {b}_{1}}\right|  = 1 \) ，与 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 满足性质 \( p \) 矛盾，舍去.

对于②， \( {b}_{1} = p - 1 \) ， \( \left| {{b}_{2} - {b}_{1}}\right|  = 2 \) ， \( \left| {{b}_{3} - {b}_{1}}\right|  = 3 \) ， \( \left| {{b}_{4} - {b}_{1}}\right|  = 2 \) 与 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 满足性质 \( p \) 矛盾, 舍去.

对于③， \( {b}_{1} = p + 1 \) ， \( \left| {{b}_{2} - {b}_{1}}\right|  = 2 \) ， \( \left| {{b}_{3} - {b}_{1}}\right|  = 3 \) ， \( \left| {{b}_{4} - {b}_{1}}\right|  = 1 \) 与 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 满足性质 \( p \) 矛盾, 舍去.

对于④, \( {b}_{1} = p + 1,\left| {{b}_{2} - {b}_{1}}\right|  = 2,\left| {{b}_{3} - {b}_{1}}\right|  = 1 \) ,与 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 满足性质 \( p \) 矛盾,舍去.

所以 \( p \in  \{ 3,4,\cdots , m - 3, m - 2\} \) 均不能同时使 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}  ,\left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 都具有性质 \( p \) .

当 \( p = 1 \) 时,有数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}   : 1,2,3,\cdots , m - 1, m \) 满足题意;

当 \( p = m \) 时,有数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}   : m, m - 1,\cdots ,3,2,1 \) 满足题意;

当 \( p = 2 \) 时,有数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}   : 2,1,3,\cdots , m - 1, m \) 满足题意;

当 \( p = m - 1 \) 时,有数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}   : m - 1, m, m - 2, m - 3,\cdots ,3,2,1 \) 满足题

意.

故满足题意的数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 只有上面四种.

## 2020 春考

一、填空题(本大题共 12 题，满分 54 分，第 1~6 题每题 4 分，第 7-12 题每题 5 分) 1. 集合 \( A = \{ 1,3\} , B = \{ 1,2, a\} \) ，若 \( A \subseteq  B \) ，则 \( a = \) ___.

## 【答案】 3

\( \because 3 \in  A \) ,且 \( A \subseteq  B,\therefore 3 \in  B,\therefore a = 3 \) .

3.

2. 不等式 \( {1x} > 3 \) 的解集为___.

【答案】 \( \left( {0,{13}}\right) \)

由 \( {1x} > 3 \) 得 \( \frac{1 - {3x}}{x} > 0 \) ,

则 \( x\left( {1 - {3x}}\right)  > 0 \) ,即 \( x\left( {{3x} - 1}\right)  < 0 \) ,解得 \( 0 < x < {13} \) ,

所以不等式的解集是 \( \left( {0,{13}}\right) \) .

\( \left( {0,{13}}\right) \) .

3. 函数 \( y = \tan {2x} \) 的最小正周期为___.

【答案】 \( {\pi 2} \)

函数 \( y = \tan {2x} \) 的最小正周期为 \( {\pi 2} \) .

\( {\pi 2} \) .

4. 已知复数 \( z \) 满足 \( z + 2\bar{z} = 6 + \mathrm{i} \) ，则 \( z \) 的实部为___.

## 【答案】 2

设 \( z = a + {bi},\left( {a, b \in  R}\right) \) .

\( \because \) 复数 \( z \) 满足 \( z + 2\bar{z} = 6 + \mathrm{i} \) ,

\( \therefore {3a} - {bi} = 6 + \mathrm{i} \) ,

可得: \( {3a} = 6, - b = 1 \) ,解得 \( a = 2, b =  - 1 \) .

则 \( z \) 的实部为 2 .

2.

5. 已知 \( 3\sin {2x} = 2\sin x, x \in  \left( {0,\pi }\right) \) ，则 \( x = \) ___.

【答案】arccos13

\( \because 3\sin {2x} = 2\sin x \) ,

\( 6\sin x\cos x = 2\sin x, \)

\( \because x \in  \left( {0,\pi }\right) \) ,

\( \therefore \sin x \neq  0 \) ,

\( \therefore \cos x = {13} \) ,

故 \( x = \arccos {13} \) .

arccos13.

6. 若函数 \( y = a \cdot  {3}^{x} + {13}^{x} \) 为偶函数,则 \( a = \) ___.

## 【答案】 1

根据题意,函数 \( y = a \cdot  {3}^{x} + {13}^{x} \) 为偶函数,则 \( f\left( {-x}\right)  = f\left( x\right) \) ,

即 \( a \cdot  {3}^{\left( -x\right) } + {13}^{\left( -x\right) } = a \cdot  {3}^{x} + {13}^{x} \) ,

变形可得: \( a\left( {{3}^{x} - {3}^{-x}}\right)  = \left( {{3}^{x} - {3}^{-x}}\right) \) ,

必有 \( a = 1 \) .

1.

7. 已知直线 \( {l}_{1} : x + {ay} = 1,{l}_{2} : {ax} + y = 1 \) ，若 \( {l}_{1}//{l}_{2} \) ，则 \( {l}_{1} \) 与 \( {l}_{2} \) 的距离为___.

【答案】 \( \sqrt{2} \)

直线 \( {l}_{1} : \;x + {ay} = 1,\;{l}_{2} : \;{ax} + y = 1 \) ,

当 \( {l}_{1}//{l}_{2} \) 时, \( {a}^{2} - 1 = 0 \) ,解得 \( a =  \pm  1 \) ;

当 \( a = 1 \) 时 \( {l}_{1} \) 与 \( {l}_{2} \) 重合,不满足题意;

当 \( a =  - 1 \) 时 \( {l}_{1}//{l}_{2} \) ,此时 \( {l}_{1} : x - y - 1 = 0,{l}_{2} : x - y + 1 = 0 \) ;

则 \( {l}_{1} \) 与 \( {l}_{2} \) 的距离为 \( d = \frac{\left| -1 - 1\right| }{\sqrt{{1}^{2} + {\left( -1\right) }^{2}}} = \sqrt{2} \) .

\( \sqrt{2} \) .

8. 已知二项式 \( {\left( 2x + \sqrt{x}\right) }^{5} \) ，则展开式中 \( {x}^{3} \) 的系数为___.

【答案】 10

\( {C}_{5}^{4}{\left( 2x\right) }^{1}{\left( \sqrt{x}\right) }^{4} = {10}{x}^{3} \) ,所以展开式中 \( {x}^{3} \) 的系数为 10 .

10.

9. 三角形 \( {ABC} \) 中， \( D \) 是 \( {BC} \) 中点， \( {AB} = 2,{BC} = 3,{AC} = 4 \) ，则 \( \overrightarrow{AD} \cdot  \overrightarrow{AB} = \) ___.

【答案】 4

\( \because {ABC} \) 中, \( {AB} = 2,{BC} = 3,{AC} = 4 \) ,

\( \therefore \) 由余弦定理得, \( \cos \angle {BAC} = \frac{A{B}^{2} + A{C}^{2} - B{C}^{2}}{{2A}B \cdot  {AC}} = \frac{4 + {16} - 9}{2 \times  2 \times  4} = \frac{11}{16} \) ，

\( \therefore \overrightarrow{AB} \cdot  \overrightarrow{AC} = 2 \times  4 \times  \frac{11}{16} = 2 \) ,且 \( D \) 是 \( {BC} \) 的中点,

\( \therefore \overrightarrow{AD} \cdot  \overrightarrow{AB} = {12}\left( {\overrightarrow{AB} + \overrightarrow{AC}}\right)  \cdot  \overrightarrow{AB} = {12}\left( {{\overrightarrow{AB}}^{2} + \overrightarrow{AB} \cdot  \overrightarrow{AC}}\right)  = {12} \times  \left( {4 + 2}\right)  = 4 \) .

4.

10. 已知 \( A = \{  - 3, - 2, - 1,0,1,2,3\} , a\text{ 、 }b \in  A \) ,则 \( \left| a\right|  < \left| b\right| \) 的情况有___种.

## 【答案】 18

当 \( a =  - 3,0 \) 种,

当 \( a =  - 2,2 \) 种,

当 \( a =  - 1,4 \) 种,

当 \( a = 0,6 \) 种,

当 \( a = 1,4 \) 种,

当 \( a = 2,2 \) 种,

当 \( a = 3,0 \) 种,

故共有: \( 2 + 4 + 6 + 4 + 2 = {18} \) .

18.

11. 已知 \( {A}_{1}\text{ 、 }{A}_{2}\text{ 、 }{A}_{3}\text{ 、 }{A}_{4}\text{ 、 }{A}_{5} \) 五个点,满足 \( \overrightarrow{{A}_{n}{A}_{n + 1}} \cdot  \overrightarrow{{A}_{n + 1}{A}_{n + 2}} = 0\left( {n = 1,2,3}\right) ,\left| \overrightarrow{{A}_{n}{A}_{n + 1}}\right| \) . \( \left| \overrightarrow{{A}_{n + 1}{A}_{n + 2}}\right|  = n + 1\left( {n = 1,2,3}\right) \) ，则 \( \left| \overrightarrow{{A}_{1}{A}![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_312_404_1184_370_342_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_312_404_1184_370_342_0.jpg)9b5b00_312_404_1184_370_342_0.jpg)

设 \( \left| \overrightarrow{{A}_{1}{A}_{2}}\right|  = x \) ,则 \( \left| \overrightarrow{{A}_{2}{A}_{3}}\right|  = \frac{2}{x},\left| \overrightarrow{{A}_{3}{A}_{4}}\right|  = \frac{3x}{2},\left| \overrightarrow{{A}_{4}{A}_{5}}\right|  = {83x} \) ,

设 \( {A}_{1}\left( {0,0}\right) \) ,如图,

\( \because \) 求 \( \left| \overrightarrow{{A}_{1}{A}_{5}}\right| \) 的最小值,则:

\( {A}_{2}\left( {x,0}\right) ,\;{A}_{3}\left( {x,{2x}}\right) ,\;{A}_{4}\left( {-{x2},{2x}}\right) ,\;{A}_{5}\left( {-{x2}, - {23x}}\right) , \)

\( \therefore {\left| \overrightarrow{{A}_{1}{A}_{5}}\right| }^{2} = {\left( -x2\right) }^{2} + {\left( -{23}x\right) }^{2} = 4 + {49}{x}^{2} \geq  {23} \) ,当且仅当 \( 4 = {49}{x}^{2} \) ,即 \( x = 3 \) 时取等号,

\( \therefore \left| \overrightarrow{{A}_{1}{A}_{5}}\right| \) 的最小值为 3 .

3.

12. 已知 \( f\left( x\right)  = \sqrt{x - 1} \) ,其反函数为 \( {f}^{-1}\left( x\right) \) ,若 \( {f}^{-1}\left( x\right)  - a = f\left( {x + a}\right) \) 有实数根,则 \( a \) 的取值范围为___.

【答案![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_313_410_550_393_348_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_313_410_550_393_348_0.jpg)39b5b00_313_410_550_393_348_0.jpg)

因为 \( y = {f}^{-1}\left( x\right)  - a \) 与 \( y = f\left( {x + a}\right) \) 互为反函数,

若 \( y = {f}^{-1}\left( x\right)  - a \) 与 \( y = f\left( {x + a}\right) \) 有实数根,

则 \( y = f\left( {x + a}\right) \) 与 \( y = x \) 有交点,

所以 \( \sqrt{x + a - 1} = x \) ,

即 \( a = {x}^{2} - x + 1 = {\left( x - {12}\right) }^{2} + {34} \geq  {34} \) .

\( \lbrack {34}, + \infty ) \) .

## 二、选择题 (本大题共 4 题, 每题 5 分, 共 20 分)

13. 计算: \( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{{3}^{n} + {5}^{n}}{{3}^{n - 1} + {5}^{n - 1}} =  \) (   )

A. 3 B. 53 C. 35 D. 5

【答案】 \( D \)

\( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{{3}^{n} + {5}^{n}}{{3}^{n - 1} + {5}^{n - 1}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{3{\left( {35}\right) }^{n - 1} + 5}{{\left( {35}\right) }^{n - 1} + 1} = 5. \)

故选 \( D \)

14. ” \( a = \beta \) ” 是 “ \( {\sin }^{2}\alpha  + {\cos }^{2}\beta  = 1 \) ” 的 ( )

A. 充分非必要条件 B. 必要非充分条件

C. 充要条件 D. 既非充分又非必要条件

【答案】 \( A \)

①若 \( \alpha  = \beta \) ，则 \( {\sin }^{2}\alpha  + {\cos }^{2}\beta  = {\sin }^{2}\alpha  + {\cos }^{2}\alpha  = 1 \) ，

\( \therefore \) “ \( \alpha  = \beta \) “是 “ \( {\sin }^{2}\alpha  + {\cos }^{2}\beta  = 1 \) “的充分条件;

②若 \( {\sin }^{2}\alpha  + {\cos }^{2}\beta  = 1 \) ，则 \( {\sin }^{2}\alpha  = {\sin }^{2}\beta \) ，得不出 \( \alpha  = \beta \) ，

\( \therefore \) “ \( \alpha  = \beta \) ” 不是 “ \( {\sin }^{2}\alpha  + {\cos }^{2}\beta  = 1 \) ” 的必要条件,

\( \therefore \) “ \( \alpha  = \beta \) ” 是 “ \( {\sin }^{2}\alpha  + {\cos }^{2}\beta  = 1 \) ” 的充分非必要条件.

故选 \( A \)

15. 已知椭圆 \( 2 + {y}^{2} = 1 \) ，作垂直于 \( x \) 轴的垂线交椭圆于 \( A \) 、 \( B \) 两点，作垂直于 \( y \) 轴的垂线交椭圆于 \( C \) 、 \( D \) 两点,且 \( {AB} = {CD} \) ，两垂线相交于点 \( P \) ，则点 \( P \) 的轨迹是 ( )

A. 椭圆 ![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_314_416_1205_410_311_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_314_416_1205_410_311_0.jpg)9b5b00_314_416_1205_410_311_0.jpg)

\( \because {AB} \leq  2,{CD} \leq  2 \) ，判断轨迹为上下两支，即选双曲线，

设 \( A\left( {m, t}\right) \) ， \( D\left( {t, n}\right) \) ，

所以 \( P\left( {m, n}\right) \) ，

因为 \( 2 + {t}^{2} = 1,2 + {n}^{2} = 1 \) ,消去 \( t \) 可得: \( 2{n}^{2} - 2 = 1 \) .

故选 \( B \)

16. 数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 各项均为实数,对任意 \( n \in  {N}^{ * } \) 满足 \( {a}_{n + 3} = {a}_{n} \) ,且行列式 \( \left| \begin{matrix} {a}_{n} & {a}_{n + 1} \\  {a}_{n + 2} & {a}_{n + 3} \end{matrix}\right|  = c \) 为定值, 则下列选项中不可能的是 ( )

A. \( {a}_{1} = 1, c = 1 \) B. \( {a}_{1} = 2, c = 2 \) C. \( {a}_{1} =  - 1, c = 4 \) D. \( {a}_{1} = 2, c = 0 \)

## 【答案】 \( B \)

行列式 \( \left| \begin{matrix} {a}_{n} & {a}_{n + 1} \\  {a}_{n + 2} & {a}_{n + 3} \end{matrix}\right|  = {a}_{n}{a}_{n + 3} - {a}_{n + 1}{a}_{n + 2} = c \) ,

\( \because \) 对任意 \( n \in  {N}^{ * } \) 满足 \( {a}_{n + 3} = {a}_{n} \) ,

\( \therefore \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {a}_{n}^{2} - {a}_{n + 1}{a}_{n + 2} = c \\  {a}_{n + 1}^{2} - {a}_{n + 2}{a}_{n + 3} = c \end{array}\right. \)

作差整理得: \( {a}_{n + 1} = {a}_{n} \) (常数列, \( c = 0 \) ),或 \( {a}_{n} + {a}_{n + 1} + {a}_{n + 2} = 0 \) ,

当 \( {a}_{n} + {a}_{n + 1} + {a}_{n + 2} = 0 \) ,则 \( {a}_{n + 1} + {a}_{n + 2} =  - {a}_{n} \) 及 \( {a}_{n + 1}{a}_{n + 2} = {a}_{n}^{2} - c \) ,

\( \therefore \) 方程 \( {x}^{2} + {a}_{n}x + {a}_{n}^{2} - c \) 有两根 \( {a}_{n + 1},{a}_{n + 2} \) ,

\( \therefore \Delta  = {a}_{n}^{2} - 4\left( {{a}_{n}^{2} - c}\right)  = {4c} - 3{a}_{n}^{2} > 0 \) .

因为 \( B \) 错.

故选 \( B \)

三、解答题 (本大题共 5 题, 共 \( {14} + {14} + {14} + {16} + {18} = {76} \) 分)

17. 已知四棱锥 \( P - {ABCD} \) ，底面 \( {ABCD} \) 为正方形，边长为3， ![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_315_263_1411_367_269_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_315_263_1411_367_269_0.jpg)9b5b00_315_263_1411_367_269_0.jpg)

(1)若 \( {PC} = 5 \) ，求四棱锥 \( P - {ABCD} \) 的体积；

【答案】 12

\( \because {PD} \bot \) 平面 \( {ABCD},\therefore {PD} \bot  {DC} \) .

\( \because {CD} = 3,\therefore {PC} = 5,\;\therefore {PD} = 4 \) ,

\( \therefore {V}_{P - {ABCD}} = {13} \times  {3}^{2} \times  4 = {12} \) ,

所以四棱锥的体积为 12 .

(2)若直线 \( {AD} \) 与 \( {BP} \) 的夹角为 \( {60}^{ \circ  } \) ，求 \( {PD} \) 的长.

【答案】 \( 3\sqrt{2} \)

\( \because {ABCD} \) 是正方形， \( {PD} \bot \) 平面 \( {ABCD} \) ,

\( \therefore {BC} \bot  {PD},{BC} \bot  {CD} \) ,

又 \( \because {PD} \cap  {CD} = D \) ,

\( \therefore {BC} \bot \) 平面 \( {ABCD} \) ,

\( \therefore {BC} \bot  {PC} \) ,

\( \because \) 异面直线 \( {AD} \) 与 \( {PB} \) 所成角为 \( {60}^{ \circ  },{BC}//{AD} \) ,

\( \therefore \) 在 RtPBC 中, \( \angle {PBC} = {60}^{ \circ  },{BC} = 3 \) ,

故 \( {PC} = 3\sqrt{3} \) ,

在 RtPBC 中, \( {CD} = 3 \) ,

\( \therefore {PD} = 3\sqrt{2} \) .

18. 已知各项均为正数的数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) ,其前 \( n \) 项和为 \( {S}_{n},{a}_{1} = 1 \) .

(1)若数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 为等差数列， \( {S}_{10} = {70} \) ，求数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的通项公式；

【答案】 \( {a}_{n} = {43n} - {13} \)

数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 为公差为 \( d \) 的等差数列, \( {S}_{10} = {70},{a}_{1} = 1 \) ,

可得 \( {10} + {12} \times  {10} \times  {9d} = {70} \) ,解得 \( d = {43} \) ,

则 \( {a}_{n} = 1 + {43}\left( {n - 1}\right)  = {43n} - {13} \) .

( 2 )若数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 为等比数列， \( {a}_{4} = {18} \) ，求满足 \( {S}_{n} > {{100}{a}_{n}} \) 时 \( n \) 的最小值.

【答案】 \( n \) 的最小值为 7

数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 为公比为 \( q \) 的等比数列, \( {a}_{4} = {18},{a}_{1} = 1 \) ,

可得 \( {q}^{3} = \frac{1}{8} \) ,即 \( q = {12} \) ,

则 \( {a}_{n} = {\left( {12}\right) }^{n - 1},{S}_{n} = \frac{1 - {\left( {12}\right) }^{n}}{1 - {12}} = 2 - {\left( {12}\right) }^{n - 1} \) ,

\( {S}_{n} > {100}{a}_{n} \) ,即为 \( 2 - {\left( {12}\right) }^{n - 1} > {100} \cdot  {\left( {12}\right) }^{n - 1} \) ,

即 \( {2}^{n} > {101} \) ,可得 \( n \geq  7 \) ,即 \( n \) 的最小值为 7 .

19. 有一条长为 120 米的步行道 \( {OA}, A \) 是垃圾投放点 \( {\omega }_{1} \) ,若以 \( O \) 为原点, \( {OA} \) 为 \( x \) 轴正半轴建立直角坐标系,设点 \( B\left( {x,0}\right) \) ,现要建设另一座垃圾投放点 \( {\omega }_{2}\left( {t,0}\right) \) ,函数 \( {f}_{t}\left( x\right) \) 表示与点 \( B \) 距离最近的垃圾投放点的距离.

(1) 若 \( t = {60} \) ,求 \( {f}_{60}\left( {10}\right) \text{ 、 }{f}_{60}\left( {80}\right) \text{ 、 }{f}_{60}\left( {95}\right) \) 的值,并写出 \( {f}_{60}\left( x\right) \) 的函数解析式;

【答案】 \( {50};\;{20};\;{25};\;{f}_{60}\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{l} \left| {{60} - x}\right| , \\  \left| {{120} - x}\right| , \end{array}\right. \)

投放点 \( {\omega }_{1}\left( {{120},0}\right) ,{\omega }_{2}\left( {{60},0}\right) ,{f}_{60}\left( {10}\right) \) 表示与 \( B \) 距离最近的投放点 (即 \( {\omega }_{2} \) ) 的距离, 所以 \( {f}_{60}\left( {10}\right)  = \left| {{60} - {10}}\right|  = {50} \) ,同理分析 \( {f}_{60}\left( {80}\right)  = \left| {{60} - {80}}\right|  = {20},{f}_{60}\left( {95}\right)  =  \mid  {120} - \; {95} \mid   = {25} \) ,

由题意得, \( {f}_{60}\left( x\right)  = {\left\{  \left| {60} - x\right| ,\;\left| {120} - x\right| \right\}  }_{\min } \) ,

则当 \( \left| {{60} - x}\right|  \leq  \left| {{120} - x}\right| \) ,即 \( x \leq  {90} \) 时, \( {f}_{60}\left( x\right)  = \left| {{60} - x}\right| \) ;

当 \( \left| {{60} - x}\right|  > \left| {{120} - x}\right| \) ,即 \( x > {90} \) 时, \( {f}_{60}\left( x\right)  = \left| {{120} - x}\right| \) ;

综上 \( {f}_{60}\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{l} \left| {{60} - x}\right| , \\  \left| {{120} - x}\right| , \end{array}\right. \)

(2)若可以通过 \( {f}_{t}\left( x\right) \) 与坐标轴围成的面积来测算扔垃圾的便利程度，面积越小越便利. 问:垃圾投放点 \( {\omega }_{2} \) 建在何处才能比建在中点时更加便利?

【答案】垃圾投放点 \( {\omega }_{2} \) 建在 \( \left( {{20},0}\right) \) 与 \( \left( {![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_317_418_1077_424_222_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_317_418_1077_424_222_0.jpg)9b5b00_317_418_1077_424_222_0.jpg)

由题意得 \( {f}_{t}\left( x\right)  = \{ \left| {t - x}\right| ,\;\left| {{120} - x}\right| {\} }_{\min } \) ,

所以 \( {f}_{t}\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{l} \left| {t - x}\right| , \\  \left| {{120} - x}\right| , \end{array}\right. \) ,则 \( {f}_{t}\left( x\right) \) 与坐标轴围成的面积如阴影部分所示,

所以 \( S = {12}{t}^{2} + {14}{\left( {120} - t\right) }^{2} = {34}{t}^{2} - {60t} + {3600} \) ,

由题意， \( S < S\left( {60}\right) \) ，即 \( {{34}{t}^{2} - {60t} + {3600}} < {2700} \) ，

【解析】得 \( {20} < t < {60} \) ,即垃圾投放点 \( {\omega }_{2} \) 建在 \( \left( {{20},0}\right) \) 与 \( \left( {{60},0}\right) \) 之间时,比建在中点时更加便利.

20. 已知抛物线 \( {y}^{2} = x \) 上的动点 \( M\left( {{x}_{0},{y}_{0}}\right) \) ,过 \( M \) 分别作两条直线交抛物线于 \( P\text{ 、 }Q \) 两点,交直线 \( x = t \) 于 \( A\text{ 、 }B \) 两点.

(1)若点 \( M \) 纵坐标为 \( \sqrt{2} \) ，求 \( M \) 与焦点的距离；

【答案】 94

\( \because \) 抛物线 \( {y}^{2} = x \) 上的动点 \( M\left( {{x}_{0},{y}_{0}}\right) \) ,

过 \( M \) 分别作两条直线交抛物线于 \( P\text{ 、 }Q \) 两点,交直线 \( x = t \) 于 \( A\text{ 、 }B \) 两点.

点 \( M \) 纵坐标为 \( \sqrt{2} \) ,

\( \therefore \) 点 \( M \) 的横坐标 \( {x}_{M} = {\left( \sqrt{2}\right) }^{2} = 2 \) ,

\( \because {y}^{2} = x,\;\therefore p = {12} \) ,

\( \therefore M \) 与焦点的距离为 \( {MF} = {x}_{M} + {p2} = 2 + {14} = {94} \) .

( 2 )若 \( t =  - 1 \) ， \( P\left( {1,1}\right) \) ， \( Q\left( {1, - 1}\right) \) ，求证: \( {y}_{A} \cdot  {y}_{B} \) 为常数；

【答案】见解析

设 \( M\left( {{y}_{0}^{2},{y}_{0}}\right) \) ,直线 \( {PM} : y - 1 = \frac{{y}_{0} - 1}{{y}_{0}^{2} - 1}\left( {x - 1}\right) \) ,

当 \( x =  - 1 \) 时, \( {y}_{A} = \frac{{y}_{0} - 1}{{y}_{0} + 1} \) ,

直线 \( {QM} : y + 1 = \frac{{y}_{0} + 1}{{y}_{0}^{2} - 1}\left( {x - 1}\right) , x =  - 1 \) 时, \( {y}_{B} = \frac{-{y}_{0} - 1}{{y}_{0} - 1},\therefore {y}_{A}{y}_{B} =  - 1 \) ,

\( \therefore {y}_{A} \cdot  {y}_{B} \) 为常数 -1 .

(3) 是否存在 \( t \) ,使得 \( {y}_{A} \cdot  {y}_{B} = 1 \) 且 \( {y}_{P} \cdot  {y}_{Q} \) 为常数? 若存在,求出 \( t \) 的所有可能值,若不存在,请说明理由.

【答案】存在 \( t = 1 \) ,使得 \( {y}_{A} \cdot  {y}_{B} = 1 \) 且 \( {y}_{P} \cdot  {y}_{Q} = 1 \) 为常数 1

设 \( M\left( {{y}_{0}^{2},{y}_{0}}\right) ,\;A\left( {t,{y}_{A}}\right) \) ,直线 \( {MA} : y - {y}_{0} = \frac{{y}_{0} - {y}_{A}}{{y}_{0}^{2} - t}\left( {x - {y}_{0}^{2}}\right) \) ,

联立 \( {y}^{2} = x \) ,得 \( {y}^{2} - \frac{{y}_{0}^{2} - t}{{y}_{0} - {y}_{A}} + \frac{{y}_{0}^{2} - t}{{y}_{0} - {y}_{A}}{y}_{0} - {y}_{0}^{2} = 0 \) ,

\( \therefore {y}_{0} + {y}_{P} = \frac{{y}_{0}^{2} - t}{{y}_{0} - {y}_{A}} \) ,即 \( {y}_{P} = \frac{{y}_{0}{y}_{A} - t}{{y}_{0} - {y}_{A}} \) ,

同理得 \( {y}_{Q} = \frac{{y}_{0}{y}_{B} - 1}{{y}_{0} - {y}_{B}} \) ,

\( \because {y}_{A} \cdot  {y}_{B} = 1 \) ,

\( \therefore {y}_{P}{y}_{Q} = \frac{{y}_{0}^{2} - t{y}_{0}\left( {{y}_{A} + {y}_{B}}\right)  + {t}^{2}}{{y}_{0}^{2} - {y}_{0}\left( {{y}_{A} + {y}_{B}}\right)  + 1} \) ,

要使 \( {y}_{P}{y}_{Q} \) 为常数,即 \( t = 1 \) ,此时 \( {y}_{P}{y}_{Q} \) 为常数 1,

\( \therefore \) 存在 \( t = 1 \) ,使得 \( {y}_{A} \cdot  {y}_{B} = 1 \) 且 \( {y}_{P} \cdot  {y}_{Q} \) 为常数 1 .

21. 已知非空集合 \( A \subseteq  R \) ,函数 \( y = f\left( x\right) \) 的定义域为 \( D \) ,若对任意 \( t \in  A \) 且 \( x \in  D \) ,不等式 \( f\left( x\right) \)

\( \leq  f\left( {x + t}\right) \) 恒成立,则称函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 具有 \( A \) 性质.

(1) 当 \( A = \{  - 1\} \) ,判断 \( f\left( x\right)  =  - x\text{ 、 }g\left( x\right)  = {2x} \) 是否具有性质;

【答案】 \( f\left( x\right)  =  - x \) 具有 \( A \) 性质； \( g\left( x\right)  = {2x} \) 不具有 \( A \) 性质

\( \because f\left( x\right)  =  - x \) 为减函数,

\( \therefore f\left( x\right)  < f\left( {x - 1}\right) \) ,

\( \therefore f\left( x\right)  =  - x \) 具有 \( A \) 性质;

\( \because g\left( x\right)  = {2x} \) 为增函数,

\( \therefore g\left( x\right)  > g\left( {x - 1}\right) \) ,

\( \therefore g\left( x\right)  = {2x} \) 不具有 \( A \) 性质.

(2) 当 \( A = \left( {0,1}\right) , f\left( x\right)  = x + {1x}, x \in  \lbrack a, + \infty ) \) ,若 \( f\left( x\right) \) 具有 \( A \) 性质,求 \( a \) 的取值范围;

【答案】 \( \lbrack 1, + \infty ) \)

依题意,对任意 \( t \in  \left( {0,1}\right) , f\left( x\right)  \leq  f\left( {x + t}\right) \) 恒成立,

\( \therefore f\left( x\right)  = x + {1x}\left( {x \geq  a}\right) \) 为增函数 (不可能为常值函数),

由双勾函数的图象及性质可得 \( a \geq  1 \) ,

当 \( a \geq  1 \) 时,函数单调递增,满足对任意 \( t \in  \left( {0,1}\right) , f\left( x\right)  \leq  f\left( {x + t}\right) \) 恒成立,

综上,实数 \( a \) 的取值范围为 \( \lbrack 1, + \infty ) \) .

(3) 当 \( A = \{  - 2, m\} , m \in  Z \) ,若 \( D \) 为整数集且具有 \( A \) 性质的函数均为常值函数,求所有符合条件的 \( m \) 的值.

【答案】 \( m \) 为奇数

\( \because D \) 为整数集,具有 \( A \) 性质的函数均为常值函数,

\( \therefore \) 当 \( t =  - 2, f\left( x\right)  = f\left( {x - 2}\right) \) 恒成立,即 \( f\left( {2k}\right)  = p\left( {k \in  Z}\right) , f\left( {{2n} - 1}\right)  = q\left( {n \in  Z}\right) \) ,

由题意， \( p = q \) ，则 \( f\left( {2k}\right)  = f\left( {{2n} - 1}\right) \) ，

当 \( x = {2k} \) ， \( f\left( x\right)  = f\left( {x + {2n} - {2k} - 1}\right) \) ， \( \therefore m = {2n} - {2k} - 1\left( {n, k \in  Z}\right) \) ，

当 \( x = {2n} - 1, f\left( x\right)  = f\left( {x + {2k} - {2n} + 1}\right) ,\;\therefore m = {2k} - {2n} + 1\left( {n, k \in  Z}\right) \) ,

综上, \( m \) 为奇数.

## 2021 秋考

一、填空题 (本大题共 12 题,满分 54 分,第 \( 1 \sim  6 \) 题每题 4 分,第 \( 7 \sim  {12} \) 题每题 5 分)

1. 已知 \( {z}_{1} = 1 + \mathrm{i},{z}_{2} = 2 + 3\mathrm{i} \) ，则 \( {z}_{1} + {z}_{2} = \) ___.

【答案】 \( 3 + 4\mathrm{i} \)

\[
{z}_{1} + {z}_{2} = 1 + \mathrm{i} + 2 + 3\mathrm{i} = 3 + 4\mathrm{i}.
\]

2. 已知 \( A = \{ x \mid  {2x} \leq  1\} , B = \{  - 1,0,1\} \) ,则 \( A \cap  B = \) ___.

【答案】 \( \{  - 1,0\} \)

\( A = \left( {-\infty ,\frac{1}{2}}\right\rbrack  ,\;B = \{  - 1,0,1\} ,\;A \cap  B = \{  - 1,0\} . \)

3. 已知圆 \( {x}^{2} + {y}^{2} - {2x} - {4y} = 0 \) ，则该圆的圆心坐标为___.

【答案】 \( \left( {1,2}\right) \)

\( {x}^{2} + {y}^{2} - {2x} - {4y} = 0 \Rightarrow  {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2} + {\left( y - 2\right) }^{2} = 5 \) ,故圆心为 \( \left( {1,2}\right) \) .

4. 正方形 \( {ABCD} \) 的边长为 3，则 \( \overrightarrow{AB} \cdo![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_320_261_1806_279_238_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_320_261_1806_279_238_0.jpg)9b5b00_320_261_1806_279_238_0.jpg)

【答案】 9

由数量积几何意义, \( \overrightarrow{AB} \cdot  \overrightarrow{AC} = {\overrightarrow{AB}}^{2} = 9 \) .

5. 已知 \( f\left( x\right)  = \frac{3}{x} + 2 \) ,则 \( {f}^{-1}\left( 1\right)  = \) ___.

【答案】-3

\( f\left( x\right)  = \frac{3}{x} + 2 = 1 \Rightarrow  x =  - 3,\;\therefore f\left( {-3}\right)  = 1 \Rightarrow  {f}^{-1}\left( 1\right)  =  - 3. \)

6. 已知二项式 \( {\left( x + a\right) }^{5} \) 展开式中， \( {x}^{2} \) 项的系数为 80，则 \( a = \) ___.

【答案】 2

\( {C}_{5}^{3}{x}^{2}{a}^{3} = {80}{x}^{2} \Rightarrow  a = 2. \)

7. 已知实数 \( x \) 、 \( y \) 满足 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} x \leq  3 \\  {2x} - y - 2 \geq  0 \\  {3x} + y - 8 \geq  0 \end{array}\right. \) ，则 \( z = x - y \) 的最大值为___.

【答案】 4

可行域的三个顶点为 \( \left( {3,4}\right) \text{ 、 }\left( {2,2}\right) \text{ 、 }\left( {3, - 1}\right) \) ,可知 \( {z}_{\max } = 3 - \left( {-1}\right)  = 4 \) .

8. 已知无穷等比数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 和 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) ,满足 \( {a}_{1} = 3,{b}_{n} = {a}_{2n},{a}_{n} \) 的各项和为 9,则数列 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 的各项和为___.

【答案】 \( \frac{18}{5} \)

\[
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\left( {{a}_{1} + {a}_{2} +  + {a}_{n}}\right)  = \frac{3}{1 - q} = 9 \Rightarrow  q = \frac{2}{3},\;{a}_{2} = {a}_{1}q = 2,
\]

\[
\therefore \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\left( {{a}_{2} + {a}_{4} +  + {a}_{2n}}\right)  = \frac{{a}_{2}}{1 - {q}^{2}} = \frac{18}{5}\text{ . }
\]

9. 已知圆柱的底面半径为 1,高为 2, \( {AB} \) 为上底面圆的一条直径， \( C \) 为下底面圆周上的一个动点,则 \( {ABC} \) 的面积的取值范围为___.

【答案】 \( \left\lbrack  {2,\sqrt{5}}\right\rbrack \)

\[
{S}_{ABC} = \frac{1}{2}{AB} \cdot  h = h,\;\because h \in  \left\lbrack  {2,\sqrt{5}}\right\rbrack  ,\;\therefore {S}_{ABC} \in  \left\lbrack  {2,\sqrt{5}}\right\rbrack  .
\]

10. 已知花博会有四个不同的场馆 \( A \) 、 \( B \) 、 \( C \) 、 \( D \) ，甲、乙两人每人选 2 个去参观，则他们的选择中, 恰有一个场馆相同的概率为___.

【答案】 23

\[
\frac{{C}_{4}^{1}{A}_{3}^{2}}{{C}_{4}^{2}{C}_{4}^{2}} = \frac{2}{3}.
\]

11. 已知抛物线: \( {y}^{2} = {2px}\left( {p0}\right) \) ,若第一象限的 \( A, B \) 两点在抛物线上,焦点为 \( F,\left| {AF}\right|  = 2 \) , \( \left| {BF}\right|  = 4 \) ， \( \left| {AB}\right|  = 3 \) ，则直线 \( {AB} \) 的斜率为___![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_323_406_217_412_404_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_323_406_217_412_404_0.jpg)39b5b00_323_406_217_412_404_0.jpg)

设 \( A\left( {{x}_{1},{y}_{1}}\right) , B\left( {{x}_{2},{y}_{2}}\right) ,\left| {AF}\right|  = {x}_{1} + \frac{p}{2} = 2,\left| {BF}\right|  = {x}_{2} + \frac{p}{2} = 4 \) ,

\( \therefore \left| {{x}_{1} - {x}_{2}}\right|  = 2 \) ,由 \( \left| {AB}\right|  = \sqrt{1 + {k}^{2}}\left| {{x}_{1} - {x}_{2}}\right|  = 3 \) ,且 \( k > 0,\therefore k = \frac{\sqrt{5}}{2} \) .

\( A{A}_{1} = 2, B{B}_{1} = 4, \)

由 \( \frac{A{A}_{1}}{B{B}_{1}} = \frac{1}{2} \Rightarrow  {AP} = {AB} = 3 \)

\( \therefore \cos \angle {AB}{B}_{1} = \frac{B{B}_{1}}{BP} = \frac{4}{6} \Rightarrow  \tan \angle {AB}{B}_{1} = \frac{\sqrt{5}}{2} \)

即: \( {k}_{AB} = \frac{\sqrt{5}}{2} \) .

12. 已知 \( a \in  {N}^{ * }\left( {\mathrm{i} = 1,2,,9}\right) \) ,对任意的 \( k \in  {N}^{ * }\left( {2 \leq  k \leq  8}\right) ,{a}_{k} = {a}_{k - 1} + 1 \) 或 \( {a}_{k} = {a}_{k + 1} - 1 \) 中有且仅有一个成立,且 \( {a}_{1} = 6,{a}_{9} = 9 \) ,则 \( {a}_{1} +  + {a}_{9} \) 的最小值为___.

## 【答案】31

令 \( {b}_{k} = {a}_{k + 1} - {a}_{k} \) ,则依题意: \( {b}_{k} \) 和 \( {b}_{k + 1} \) 中,仅有 1 个为 1 (即只能隔项为 1 )

若 \( {b}_{1} = {b}_{3} = {b}_{5} = {b}_{7} = 1 \) ,则: \( {a}_{1} = 6,{a}_{2} = 7,{a}_{3} \geq  1,{a}_{4} \geq  2,{a}_{5} \geq  1,{a}_{6} \geq  2,{a}_{7} \; \geq  1,{a}_{8} \geq  2,{a}_{9} = 9 \) ,此时: \( {a}_{1} +  + {a}_{9} \) 最小值为 31 .

若 \( {b}_{2} = {b}_{4} = {b}_{6} = {b}_{8} = 1 \) ,则 \( {a}_{2} \geq  1,{a}_{3} \geq  2,{a}_{4} \geq  1,{a}_{5} \geq  2,{a}_{6} \geq  1,{a}_{7} \geq  2,{a}_{8} = \) 8, \( {a}_{9} = 9 \) ,此时: \( {a}_{1} +  + {a}_{9} \) 最小值为 32 .

综上: \( {a}_{1} +  + {a}_{9} \) 最小值为 31 .

二、选择题 (本大题共 4 题, 每题 5 分, 共 20 分)

13. 下列函数中, 既是奇函数又是减函数的是 ( )

A. \( y =  - {3x} \) B. \( y = {x}^{3} \) C. \( y = {\log }_{3}x \) D. \( y = {3}^{x} \)

## 【答案】 \( A \)

选项 \( {BCD} \) 均为增函数.

14. 已知参数方程 \( \left\{  {\begin{array}{l} x = {3t} - 4{t}^{3} \\  y = {2t}\sqrt{1 - {t}^{2}} \end{array}, t \in  \left\lbrack  {-1,1}\right\rbrack  }\ri![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_324_353_872_262_251_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_324_353_872_262_251_0.jpg)39b5b0![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_324_951_878_268_250_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_324_951_878_268_250_0.jpg)39b5b0![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_324_372_1157_256_244_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_324_372_1157_256_244_0.jpg)9b5b00![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_324_948_1154_306_247_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_324_948_1154_306_247_0.jpg)9b5b00_324_948_1154_306_247_0.jpg)

【答案】 \( B \)

特殊值法,当 \( y = 0 \) 时, \( t = 0\text{ 、 }1\text{ 、 } - 1 \) ,对应 \( x = 0\text{ 、 } - 1\text{ 、 }1 \) . 故选 \( B \)

15. 已知 \( f\left( x\right)  = 3\sin x + 2 \) ,对任意的 \( {x}_{1} \in  \left\lbrack  {0,\frac{\pi }{2}}\right\rbrack \) ,都存在 \( {x}_{2} \in  \left\lbrack  {0,\frac{\pi }{2}}\right\rbrack \) ,使得 \( f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  = {2f}\left( {{x}_{2} + \theta }\right) \; + 2 \) 成立,则下列选项中, \( \theta \) 可能的值为 ( )

A. \( \frac{3\pi }{5} \) B. \( \frac{4\pi }{5} \) C. \( \frac{6\pi }{5} \) D. \( \frac{7\pi }{5} \)

【答案】 \( B \)

设 \( f\left( x\right) \) 范围为 \( A,{2f}\left( {{x}_{2} + \theta }\right)  + 2 \) 范围为 \( B \) ,由题意， \( A \subseteq  B \) ,

\( \because f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  \in  \left\lbrack  {2,5}\right\rbrack \) ,且 \( {2f}\left( {{x}_{2} + \theta }\right)  + 2 = 6\sin \left( {{x}_{2} + \theta }\right)  + 6 \) ,

当 \( \theta  = \frac{4\pi }{5} \) 时, \( {x}_{2} + \theta  \in  \left\lbrack  {\frac{4\pi }{5},\frac{13\pi }{10}}\right\rbrack \) ,

\( 6\sin \left( {{x}_{2} + \theta }\right)  + 6 \in  \left\lbrack  {6\sin \frac{13\pi }{10} + 6,6\sin \frac{4\pi }{5} + 6}\right\rbrack  ,\;6\sin \frac{13\pi }{10} + 6 < 2,\;6\sin \frac{4\pi }{5} + 6 > 5, \) 符合题意.

故选 \( B \)

16. 已知实数 \( {x}_{1}\text{ 、 }{y}_{1}\text{ 、 }{x}_{2}\text{ 、 }{y}_{2}\text{ 、 }{x}_{3}\text{ 、 }{y}_{3} \) 为同时满足: ① \( {x}_{1} < {y}_{1}\text{ ， }{x}_{2} < {y}_{2}\text{ ， }{x}_{3} < {y}_{3} \) ; ② \( {x}_{1} + {y}_{1} = \; {x}_{2} + {y}_{2} = {x}_{3} + {y}_{3} \) ; ③ \( {x}_{1}{y}_{1} + {x}_{3}{y}_{3} = 2{x}_{2}{y}_{2} \) ，则下列选项恒成立的是 ( )

A. \( 2{x}_{2} < {x}_{1} + {x}_{3} \) B. \( 2{x}_{2} > {x}_{1} + {x}_{3} \) C. \( {x}_{2}^{2} < {x}_{1}{x}_{3} \) D. \( {x}_{2}^{2} >![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_325_426_1086_810_660_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_325_426_1086_810_660_0.jpg)9b5b00_325_426_1086_810_660_0.jpg)

令 \( {x}_{1} + {y}_{1} = {x}_{2} + {y}_{2} = {x}_{3} + {y}_{3} = {2a} \) ,由①可知, \( {x}_{1} < a,{x}_{2} < a,{x}_{3} < a \) ,

由③得， \( {x}_{1}\left( {{2a} - {x}_{1}}\right)  + {x}_{3}\left( {{2a} - {x}_{3}}\right)  = 2{x}_{2}\left( {{2a} - {x}_{2}}\right) \) ，构造函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = x\left( {{2a} - x}\right) \) ，

\( \therefore f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  + f\left( {x}_{3}\right)  = {2f}\left( {x}_{2}\right) \) ,如图所示, \( f\left( x\right) \) 为上凸函数,满足

\( f\left( \frac{{x}_{1} + {x}_{3}}{2}\right) \frac{f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  + f\left( {x}_{3}\right) }{2} = f\left( {x}_{2}\right) , \)

\( \because f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( \left( {-\infty , a}\right) \) 上严格增, \( \therefore \frac{{x}_{1} + {x}_{3}}{2} > {x}_{2} \) .

三、解答题 (本大题共 5 题, 共 \( {14} + {14} + {14} + {16} + {18} = {76} \) 分)

17. 如图,在长方体 \( {ABCD} - {A}_{1}{B}_{1}{C}_{1}{D}_{1} \) ,已知 \( {A![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_326_264_649_303_316_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_326_264_649_303_316_0.jpg)39b5b00_326_264_649_303_316_0.jpg)

(1)若点 \( P \) 是棱 \( {A}_{1}{D}_{1} \) 上的动点，求三棱锥 \( C - {PAD} \) 的体积；

【答案】 2

\[
{V}_{P - {ADC}} = \frac{1}{3} \cdot  {S}_{AOC} \cdot  h = \frac{1}{3} \times  2 \times  3 = 2.
\]

( 2 )求直线 \( A{B}_{1} \) 与平面 \( {AC}{C}_{1}{A}_{1} \) 的夹角大小.

\( \arcsin \frac{\sqrt{26}}{13} \)

\( {d}_{{B}_{1} - {AC}{C}_{1}{A}_{1}} = {d}_{{B}_{1} - {C}_{1}{A}_{1}} = \sqrt{2},\;A{B}_{1} = \sqrt{13}, \)

\( \therefore \sin \theta  = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{13}} = \frac{\sqrt{26}}{13} \) ,即所求角为 \( \arcsin \frac{\sqrt{26}}{13} \) .

18. 已知在 \( {ABC} \) 中， \( A \) 、 \( B \) 、 \( C \) 所对边分别为 \( a \) 、 \( b \) 、 \( c \) ，且 \( a = 3 \) ， \( b = {2c} \) .

(1)若 \( A = \frac{2\pi }{3} \) ，求 \( {ABC} \) 的面积；

【答案】 \( \frac{9\sqrt{3}}{14} \)

\[
\cos A = \frac{{b}^{2} + {c}^{2} - {a}^{2}}{2bc} \Rightarrow   - \frac{1}{2} = \frac{4{c}^{2} + {c}^{2} - 9}{4{c}^{2}} \Rightarrow  c = \frac{3\sqrt{7}}{7}\text{ , }
\]

\[
{S}_{ABC} = \frac{1}{2}{bc}\sin A = \frac{1}{2} \times  2 \times  \frac{9}{7} \times  \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} = \frac{9\sqrt{3}}{14}.
\]

(2) 若 \( 2\sin B - \sin C = 1 \) ，求 \( {ABC} \) 的周长.

【答案】 \( 4\sqrt{2} - \sqrt{5} + 3 \) 或 \( 4\sqrt{2} + \sqrt{5} + 3 \)

依题意,正弦定理: \( \frac{b}{\sin B} = \frac{c}{\sin C} \Rightarrow  \sin B = 2\sin C \) ,

\( \therefore \) 代入计算: \( 4\sin C - \sin C = 1 \Rightarrow  \sin C = \frac{1}{3} \) ,则 \( \sin B = \frac{2}{3} \)

当 \( B \) 为锐角时,

\( \sin A = \sin \left( {B + C}\right)  = \sin B\cos C + \cos B\sin C = \frac{2}{3} \times  \frac{2\sqrt{2}}{3} + \frac{\sqrt{5}}{3} \times  \frac{1}{3} = \frac{4\sqrt{2} + \sqrt{5}}{9} \)

\( \frac{a}{\sin A} = \frac{b}{\sin B} = \frac{c}{\sin C} \Rightarrow  \left\{  \begin{array}{l} c = \frac{4\sqrt{2} + \sqrt{5}}{3} \\  b = \frac{8\sqrt{2} + 2\sqrt{5}}{3} \end{array}\right. \)

\( \therefore {C}_{ABC} = 4\sqrt{2} + \sqrt{5} + 3 \)

综上: \( {C}_{ABC} = 4\sqrt{2} - \sqrt{5} + 3 \) 或 \( 4\sqrt{2} + \sqrt{5} + 3 \) .

19. 已知某企业今年(2021 年)第一季度的营业额为 1.1 亿元，以后每个季度的营业额比上个季度增加 0.05 亿元，该企业第一季度的利润为 0.16 亿，以后每季度比前一季度增长 4%.

(1)求2021年起前 20 季度营业额的总和；

【答案】31.5 亿

依题意: 营业额是首项为 1.1 , 公差为 0.05 的等差数列;

\( \therefore \) 前 20 季度营业额之和为: \( {S}_{20} = {20} \times  {1.1} + \frac{{20} \times  {19}}{2} \times  {0.05} = {31.5} \) (亿).

(2)请问哪一季度的利润首次超过该季度营业额的 18%？

## 【答案】 26

设 2021 年起第 \( n \) 季度 \( \left( {n \in  {N}^{ * }}\right) \) 满足条件,依题意:

第 \( n \) 季度的营业额为: \( {a}_{n} = {1.1} + \left( {n - 1}\right)  \times  {0.05} = {0.05n} + {1.05} \) ,

第 \( n \) 季度的利润为: \( {0.16} \times  {\left( 1 + 4\% \right) }^{n - 1} \) ,

依题意: \( {0.16} \times  {\left( 1 + 4\% \right) }^{n - 1} \geq  \left( {{0.05n} + {1.05}}\right)  \times  {18}\% \) ,解得: \( n \geq  {26} \)

即今年起第 26 个季度时满足条件.

20. 已知椭圆 \( \Gamma  : \frac{{x}^{2}}{2} + {y}^{2} = 1,{F}_{1}\text{ 、 }{F}_{2} \) 是其左右焦点,直线 \( l \) 过点 \( P\left( {m,0}\right) \left( {m <  - \sqrt{2}}\right) \) 交椭圆 \( \Gamma \) 于 \( A\text{ 、 }B \) 两点,且 \( A\text{ 、 }B \) 在 \( x \) 轴上方,点 \( A \) 在线段 \( {BP} \) 上.

(1)若 \( B \) 是上顶点， \( \left| \overrightarrow{B{F}_{1}}\right|  = \left| \overrightarrow{P{F}_{1}}\right| \) ，求 \( m \) 的值；

【答案】 \( - 1 - \sqrt{2} \)

依题意: \( {a}^{2} = 2,{b}^{2} = 1 \) ,半焦距 \( c = 1 \) ,

则 \( \left| \overrightarrow{B{F}_{1}}\right|  = \left| \overrightarrow{P{F}_{1}}\right|  = a = \sqrt{2} \)

\( \therefore \left| {OP}\right|  = \left| {P{F}_{1}}\right|  + c = \sqrt{2} + 1 \) ,

此时: \( m =  - 1 - \sqrt{2} \) .

( 2 )若 \( \overrightarrow{{F}_{1}A} \cdot  \overrightarrow{{F}_{2}A} = {13} \) ，且原点 \( O \) 到直线 \( l \) 的距离为 \( \frac{4\sqrt{15}}{15} \) ，求直线 \( l \) 的方程；

【答案】 \( y = \frac{1}{3}\left( {x + \frac{4\sqrt{6}}{3}}\right) \)

设直线 \( l \) 的方程为: \( y = k\left( {x - m}\right) \) ( \( k \) 必存在)，又 \( A, B \) 在 \( x \) 轴上方，点 \( A \) 在线段 \( {BP} \) 上，

则设 \( A\left( {{x}_{1},{y}_{1}}\right) \) ,且 \( {x}_{1} < 0 \) ,

又 \( {F}_{1}\left( {-1,0}\right) ,{F}_{2}\left( {1,0}\right) \) ,

故有 \( {F}_{1}A \cdot  {F}_{2}A = \left( {{x}_{1} + 1}\right) \left( {{x}_{1} - 1}\right)  + {y}_{1}^{2} = {x}_{1}^{2} - 1 + {y}_{1}^{2} = \frac{1}{3} \)

又 \( \frac{{x}_{1}^{2}}{2} + {y}_{1}^{2} = 1 \Rightarrow  {y}_{1}^{2} = 1 - \frac{{x}_{1}^{2}}{2} \) ,

代入 \( \overrightarrow{{F}_{1}A} \cdot  {}^{3}{F}_{2}A = {x}_{1}^{2} + {y}_{1}^{2} - 1 = {x}_{1}^{2} + 1 - \frac{{x}_{1}^{2}}{2} - 1 = \frac{1}{3} \)

\( \Rightarrow  {x}_{1} =  - \frac{\sqrt{6}}{3} \) (正值舍去)

则 \( {y}_{1} = \frac{\sqrt{6}}{3} \) ,

即直线 \( l \) 满足 \( \frac{\sqrt{6}}{3} = k \cdot  \left( {-\frac{\sqrt{6}}{3} - m}\right) \) ①

又点 \( O \) 到直线 \( l \) 的距离 \( d = \frac{\left| \mathrm{{km}}\right| }{\sqrt{1 + {k}^{2}}} = \frac{4\sqrt{15}}{15} \) ②

联立①②可得 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} m =  - \frac{4\sqrt{6}}{3} \\  k = \frac{1}{3} \end{array}\right. \) (另一组解舍去，因与 \( m <  - \sqrt{2} \) 矛盾)，

即直线 \( l \) 的方程为: \( y = \frac{1}{3}\left( {x + \frac{4\sqrt{6}}{3}}\right) \) .

(3)对于任意点 \( P \) ，是否存在唯一直线 \( l \) ，使得 \( \overrightarrow{{F}_{1}A}//\overrightarrow{{F}_{2}B} \) 成立，若存在，求出直线 \( l \) 的斜率，若不存在, 请说明理由.

【答案】 \( \sqrt{\frac{1}{2{m}^{2} - 4}} \)

设直线 \( l \) 的方程为: \( y = k\left( {x - m}\right) \left( {k0}\right) \) ， \( A\left( {{x}_{1},{y}_{1}}\right) \) ， \( B\left( {{x}_{2},{y}_{2}}\right) \) ，

又 \( {F}_{1}\left( {-1,0}\right) ,{F}_{2}\left( {1,0}\right) \) ,

则 \( \overrightarrow{{F}_{1}A} = \left( {{x}_{1} + 1,{y}_{1}}\right) \) ,

\( \overrightarrow{{F}_{2}B} = \left( {{x}_{2} + 1,{y}_{2}}\right) , \)

\( \overrightarrow{{F}_{1}A}//\overrightarrow{{F}_{2}B} \Rightarrow  \left( {{x}_{1} + 1}\right)  \cdot  {y}_{2} = \left( {{x}_{2} - 1}\right)  \cdot  {y}_{1}, \)

则 \( \left( {{x}_{1} + 1}\right)  \cdot  k\left( {{x}_{2} - m}\right)  = \left( {{x}_{2} - 1}\right)  \cdot  k\left( {{x}_{1} - m}\right) \) ,

化简可得: \( {x}_{1} + {x}_{2} + m\left( {{x}_{2} - {x}_{1}}\right)  - {2m} = 0 \) ,

联立:

\( \left\{  {\begin{array}{l} y = k\left( {x - m}\right) \\  {x}^{2} + 2{y}^{2} = 2 \end{array} \Rightarrow  \left( {1 + 2{k}^{2}}\right) {x}^{2} - {4m}{k}^{2}x + 2{k}^{2}{m}^{2} - 2 = 0,}\right. \)

\( \Delta  > 0 \) ,

则 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {x}_{1} + {x}_{2} = \frac{4mk}{1 + 2{k}^{2}} \\  {x}_{1}{x}_{2} = \frac{2{k}^{2}{m}^{2} - 2}{1 + 2{k}^{2}} \end{array}\right. \)

则可得

\( \frac{{4m}{k}^{2}}{1 + 2{k}^{2}} + m\left( {{x}_{2} - {x}_{1}}\right)  - {2m} = 0 \Rightarrow  {x}_{2} - {x}_{1} = \frac{2}{1 + 2{k}^{2}} \) ,

又: \( {\left( {x}_{2} - {x}_{1}\right) }^{2} = {\left( {x}_{1} + {x}_{2}\right) }^{2} - 4{x}_{1}{x}_{2} = {\left( \frac{2}{1 + 2{k}^{2}}\right) }^{2} \) ,

代入 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {x}_{1} + {x}_{2} = \frac{4mk}{1 + 2{k}^{2}} \\  {x}_{1}{x}_{2} = \frac{2{k}^{2}{m}^{2} - 2}{1 + 2{k}^{2}} \end{array}\right. \)

化简可得: \( 4{k}^{2} - 2{k}^{2}{m}^{2} + 1 = 0 \Rightarrow  {k}^{2} = \frac{1}{2{m}^{2} - 4} \) ,

则 \( k = \sqrt{\frac{1}{2{m}^{2} - 4}}, m <  - \sqrt{2} \) ,

故对于任意点 \( P \) ,存在唯一直线 \( l \) ,使得 \( \overrightarrow{{F}_{1}A}//\overrightarrow{{F}_{2}B} \) 成立,此时直线 \( l \) 的斜率为 \( \sqrt{\frac{1}{2{m}^{2} - 4}} \) .

21. 已知 \( f\left( x\right) \) 是定义在 \( R \) 上的函数,若对任意的 \( {x}_{1}\text{ 、 }{x}_{2} \in  R,{x}_{1} - {x}_{2} \in  S \) ,均有 \( f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{2}\right) \; \in  S \) ,则称 \( f\left( x\right) \) 是 \( S \) 关联.

(1)判断和证明 \( f\left( x\right)  = {2x} + 1 \) 是否是 \( \left\lbrack  {0,\infty }\right) \) 关联? 是否是 \( \left\lbrack  {0![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_330_431_268_377_326_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_330_431_268_377_326_0.jpg)39b5b00_330_431_268_377_326_0.jpg)

任取 \( {x}_{1},\;{x}_{2} \in  R \) ,若 \( {x}_{1} - {x}_{2} \in  \lbrack 0, + \infty ) \) ,

则: \( f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  = 2\left( {{x}_{1} - {x}_{2}}\right)  \in  \lbrack 0, + \infty ),\therefore f\left( x\right) \) 是 \( \lbrack 0, + \infty ) \) 关联;

若 \( {x}_{1} - {x}_{2} \in  \left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack \) ,则 \( f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  = 2\left( {{x}_{1} - {x}_{2}}\right)  \in  \left\lbrack  {0,2}\right\rbrack  ,\therefore f\left( x\right) \) 不是 \( \left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack \) 关联.

( 2 )若 \( f\left( x\right) \) 是 \( \{ 3\} \) 关联，当 \( x \in  \lbrack 0,3) \) 时， \( f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{2} - {2x} \) ，解不等式 \( 2 \leq  f\left( x\right)  \leq  3 \) ；

【答案】 \( x \in  \left\lbrack  {1 + \sqrt{3},5}\right\rbrack \)

依题意: 当 \( {x}_{1} - {x}_{2} = 3 \) 时,

\( f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  = 3 \) ,即满足: \( f\left( {x + 3}\right)  - f\left( x\right)  = 3 \)

数形结合: 求出 \( A\left( {1 + \sqrt{3},2}\right) , B\left( {5,3}\right) \) ,

\( \therefore \) 原不等式的解集为: \( x \in  \left\lbrack  {1 + \sqrt{3},5}\right\rbrack \) .

(3)证明: “ \( f\left( x\right) \) 是 \( \{ 1\} \) 关联，且是 \( \lbrack 0, + \infty ) \) 关联” 的充要条件是 “ \( f\left( x\right) \) 是 \( \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack \) 关联” .

【答案】见解析

必要性:

根据条件可以得到 \( f\left( {x + 1}\right)  = f\left( x\right)  + 1 \) ,

\[
\therefore f\left( {x + n}\right)  = f\left( x\right)  + n, n \in  Z,{x}_{2} \geq  {x}_{1}, f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  \geq  f\left( {x}_{1}\right) \text{ , }
\]

若 \( 1 \leq  {x}_{2} - {x}_{1} \leq  2,\therefore {x}_{1} + 1 \leq  {x}_{2} \leq  {x}_{1} + 2,\;\therefore f\left( {{x}_{1} + 1}\right)  \leq  f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  \leq  f\left( {{x}_{2} + 2}\right) \)

\( \therefore f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  + 1 \leq  f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  \leq  f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  + 2,\;\therefore 1 \leq  f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  \leq  2,\;\therefore f\left( x\right) \) 是 \( \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack \) 关联;

充分性: \( 1 \leq  {x}_{2} - {x}_{1} \leq  2,\;1 \leq  f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  \leq  2 \) ,

\( 1 \leq  f\left( {x + 2}\right)  - f\left( {x + 1}\right)  \leq  2,\;1 \leq  f\left( {x + 1}\right)  - f\left( x\right)  \leq  2, \)

\( \therefore 2 \leq  f\left( {x + 2}\right)  - f\left( x\right)  \leq  4 \) ,又 \( 1 \leq  \left( {x + 2}\right)  - x \leq  2,\therefore 1 \leq  f\left( {x + 2}\right)  - f\left( x\right)  \leq  2 \) ,

\( \therefore f\left( {x + 2}\right)  - f\left( x\right)  = 2,\therefore f\left( {x + 2}\right)  - f\left( {x + 1}\right)  = 1, f\left( {x + 1}\right)  - f\left( x\right)  = 1 \) , \( f\left( {x + n}\right)  = f\left( x\right)  + n, n \in  Z,\therefore f\left( x\right) \) 是 \( \{ 1\} \) 关联;

若 \( {x}_{2} - {x}_{1} \in  \left\lbrack  {n, n + 1}\right\rbrack  , n \in  N,{x}_{2} - \left\lbrack  {x + \left( {n - 1}\right) }\right\rbrack   \in  \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack  , n - 1 \in  Z \) ,

\( \therefore f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  - f\left\lbrack  {{x}_{1} + \left( {n - 1}\right) }\right\rbrack   \in  \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack  ,\;f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  - \left( {n - 1}\right)  \in  \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack \) ,

\( \therefore f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  \in  \left\lbrack  {n, n + 1}\right\rbrack   \subseteq  \lbrack 0, + \infty ) \) ,而 \( \lbrack 0, + \infty ) = \left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack   \cup  \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack   \cup   +  \cup  \left\lbrack  {n, n + 1}\right\rbrack \) U,

\( \therefore {x}_{2} - {x}_{1} \in  \lbrack 0, + \infty ),\;\therefore \) 存在 \( n \) 使 \( {x}_{2} - {x}_{1} \in  \left\lbrack  {n, n + 1}\right\rbrack  , f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  \in  \left\lbrack  {n, n + 1}\right\rbrack   \subseteq \)

\( \lbrack 0, + \infty ) \)

\( \therefore f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  \in  \lbrack 0, + \infty ) \) ,故 \( f\left( x\right) \) 是 \( \lbrack 0, + \infty ) \) 关联.

## 2021春考

一、填空题 (本大题共 12 题,满分 54 分,第 \( 1 \sim  6 \) 题每题 4 分,第 7 \( \sim  {12} \) 题每题 5 分) 1. 已知等差数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的首项为3，公差为2，则 \( {a}_{10} = \) ___.

## 【答案】 21

【分析】: 由已知结合等差数列的通项公式即可直接求解.

因为等差数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的首项为 3,公差为 2,

则 \( {a}_{10} = {a}_{1} + {9d} = 3 + 9 \times  2 = {21} \) .

21.

2. 已知 \( z = 1 - 3\mathrm{i} \) ，则 \( \left| {\bar{z} - \mathrm{i}}\right|  = \) ___.

## 【答案】 √5

【分析】: 由已知求得 \( \bar{z} - \mathrm{i} \) ,再由复数模的计算公式求解.

\( \because z = 1 - 3\mathrm{i} \) ,

\( \therefore \bar{z} - \mathrm{i} = 1 + 3\mathrm{i} - \mathrm{i} = 1 + 2\mathrm{i} \) ,

则 \( \left| {\bar{z} - \mathrm{i}}\right|  = \left| {1 + 2\mathrm{i}}\right|  = \sqrt{\left( {1}^{2} + {2}^{2}\right) } = \sqrt{5} \) .

\( \sqrt{5} \) .

3. 已知圆柱的底面半径为 1 ，母线长为 2 ，则该圆柱的侧面积等于 ___.

## 【答案】 \( {4\pi } \)

\( \because \) 圆柱的底面半径为 \( r = 1 \) ,母线长为 \( l = 2 \) ,

\( \therefore \) 其侧面积为 \( S = {2\pi rl} = {2\pi } \times  1 \times  2 = {4\pi } \) .

\( {4\pi } \) .

4. 不等式 \( \frac{{2x} + 5}{x - 2} < 1 \) 的解集为___.

【答案】 \( \left( {-7,2}\right) \)

【分析】: 由已知进行转化 \( \frac{x + 7}{x - 2} < 0 \) ,进行可求.

\( \frac{{2x} + 5}{x - 2} < 1 \Rightarrow  \frac{{2x} + 5}{x - 2} - 1 < 0 \Rightarrow  \frac{x + 7}{x - 2} < 0, \)

【解析】得, \( - 7 < x < 2 \) .

【答案】 \( \left( {-7,2}\right) \) .

5. 直线 \( x =  - 2 \) 与直线 \( \sqrt{3}x - y + 1 = 0 \) 的夹角为___.

【答案】 \( \frac{\pi }{6} \)

【分析】: 先求出直线的斜率, 可得它们的倾斜角, 从而求出两条直线的夹角.

\( \because \) 直线 \( x =  - 2 \) 的斜率不存在,倾斜角为 \( \frac{\pi }{2} \) ,

直线 \( \sqrt{3}x - y + 1 = 0 \) 的斜率为 \( \sqrt{3} \) ,倾斜角为 \( \frac{\pi }{3} \) ,

故直线 \( x =  - 2 \) 与直线 \( \sqrt{3}x - y + 1 = 0 \) 的夹角为 \( \frac{\pi }{2} - \frac{\pi }{3} = \frac{\pi }{6} \) .

\( \frac{\pi }{6} \)

6. 若方程组 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {a}_{1}x + {b}_{1}y = {c}_{1} \\  {a}_{2}x + {b}_{2}y = {c}_{2} \end{array}\right. \) 无解,则 \( \left| \begin{array}{l} {a}_{1} \\  {a}_{2} \end{array}\right|  = \) ___.

## 【答案】 0

【分析】: 利用二元一次方程组的解的行列式表示进行分析即可得到答案.

对于方程组 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {a}_{1}x + {b}_{1}y = {c}_{1} \\  {a}_{2}x + {b}_{2}y = {c}_{2} \end{array}\right. \) ,有 \( D = \left| \begin{array}{l} {a}_{1} \\  {a}_{2} \end{array}\right| ,\;{D}_{x} = \left| \begin{array}{l} {c}_{1} \\  {c}_{2} \end{array}\right| ,\;{D}_{y} = \left| \begin{array}{l} {a}_{1} \\  {a}_{2} \end{array}\right| , \)

当 \( D \neq  0 \) 时,方程组的解为 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = \frac{{D}_{x}}{D} \\  y = \frac{{D}_{y}}{D} \end{array}\right. \)

根据题意,方程组 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {a}_{1}x + {b}_{1}y = {c}_{1} \\  {a}_{2}x + {b}_{2}y = {c}_{2} \end{array}\right. \) 无解,

所以 \( D = 0 \) ,即 \( D = \left| \begin{array}{l} {a}_{1} \\  {a}_{2} \end{array}\right|  = 0 \) .

0 .

7. 已知 \( {\left( 1 + x\right) }^{n} \) 的展开式，唯有 \( {x}^{3} \) 的系数最大，则 \( {\left( 1 + x\right) }^{n} \) 的系数和为___.

## 【答案】64

由已知可得 \( n = 6 \) ,令 \( x = 1 \) ,即可求得系数和.

由题意， \( {C}_{n}^{3} > {C}_{n}^{2} \) ，且 \( {C}_{n}^{3} > {C}_{n}^{4} \) ，

所以 \( n = 6 \) ,

所以令 \( x = 1,{\left( 1 + x\right) }^{6} \) 的系数和为 \( {2}^{6} = {64} \) .

64.

8. 已知函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = {3}^{x} + \frac{a}{{3}^{x} + 1}\left( {a0}\right) \) 的最小值为 5,则 \( a = \) ___.

【答案】 9

【分析】: 利用基本不等式求最值需要满足 “一正、二定、三相等”, 该题只需将函数解析式变形成 \( f\left( x\right)  = {3}^{x} + 1 + \frac{a}{{3}^{x} + 1} - 1 \) ,然后利用基本不等式求解即可,注意等号成立的条件.

\( f\left( x\right)  = {3}^{x} + \frac{a}{{3}^{x} + 1} = {3}^{x} + 1 + \frac{a}{{3}^{x} + 1} - 1 \geq  2\sqrt{a} - 1 = 5, \)

所以 \( a = 9 \) ,经检验, \( {3}^{x} = 2 \) 时等号成立.

9.

9. 在无穷等比数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 中， \( \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n\infty }}\left( {{a}_{1} - {a}_{n}}\right)  = 4 \) ，则 \( {a}_{2} \) 的取值范围是___.

【答案】 \( \left( {-4,0}\right)  \cup  \left( {0,4}\right) \)

【分析】: 由无穷等比数列的概念可得公比 \( q \) 的取值范围,再由极限的运算知 \( {a}_{1} = \) 4,从而得解.

\( \because \) 无穷等比数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}  ,\therefore \) 公比 \( q \in  \left( {-1,0}\right)  \cup  \left( {0,1}\right) \) ,

\( \therefore \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n\infty }}{a}_{n} = 0 \) ,

\( \therefore \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n\infty }}\left( {{a}_{1} - {a}_{n}}\right)  = {a}_{1} = 4 \) ,

\( \therefore {a}_{2} = {a}_{1}q = {4q} \in  \left( {-4,0}\right)  \cup  \left( {0,4}\right) \) .

\( \left( {-4,0}\right)  \cup  \left( {0,4}\right) \) .

10. 某人某天需要运动总时长大于等于 60 分钟，现有五项运动可以选择，如表所示，问有几种运动方式组合___.

<table><tr><td>\( A \) 运动</td><td>\( B \) 运动</td><td>\( C \) 运动</td><td>\( D \) 运动</td><td>\( E \) 运动</td></tr><tr><td>7 点 -8 点</td><td>8 点 -9 点</td><td>9 点 -10 点</td><td>10 点 -11 点</td><td>11 点 -12 点</td></tr><tr><td>30 分钟</td><td>20 分钟</td><td>40 分钟</td><td>30 分钟</td><td>30 分钟</td></tr></table>

【答案】 23 种

【分析】: 由题意知至少要选 2 种运动,并且选 2 种运动的情况中, \( {AB}\text{ 、 }{DB} \) 、

\( {EB} \) 的组合不符合题意,由此求出结果.

由题意知,至少要选 2 种运动,并且选 2 种运动的情况中, \( {AB}\text{ 、 }{DB}\text{ 、 }{EB} \) 的组合不符合题意;

所以满足条件的运动组合方式为: \( {C}_{5}^{2} + {C}_{5}^{3} + {C}_{5}^{4} + {C}_{5}^{5} - 3 = {10} + {10} + 5 + 1 - 3 = {23} \) (种).

23 种.

11. 已知椭圆 \( {x}^{2} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{{b}^{2}} = 1\left( {0 < b < 1}\right) \) 的左、右焦点为 \( {F}_{1} \) 、 \( {F}_{2} \) ,以 \( O \) 为顶点， \( {F}_{2} \) 为焦点作抛物线交椭圆于 \( P \) ,且 \( \angle P{F}_{1}{F}_{2} = {45}^{ \circ  } \) ,则抛物线的准线方程是___.

【答案】 \( x = 1 - \sqrt{2} \)

【分析】: 先设出椭圆的左右焦点坐标,进而可得抛物线的方程,设出直线 \( P{F}_{1} \) 的方程并与抛物线联立,求出点 \( P \) 的坐标,由此可得 \( P{F}_{2} \bot  {F}_{1}{F}_{2} \) ,进而可以求出 \( P{F}_{1} \) , \( P{F}_{2} \) 的长度,再由椭圆的定义即可求解.

设 \( {F}_{1}\left( {-c,0}\right) ,{F}_{2}\left( {c,0}\right) \) ,则抛物线 \( {y}^{2} = {4cx} \) ,

直线 \( P{F}_{1} : \;y = x + c \) ,联立方程组 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} {y}^{2} = {4cx} \\  y = x + c \end{array}\right. \) ,解得 \( x = c, y = {2c} \) ,

所以点 \( P \) 的坐标为 \( \left( {c,{2c}}\right) \) ,所以 \( P{F}_{2} \bot  {F}_{1}{F}_{2} \) ,又 \( P{F}_{2} = {F}_{2}{F}_{1} = {2c} \) ,所以 \( P{F}_{1} = 2\sqrt{2}c \) 所以 \( P{F}_{1} = 2\sqrt{2}c \) ,所以 \( P{F}_{1} + P{F}_{2} = \left( {2 + 2\sqrt{2}}\right) c = {2a} = 2 \) ,

则 \( c = \sqrt{2} - 1 \) ,

所以抛物线的准线方程为: \( x =  - c = 1 - \sqrt{2} \) .

\( x = 1 - \sqrt{2} \) .

12. 已知 \( \theta  > 0 \) ,存在实数 \( \varphi \) ,使得对任意 \( n \in  {N}^{ * },\cos \left( {{n\theta } + \varphi }\right)  < \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \) ,则 \( \theta \) 的最小值是 ___. 【答案】 \( \frac{2\pi }{5} \)

【分析】: 在单位圆中分析可得 \( \theta  > \frac{\pi }{3} \) ,由 \( \frac{2\pi }{\theta } \in  {N}^{ * } \) ,即 \( \theta  = \frac{2\pi }{k}, k \in  {N}^{![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_336_405_1362_636_532_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_336_405_1362_636_532_0.jpg)9b5b00_336_405_1362_636_532_0.jpg)

在单位圆中分析,由题意可得 \( {n\theta } + \varphi \) 的终边要落在图中阴影部分区域 (其中 \( \angle {AOx} \; = \angle {BOx} = \frac{\pi }{6} \) ),

所以 \( \theta  > \angle {AOB} = \frac{\pi }{3} \) ,

因为对任意 \( n \in  {N}^{ * } \) 都成立,

所以 \( \frac{2\pi }{\theta } \in  {N}^{ * } \) ,即 \( \theta  = \frac{2\pi }{k}, k \in  {N}^{ * } \) ,

同时 \( \theta  > \frac{\pi }{3} \) ,所以 \( \theta \) 的最小值为 \( \frac{2\pi }{5} \) .

\( \frac{2\pi }{5}. \)

## 二、选择题 (本大题共 4 题, 每题 5 分, 共 20 分)

13. 下列函数中, 在定义域内存在反函数的是 ( )

A. \( f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{2} \) B. \( f\left( x\right)  = \sin x \) C. \( f\left( x\right)  = {2x} \) D. \( f\left( x\right)  = 1 \)

## 【答案】 \( C \)

【分析】: 根据函数的定义以及映射的定义即可判断选项是否正确.

A. 因为函数是二次函数，属于二对一的映射，

根据函数的定义可得函数不存在反函数, \( A \) 错误;

B. 因为函数是三角函数,有周期性和对称性,属于多对一的映射,

根据函数的定义可得函数不存在反函数, \( B \) 错误;

\( C \) . 因为函数的单调递增的指数函数,属于一一映射,所以函数存在反函数, \( C \) 正确;

\( D \) . 因为函数是常数函数,属于多对一的映射,所以函数不存在反函数, \( D \) 错误. 故选 \( C \)

14. 已知集合 \( A = \{ x \mid  x - 1, x \in  R\} , B = \left\{  {x \mid  {x}^{2} - x - 2 \geq  0, x \in  R}\right\} \) ，则下列关系中，正确的是 ( )

A. \( A \subseteq  B \) B. \( {\int }_{R}A \subseteq  {\int }_{R}B \) C. \( A \cap  B = \varphi \) D. \( A \cup  B = R \)

【答案】 \( D \)

【分析】: 根据集合的基本运算对每一选项判断即可.

已知集合 \( A = \{ x \mid  x - 1, x \in  R\} ,\;B = \left\{  {x \mid  {x}^{2} - x - 2 \geq  0, x \in  R}\right\} \) ,

【解析】得 \( B = \{ x \mid  x \geq  2 \) 或 \( x \leq   - 1, x \in  R\} \) ,

\( {\complement }_{R}A = \{ x \mid  x \leq   - 1, x \in  R\} ,\;{\complement }_{R}B = \{ x \mid   - 1 < x < 2\} ; \)

则 \( A \cup  B = R, A \cap  B = \{ x \mid  x \geq  2\} \) .

故选 \( D \)

15. 已知函数 \( y = f\left( x\right) \) 的定义域为 \( R \) ,下列是 \( f\left( x\right) \) 无最大值的充分条件是 ( )

A. \( f\left( x\right) \) 为偶函数且关于点 \( \left( {1,1}\right) \) 对称 B. \( f\left( x\right) \) 为偶函数且关于直线 \( x = 1 \) 对称

C. \( f\left( x\right) \) 为奇函数且关于点 \( \left( {1,1}\right) \) 对称 D. \( f\left( x\right) \) 为奇函数且关于直线 \( x = 1 \) 对称

## 【答案】 \( C \)

【分析】: 根据题意,依次判断选项: 对于 \( {ABD} \) ,举出反例可得三个选项错误,对于 \( C \) ,利用反证法可得其正确.

根据题意, 依次判断选项:

A. \( f\left( x\right)  = \cos \frac{\pi x}{2} + 1, f\left( x\right) \) 为偶函数,且关于点 \( \left( {1,1}\right) \) 对称,存在最大值, \( A \) 错误;

B. \( f\left( x\right)  = \cos \left( {\pi x}\right) , f\left( x\right) \) 为偶函数且关于直线 \( x = 1 \) 对称,存在最大值, \( B \) 错误;

\( C \) . 假设 \( f\left( x\right) \) 有最大值,设其最大值为 \( M \) ,其最高点的坐标为 \( \left( {a, M}\right) \) ,

\( f\left( x\right) \) 为奇函数,其图象关于原点对称,则 \( f\left( x\right) \) 的图象存在最低点 \( \left( {-a, - M}\right) \) ,

又由 \( f\left( x\right) \) 的图象关于点 \( \left( {1,1}\right) \) 对称,则 \( \left( {-a, - M}\right) \) 关于点 \( \left( {1,1}\right) \) 对称的点为 \( \left( {2 + a,2 + M}\right) \) ,

与最大值为 \( M \) 相矛盾,则此时 \( f\left( x\right) \) 无最大值, \( C \) 正确;

D. \( f\left( x\right)  = \sin \frac{\pi x}{2}, f\left( x\right) \) 为奇函数且关于直线 \( x = 1 \) 对称, \( D \) 错误,

故选 \( C \)

16. 在 \( {ABC} \) 中， \( D \) 为 \( {BC} \) 中点， \( E \) 为 \( {AD} \) 中点，则以下结论:①存在 \( {ABC} \) ，使得 \( \overrightarrow{AB} \cdot  \overrightarrow{CE} = \) 0;②存在三角形 \( {ABC} \) ,使得 \( \overrightarrow{CE}//\left( {\overrightarrow{CB} + \overrightarrow{CA}}\right) \) ; 他们的成立情况是 ( )

A. ①成立，②成立 B. ①成立，②不成立

C. ①不成立，②成立 D. ①不成立，②不成立

## 【答案】 \( B \)

【分析】: 设 \( A\left( {{2x},{2y}}\right) , B\left( {-1,0}\right) , C\left( {1,0}\right) , D\left( {0,0}\right) , E\left( {x, y}\right) \) ,由向量数量的坐

标运算即可判断①； \( F \) 为 \( {AB} \) 中点，可得 \( \left( {\overrightarrow{CB} + \overrightarrow{CA}}\right)  = 2\overrightarrow{CF} \) ，由 \( D \) 为 \( {BC} \) 中点，可得 \( {CF} \) 与 \( ![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_339_408_324_505_395_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_339_408_324_505_395_0.jpg)39b5b00_339_408_324_505_395_0.jpg)

不妨设 \( A\left( {{2x},{2y}}\right) , B\left( {-1,0}\right) , C\left( {1,0}\right) , D\left( {0,0}\right) , E\left( {x, y}\right) \) ,

① \( \overrightarrow{AB} = \left( {-1 - {2x}, - {2y}}\right) ,\overrightarrow{CE} = \left( {x - 1, y}\right) \) ，

若 \( \overrightarrow{AB} \cdot  \overrightarrow{CE} = 0 \) ,则 \( - \left( {1 + {2x}}\right) \left( {x - 1}\right)  - 2{y}^{2} = 0 \) ,即 \( - \left( {1 + {2x}}\right) \left( {x - 1}\right)  = 2{y}^{2} \) ,

满足条件的 \( \left( {x, y}\right) \) 存在,例如 \( \left( {0,\frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}}\right) \) ,满足上式,所以①成立;

② \( F \) 为 \( {AB} \) 中点， \( \left( {\overrightarrow{CB} + \overrightarrow{CA}}\right)  = 2\overrightarrow{CF} \) ， \( {CF} \) 与 \( {AD} \) 的交点即为重心 \( G \) ，

因为 \( G \) 为 \( {AD} \) 的三等分点， \( E \) 为 \( {AD} \) 中点，

所以 \( \overrightarrow{CE} \) 与 \( \overrightarrow{CG} \) 不共线,即②不成立.

故选 \( B \)

三、解答题 (本大题共 5 题, 共 \( {14} + {14} + {14} + {16} + {18} = {76} \) 分)

17. 四棱锥 \( P - {ABCD} \) ,底面为正方形 \( {ABCD} \) ,边长为 \( 4, E \) 为 \( {AB} \) 中点， \![bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_339_281_1533_387_319_0.jpg](bo_d6dclef7aajc739b5b00_339_281_1533_387_319_0.jpg)9b5b00_339_281_1533_387_319_0.jpg)

(1)若 \( {PAB} \) 为等边三角形，求四棱锥 \( P - {ABCD} \) 的体积；

【答案】 \( \frac{{32}\sqrt{3}}{3} \)

【分析】: 由 \( V = {13PE} \cdot  {S}_{\text{ 正方形 }{ABCD}} \) ,代入相应数据,进行运算,即可.

\( \because {PAB} \) 为等边三角形,且 \( E \) 为 \( {AB} \) 中点, \( {AB} = 4 \) ,

\( \therefore {PE} = 2\sqrt{3} \) ，

又 \( {PE} \bot \) 平面 \( {ABCD} \) ,
